## Round 22 — 2026-07-11 — manual

**Item in flight:** managed-llm-credits (AlgoBooth `/lazy-batch`, Step 10 `__mark_complete__` completion-coherence gate)

**Divergence point:** the `__mark_complete__` completion-coherence gate refused on 7 unchecked boxes across 5 phases with a bare "N unchecked box(es)" message that could not distinguish an un-migrated verification-shim row (marker-migration candidate) from a genuine incomplete deliverable — AND two of the blocking rows were genuinely un-runnable on THIS host (no Supabase config / no credits-proxy backend), which the pipeline has no per-row way to defer.

**Root cause:**
  - **`script-defect` (diagnostic, FIXED):** the refusal at `apply_pseudo` (`lazy_core.py` completion-coherence gate) reported only a per-phase unchecked COUNT. It did not classify the still-unchecked (post-autotick) rows, so the orchestrator/operator could not tell that 5 of 7 blocking rows were merely un-migrated verification rows (exempt by the legacy `_VERIFICATION_SECTION_RE` shim in `remaining_unchecked_are_verification_only:2372` but not by the canonical-marker-only `autotick_verification_rows:3342`) vs 2 genuine gaps.
  - **`missing-contract` (design fork, SURFACED):** the completion gate's strictness is DELIBERATE (`_phase_completion_plan` docstring, `lazy_core.py:2740`: "verification rows INCLUDED — by completion time the verification exemption's job is done"). So aligning the two recognizers is NOT a safe mechanical fix — tolerating legacy-shim rows would weaken an intentional gate (prohibition #2), and migrating/ticking a host-blocked row is a FALSE-GREEN. There is ALSO no PER-ROW host-capability deferral (only feature-level DEFERRED_REQUIRES_HOST, which blocks the whole feature) and NO dispatch path to author NEW coverage discovered at Step 10 (coherence-recovery correctly refuses implementation; a hand-composed mcp-test prompt is guard-denied; the state machine won't re-route Step 10→mcp-test with VALIDATED.md present).

**Action:**
  - Mechanical fix applied: added `classify_blocking_unchecked_rows` (mirrors `remaining_unchecked_are_verification_only`'s scope tracking) and appended an ACTIONABLE advisory to the completion-refusal — splits blocking unchecked rows into un-migrated verification-shim (clear via canonical-marker migration IF verification actually ran) vs genuine incomplete deliverables, with shim-row excerpts. Diagnostic ONLY — the gate decision is unchanged, no gate weakened. Commit: `62fdba2`.
  - NEEDS_INPUT.md updated: `docs/specs/turn-routing-enforcement/NEEDS_INPUT.md` decisions #5 (completion-gate treatment of un-migrated + host-blocked verification rows — per-row host-capability deferral vs recognizer convergence vs per-row disposition) and #6 (corrective-coverage dispatch: new `--emit-dispatch corrective-coverage` class vs Step-10→mcp-test re-route). Both cross-reference the already-open decision #2 (partial-VALIDATED completion). Design/gate-semantics forks — surfaced, not baked.

**Over-fit spin-off:** none — the mechanical fix is a NEW diagnostic classifier (structural, not a phrase added to a matcher; signal 1 N/A) and this classifier class has not recurred (first occurrence; signals 2–4 ≥2 threshold unmet). The DESIGN halves are surfaced via NEEDS_INPUT, not a spin-off.

**Intervention record:** `harden-2026-07-r22` (`target_signal: undeclared` — the actionable-refusal is a triage-quality diagnostic; it does not directly change a measurable ledger event rate, so it degrades honestly to INCONCLUSIVE-by-construction rather than declaring a spurious signal).

**Gates run:**
  test_lazy_core.py: 948/948 (0 failed; +1: classify_blocking_unchecked_rows shim-vs-genuine; orphan + dead-coverage guards pass)
  test_hooks.py: 150/150 (0 skipped, 0 failed)
  lint-skills.py: OK — 1 pre-existing planner-resolution finding (`write-plan-cognito`, same as Rounds 17/19/20/21; unrelated)
  lazy-state.py --test: OK
  bug-state.py --test: OK

## Round 23 — 2026-07-11 — manual

**Item in flight:** claude-config self-hardening — manual `/harden-harness` (trigger 5) implementing the concluded bug spec `docs/bugs/no-mid-run-observed-friction-harden-dispatch/`. Origin friction observed during the AlgoBooth `/lazy-batch` managed-llm-credits run (2026-07-11), where the orchestrator named four harness gaps mid-run through its own reasoning but had no sanctioned way to dispatch `/harden-harness` for them.

**Divergence point:** the lazy-* orchestrator's mid-run self-hardening path — the four automatic harden triggers (validate-deny / no-route / inject-hook-error / process-friction) all arrive via `--emit-dispatch hardening` from a ledger/probe signal, but there was NO dispatch class for harness friction the orchestrator OBSERVES through reasoning. A hand-composed `Agent` dispatch to run `/harden-harness` mid-run is DENIED by the validate-deny guard (unregistered prompt), so observed friction was stranded (surface-and-defer, or an out-of-band fix after the run).

**Root cause:** `missing-contract` — the harden dispatch mechanism (`--emit-dispatch hardening`, `lazy_core.build_hardening_emit_command`) was bound only to the four automatic triggers, each carrying denial/friction-specific `--context` keys. There was (1) no `observed-friction` trigger_kind / emit path, so a reasoning-observed gap's prompt could not be registered → the guard denied it mid-run; (2) no orchestrator contract requiring a harden dispatch on observed friction (the `auto-invoke` CLAUDE.md rule covered the general case, but the coupled-trio SKILLs did not encode the mid-run REQUIREMENT or the mechanics); (3) no block/background policy distinguishing a run-blocking gap (must foreground/await) from a latent one (background). Distinct from the Rounds 9-13 `missing-contract` class (dispatch-guard has no contract for worker-composed sub-subagent prompts, `lazy_guard.py:839`) — different symbol (`lazy_core.build_hardening_emit_command:16556` + the `--emit-dispatch hardening` handlers), different mechanism (an orchestrator-supplied observed-friction emit path, not a guard exemption).

**Action:**
  - Mechanical fix applied: (1) `build_hardening_emit_command` gains an `observed_friction` branch (orchestrator-supplied `friction_summary`/`friction_detail`/`blocking`, NOT a deny-ledger entry); (2) new `normalize_hardening_dispatch_context` rebinds `friction_summary` into `denied_prompt_summary` / `friction_detail` into `denial_reason` (the same rebind the process-friction branch performs), injects observed-friction `probe_json`/`registry_state` placeholders, and defaults a new `{blocking}` token — wired into the `--emit-dispatch hardening` handler in both `lazy-state.py` and `bug-state.py`; (3) `dispatch-hardening.md` @requires gains `blocking`, adds `observed-friction` to the valid trigger set, and a new efficacy-loop section prompting Step-2.5 spec-bug-first + a MEASURABLE `target_signal`-first declaration (spec 1 section 6); (4) the REQUIRED coupled-trio SKILL contract (`lazy-batch`/`lazy-bug-batch`/`lazy-batch-cloud` section 1d.1 Trigger 5) with the section-3 block/background policy + section-4 `self_edit_mode` force-await exception. Commit: `c46ed80`.

**Over-fit spin-off:** none — the fix is STRUCTURAL (a new trigger_kind branch + a reusable normalizer function + a REQUIRED SKILL contract), not a literal phrase added to a matcher (signal 1 N/A). The `missing-contract` class HAS recurred in this log (Rounds 9-13), but on a DIFFERENT symbol/mechanism (`lazy_guard.py:839` `_deny_default` sub-subagent exemption) — the >=2 recurrence threshold keys on same-class-AND-same-component, and this is the first occurrence on the harden-dispatch emit path. Signals 3/4 unmet (a general mechanism, not a near-neighbor-gapping patch; no repeated deterministic dance). Healthy structural fix → no spin-off.

**Intervention record:** `harden-2026-07-r23` (`target_signal: undeclared`). This round ADDS the observed-friction emit-path + contract INFRASTRUCTURE; it does not itself target a countable telemetry event to drive down — the baseline for mid-run observed-friction dispatches is zero (the orchestrator historically surfaced-and-deferred rather than hand-composing a guard-denied harden), and the loop's MEASURABLE signal lives in each DOWNSTREAM observed-friction harden's own intervention (section 6: "declare the friction's own recurrence event"). Honestly degrades to INCONCLUSIVE-by-construction rather than declaring a spurious rate.

Section 1c.6 in all three trio SKILLs now states the GATE, not just the obligation. Not a gate-weakening: the override is operator-authorization-only and retro-graded. Commit: `7d49490`.

## Round 25 — 2026-07-11 — manual

**Item in flight:** claude-config self-hardening — manual `/harden-harness` (trigger 5) implementing the concluded bug spec `docs/bugs/planner-resolution-lint-blind-to-internal-repos/`. Finally root-causes the standing `write-plan-cognito` planner-resolution finding that Rounds 17/19/20/21/22/23/24 all carried as "pre-existing, unrelated" — it is neither pre-existing-acceptable nor unrelated: it is a real script-defect making the mandatory skill-plane gate RED on clean `main` on this machine.

**Divergence point:** the canonical skill-plane gate `lint-skills.py --check-projected --check-capabilities` (`.claude/skill-config/quality-gates.md:11`) → `lint_planner_resolution` (`user/scripts/lint-skills.py:213`) reports `Cognito planner not found: no write-plan-cognito skill resolves under any repos/*/.claude/skills/ (D1 rename must be present)` and exits 1 — even though `write-plan-cognito` is git-tracked at `repos/cognito-forms/.claude/skills/write-plan-cognito/`.

**Root cause:** `script-defect` — the check anchored D1 resolution to `args.repos_dir` (default `~/source/repos`, `user/scripts/lint-skills.py:369-373`), a **machine-variable** location. Repo-scoped skills are git-tracked *inside* claude-config at `<claude-config>/repos/<name>/.claude/skills/`; on dev machines / WSL `~/source/repos/<name>/.claude/skills` is a symlink INTO that internal tree, which is the ONLY reason the `~/source/repos` default ever resolved. On this laptop (`DESKTOP-GHTC5K6`, user `Jacob`) only `claude-config` is checked out under `~/source/repos`, so `repo_skill_roots` was empty → false "not found". Proven: default → EXIT 1; `--repos-dir "$(pwd)/repos"` → EXIT 0 (`write-plan-cognito resolves; no execute-plan-cognito fork`); `ls ~/source/repos` → only `claude-config/`. D1 decision cited: `docs/features/plan-skills-redesign/SPEC.md:66-76` (rename the colliding Cognito planner to `/write-plan-cognito`, repo-scoped; no `execute-plan-cognito` fork).

**Action:**
  - Mechanical fix applied: `lint_planner_resolution` now builds repo skill roots from the UNION of the passed `repos_dir` AND the claude-config-internal `<claude-config>/repos/` derived from the script's own location (`Path(__file__).resolve().parents[2] / "repos"`), deduplicated by resolved path. The internal tree is the always-present, git-tracked source of truth, so D1 resolution is now machine-independent. Strictly stronger: the negative `execute-plan-cognito` invariant now also scans the internal repos. No gate weakened, no threshold softened — the fix corrects WHERE the invariant looks, not WHAT it requires. Regression: 2 tests in `test_lazy_core.py` load `lint-skills.py` via importlib and assert no `planner-resolution` finding when the passed `repos_dir` is empty (the exact bug scenario). Commit: `8ffd1d0` (bug spec: `01079ec`).

**Over-fit spin-off:** none — the fix is STRUCTURAL (union-scan resolved from the script's own location), not a literal phrase added to a matcher (signal 1 N/A). The class was OBSERVED across Rounds 17/19–24 but never root-caused/fixed until now, so this is the FIRST fix of the class (signals 2–4 `≥2`-fixes threshold unmet). Healthy structural fix → no spin-off. (Noted out-of-scope near-neighbor: `project-skills.py` shares the `~/source/repos` default and under-projects on this machine, but exits 0 — silent, not a RED gate — so not fixed here to avoid gold-plating; a follow-up if it surfaces as friction.)

**Intervention record:** `harden-2026-07-r25` (`target_signal: undeclared`). This round fixes a false-RED in a *quality gate* whose result is not emitted as a run-marker deny-ledger telemetry event (unlike `containment-refusal` / `gate-refusal`), so there is no countable ledger signal this fix drives down. Declaring a spurious signal would be dishonest → the three hypothesis flags are omitted and the record degrades honestly to INCONCLUSIVE-by-construction.

**Gates run:**
  test_lazy_core.py: 961/961 (0 failed; +2 planner-resolution regression; orphan + dead-coverage guards pass)
  test_hooks.py: 150/150 (0 skipped, 0 failed)
  lint-skills.py: OK — planner resolution now GREEN (`write-plan-cognito resolves; no execute-plan-cognito fork`); the standing finding is CLEARED
  lazy-state.py --test: OK
  bug-state.py --test: OK

This IS the class's second fix (over-fit signal 2, ≥2 threshold MET: Round 25 = first, Round 26 = second). Rather than copy-paste `8ffd1d0`'s union into a third site later, the fix EXTRACTS the shared `skill_repos.iter_config_repos` / `resolve_internal_repos_root` primitive and routes BOTH `lint-skills.py` and `project-skills.py` through it, retiring the duplicated logic. The single-event path branches out BYTE-IDENTICAL (existing rows + exact finding messages unchanged); the `NOT registered` path is untouched. Retired the `doc-drift:deliberate-divergence` marker on the `lazy-route-inject.sh` row and documented all three events in its Trigger cell (`PostCompact (*); SessionStart (compact); UserPromptSubmit (*)`) — now validates cleanly. Module docstring's `hooks`-check description updated. Regression: `test_doc_drift_lint.py` +4 hermetic multi-event fixtures (clean / documented-event-not-registered / registered-event-not-documented / per-event matcher-mismatch). Commit: `1b23a9b` (bug spec: `0f44611`).

## Round 28 — 2026-07-12 — observed-friction

**Item in flight:** `live-settings-split-brain-disarms-enforcement-plane` (self-edit run on claude-config). Three harness gaps OBSERVED mid-run during a `/lazy-bug-batch` cycle (auto-invoke observed-friction dispatch, batched into one round).

**Divergence point:** three independent points — (1) `lazy-cycle-containment.sh::main` routed every non-Bash/non-Skill tool call (incl. `Agent`/`Task`) straight to `_allow()`, so a cycle subagent's `run_in_background:true` sub-dispatch was never inspected; (2) `lazy_core.format_cycle_header` (the `--probe --forward-cycles` enrichment on both scripts) emitted the retired `### Cycle fwd N/M · …` heading, echoed verbatim by the T2 probe-presence guard; (3) `bug-state.py::_find_open_bug_dirs` re-emitted a Fixed-without-receipt `_diag` on every probe for 7 fixed-outside-pipeline dirs.

**Root cause:**
  - GAP 1 (PRIMARY) — **hook-defect.** The synchronous-await contract for cycle subagents was prose-only; the containment hook drew no distinction between a synchronous Agent/Task dispatch (safe; allowed since 2026-07-09 for Explore fan-outs) and a background one. A backgrounded child reaches only the main thread, so a subagent-parent that awaits a child→parent `SendMessage` deadlocks. Observed twice (cycles 6+7), each costing a `TaskStop` + re-dispatch (`user/hooks/lazy-cycle-containment.sh` main() fall-through).
  - GAP 2 — **script-defect.** `format_cycle_header` (WU-5, ~`lazy_core.py:6680`) was never migrated when the T2 heading contract retired the `Cycle fwd`/`· feat · sub_skill` shape (`lazy-batch/SKILL.md:1272`, `lazy-bug-batch/SKILL.md:959` — "must NOT reappear"). Verbatim echo landed the forbidden format on every forward cycle; the META path (`emit_dispatch_prompt:7517`) already used the sanctioned shape.
  - GAP 3 — **not a code defect** (the diagnostic is working-as-designed honest completion-integrity debt). 7 dirs marked `Status: Fixed` inline "no receipt by design" left the signal permanently ON. Suppression rejected (gate-weakening-adjacent); the sanctioned `--backfill-receipts` grandfather path pays the debt honestly.

**Action:**
  - GAP 1 — **Mechanical fix applied.** `lazy-cycle-containment.sh` now denies a background (`run_in_background` truthy) `Agent`/`Task` dispatch from a subagent (`agent_id` present) with a corrective directing synchronous/foreground dispatch (signature `background-dispatch`); foreground subagent dispatch + main-thread background dispatch stay allowed. New `_is_truthy_background` helper. +3 `test_hooks.py` pipe-tests. Commit: `a43808e`.
  - GAP 2 — **Mechanical fix applied.** Reshaped `format_cycle_header` to `### {Step} — {summary} [{fwd}/{max}]` (Step via a new `SUB_SKILL_STEP_NAMES` map mirroring `DISPATCH_STEP_NAMES`; summary = feature_id; `Cycle` fallback for absent sub_skill). Shared helper → both pipelines inherit, no coupled-pair mirror owed. Byte-pinned smoke baselines contain no `Cycle fwd` (no regen). Updated 2 characterization tests. Commit: `3404c9e`.
  - GAP 3 — **Data remediation** (no code change). `bug-state.py --backfill-receipts` wrote `provenance: backfilled-unverified` FIXED.md for the 7 dirs; the Fixed-without-receipt diagnostic count now = 0. Commit: `4edd224`. Bug specs (all three, Status: Concluded) committed FIRST at `01ae5e4` (Step 2.5 audit trail predates the fixes).

**Over-fit spin-off:** none. GAP 1/GAP 2 change STRUCTURE (a new deny branch keyed on the background flag; a reshaped header producer), not a literal phrase added to a matcher (over-fit signal 1 does not trip). Neither root-cause class (containment background-dispatch; cycle_header format) has recurred in the log (signal 2 needs ≥2). Healthy structural fixes — no queued spin-off.

**Intervention record:** `harden-2026-07-r28` — declared `target_signal: event:containment-refusal`, expected-direction **decrease**, signal-independence **self-emitted** (the refusal event is produced by the new `background-dispatch` deny site this fix adds; a decrease means cycle subagents stopped attempting background sub-dispatch after the corrective). GAP 2 (pure format) and GAP 3 (data remediation) carry no countable ledger signal and are covered narratively. **Capture deferred (non-blocking):** the deterministic `--record-intervention` write is an orchestrator-only op and was correctly REFUSED here (exit-0 refusal, zero side effects) because this harden ran as a dispatched cycle subagent with the live cycle marker present — spoofing `LAZY_ORCHESTRATOR=1` to bypass the guard is the integrity side-door the harness forbids, so it was NOT attempted. The orchestrator (or a later main-thread invocation) should capture the record with the declared fields:
```
python3 user/scripts/lazy-state.py --record-intervention \
  --id harden-2026-07-r28 --pipeline hardening \
  --target-signal event:containment-refusal --expected-direction decrease \
  --signal-independence "self-emitted — background-dispatch deny site; decrease = subagents stopped background sub-dispatch" \
  --repo-root .
```

**Gates run:**
  test_hooks.py: 153/153 (0 failed; +3 containment background-dispatch pipe-tests)
  test_lazy_core.py: 0 failed; all printed tests PASS incl. both reshaped `format_cycle_header` tests. ## Round 29 — 2026-07-12 — observed-friction

**Item in flight:** `live-settings-split-brain-disarms-enforcement-plane` (self-edit run on claude-config; the friction was OBSERVED by the orchestrator mid-run on the part-3 checkpoint resume). Non-blocking observed-friction harden dispatched off the live `/lazy-bug-batch` run.

**Divergence point:** the checkpoint-resume `--run-start` → first forward re-probe of `next_route = /execute-plan part-3` (`complexity: complex`; parts 1 & 2 Complete; clean+pushed tree). The probe returned `repeat_count=2` + `LOOP DETECTED` + `cycle_model=sonnet`; the orchestrator hand-overrode the model to opus (a T6 deviation) and the cycle then completed cleanly. Two independent, compounding harness gaps.

**Root cause:** **script-defect** (two coupled sites in `lazy_core.py`).
  - GAP 1 (false LOOP DETECTED) — the F1/F2 double-probe debounce (`update_repeat_counts`, `lazy_core.py:~5903,~6034`) HOLDS a repeat count only when it can prove NO dispatch landed between two identical probes: `prior consume_count == consumed_emission_count()`. That `consume_count` lives in the OS-temp signature file (`lazy-state-last-<hash>.json`), which SURVIVES `--run-end`, but a checkpoint `--run-end` deletes the prompt registry and the resuming `--run-start` recreates it fresh (`consumed_emission_count() → 0`). The stale, registry-relative baseline made the first re-probe of the deterministically-re-probed `next_route` mis-read a REGISTRY RESET as a landed dispatch → `repeat_count` 1 → 2 on a route that was never re-dispatched. A probe→checkpoint→probe is NOT a stall (a genuine stall needs a DISPATCH that failed to advance between two probes). Same *class* as `cycle-bracket-break-on-checkpoint-resume` (Round 35 — checkpoint `--run-start` re-mints run-scoped state that must be continuous), but for a NON-marker OS-temp artifact outside the `RUN_CONTINUITY_FIELDS` partition, which is why the field-complete-continuity completeness test could not catch it.
  - GAP 2 (complex part flipped to sonnet) — `emit_cycle_prompt` (`lazy_core.py:~7216`) set `model = "sonnet"` UNCONDITIONALLY when the loop block was appended, ignoring the `/execute-plan` part's declared complexity. The cycle prompt HARD-refuses complex work under a sonnet dispatch (`cycle-base-prompt.md:260,287`, `blocker_kind: model-tier-mismatch`), so the flip could not advance a `complexity: complex` part — it only climbed the stall streak toward a halt. The pre-existing comment (`lazy_core.py:7172`) documented the buggy composition (`sonnet ∧ sonnet = sonnet`) as intended.

**Action:**
  - Mechanical fix applied — STRUCTURAL (both gaps). GAP 1: new shared helper `lazy_core.rebaseline_loop_signature_after_registry_reset(repo_root, *, pipeline)` re-baselines ONLY the signature file's `consume_count` to the fresh registry count (preserving `count`/`step_count` so a GENUINE pre-pause streak survives — the loop block still fires); no-op + fail-open when no signature file / no marker. Wired into the checkpoint-resume block (`if checkpoint is not None:`) of BOTH state scripts' run-start handlers (shared helper; coupled-pair call sites; parity audit green). GAP 2: a declared-complexity FLOOR on the loop-flip — for `/execute-plan`, `plan_complexity(part) == "mechanical"` → sonnet (unchanged), else (`complex` or the untagged/unknown SAFE default) → `complexity_pinned_opus`; the loop block downgrades to sonnet ONLY when NOT pinned (loop block still appended either way). The floor matches the subagent's `model-tier-mismatch` refusal condition exactly. Tests: +2 rebaseline (prevent-false-loop; no-op-when-absent/no-marker), +3 loop-flip floor (complex stays opus / untagged stays opus / mechanical stays sonnet); retargeted 2 tests that pinned the OLD buggy behavior (`..._loop_append_and_model_flip` → `/retro`; `..._complex_part_loop_cycle_model_sonnet` → renamed `..._complex_part_loop_stays_opus`, asserts opus) + the addenda-ordering test's model assertion (opus) + the stale comment/test-header. Bug spec (Status: Concluded) committed FIRST at `6c03084` (Step 2.5 audit trail predates the fix). Commit: `719c98a`.

**Over-fit spin-off:** none. Both fixes change STRUCTURE (a new re-baseline helper; a declared-complexity floor gate keyed on `plan_complexity`), NOT a literal phrase added to a matcher — over-fit signal 1 does not trip. Signal 2 (non-phrase recurrence ≥2) is not met: the specific components (the loop-debounce signature file across a checkpoint; the loop-flip complexity floor) have not recurred. NOTED for future signal-2 tracking: GAP 1 is the FIRST occurrence of a *non-marker* run-scoped artifact being stranded across a checkpoint (prior checkpoint-continuity rounds — `cycle-bracket-break-on-checkpoint-resume`, `adhoc-checkpoint-resume-field-complete-continuity` — all fixed run-MARKER fields, guarded by the `RUN_CONTINUITY_FIELDS` completeness test which does not span OS-temp artifacts). A THIRD stranded-non-marker-state-across-checkpoint bug would be the spin-off trigger for a "checkpoint continuity spans non-marker run-scoped artifacts" generalization. Boundary deliberately tight now (Out-of-Scope: the fresh non-checkpoint `--run-start` stale-signature near-neighbor).

**Intervention record:** `harden-2026-07-r29` — declared `target_signal: undeclared` (honest degradation, per Rounds 25–27). The observed friction has no clean INDEPENDENT countable ledger event: GAP 1's false LOOP DETECTED is a probe-COMPUTED field (never emitted as a deny-ledger/telemetry `event:`), and GAP 2's `model-tier-mismatch` surfaces either as a broad `blocked` terminal (confounded by every unrelated block — poor signal independence) or, as observed live, as an orchestrator hand-override T6 deviation (a retro finding, not a ledger event). The three hypothesis flags are omitted; the record degrades to INCONCLUSIVE-by-construction rather than declaring a spurious rate. **Capture deferred (non-blocking):** `--record-intervention` is an orchestrator-only op and is REFUSED for this dispatched cycle subagent (live cycle marker present; the containment C3 guard) — spoofing `LAZY_ORCHESTRATOR=1` to bypass it is the integrity side-door the harness forbids, so it was NOT attempted (same posture as Round 28). (no `--target-signal`/`--expected-direction`/`--signal-independence` — the record degrades honestly to `target_signal: undeclared`.)

## Round 30 — 2026-07-12 — observed-friction

**Item in flight:** `live-settings-split-brain-disarms-enforcement-plane` (self-edit run on claude-config; the friction was OBSERVED by the orchestrator mid-run, blocking=true — the orchestrator awaited this foreground harden before re-probing). Dispatched off the live `/lazy-bug-batch` run.

All 5 PHASES phases `Status: Complete`, all 3 plan parts `status: Complete`, SPEC `Status: Concluded` (correct pre-`__mark_fixed__`); `find_implementation_plans` filtered the Complete parts out (`plans == []`). The SOLE remaining unchecked box is `PHASES.md:128`, a deliberately-dropped deliverable authored as a struck-through descope note: `- [ ] ~~`setup.py` gains the parallel live hook/symlink check~~ **DROPPED** (decision 2, NEEDS_INPUT.md resolution, 2026-07-12)`. The bypass helper returned `False`, so the `elif not plans` branch dispatched `write-plan` on a fully-implemented bug — a no-progress loop whose `repeat_count`/`step_repeat` climb toward a false LOOP DETECTED / max-cycles halt.

**Root cause:** **script-defect** — `lazy_core.py::remaining_unchecked_are_verification_only` (def ~:2237; row branch ~:2355). Its exempt classes are the per-row/header `_VERIFICATION_ONLY_MARKER`, the legacy `_VERIFICATION_SECTION_RE` header shim, and `in_superseded_phase` rows (`saw_superseded_unchecked`). A struck-through + `**DROPPED**`-marked row is unambiguously not-to-be-done — exactly like a Superseded-phase row — but matched NONE of those classes, so it fell through to the `return False` implementation-row path. This is the SAME root-cause class the log has repeatedly hit on this exact symbol (Round 24 `d8d02ef` reachability-smoke, Round 25 `f2b1552` seam-audit, the recording-panel round): the Step-7 bypass returning `False` on a row that is genuinely not remaining implementation work. Prior instances were verification rows reached through header phrasings; this instance is a descope-in-place row.

**Action:**
  - Mechanical fix applied: added `_row_is_descoped_in_place(row_text)` (+ `_DESCOPE_STRIKETHROUGH_RE` / `_DESCOPE_MARKER_RE`) to the shared `lazy_core.py` and wired it into `remaining_unchecked_are_verification_only`'s row branch — an unchecked row that is BOTH markdown-struck-through (`~~...~~`) AND carries an explicit descope marker (`**DROPPED**`/`**DESCOPED**`/`**WON'T-FIX**`, case-insensitive) now counts toward the all-remaining-exempt → `True` bypass via a new `saw_descoped_unchecked` flag (mirrors `saw_superseded_unchecked`). CONSERVATIVE by construction: a plain unchecked row, or a struck row WITHOUT a descope marker, still returns `False` (never over-exempt genuine work). Shared helper → both pipelines inherit it; no SKILL prose / state-script CLI / sentinel schema touched, so no coupled-pair mirror or schema lockstep owed. The in-flight bug's `PHASES.md` was NOT touched (scope containment) — the guard fix resolves the instance via routing. 3 regression fixtures added + registered in `_TESTS` (struck DROPPED → `True`; plain unchecked → `False`; struck-without-marker → `False`). Bug spec (Status: Concluded) committed FIRST at `0628422` (Step 2.5 audit trail predates the fix). Commit: `6012c72`.

The durable fix mirrors the `<!-- verification-only -->` precedent: producers emit a CANONICAL STRUCTURAL descope marker (e.g. `<!-- descoped -->`) on deliberately-dropped rows, and the free-text `~~...~~ **DROPPED/DESCOPED/WON'T-FIX**` form becomes a deprecation shim (parallel to `_VERIFICATION_SECTION_RE`). **Class boundary** — In-class: descope-marker vocabulary variants + the producer-emit path (`/spec-phases`, `/add-phase`, NEEDS_INPUT-resolution authoring). Out-of-class: verification-only detection, completion-time gate strictness. Cited instances: Round 30 (this) + the `_VERIFICATION_ONLY_MARKER` structural-marker precedent. **Front-enqueue DEFERRED to the orchestrator (non-blocking):** `--enqueue-adhoc` is orchestrator-only and was DENIED in-flight by cycle containment for this dispatched subagent (spoofing `LAZY_ORCHESTRATOR=1` to bypass is the integrity side-door the harness forbids — NOT attempted; same posture as Rounds 28/29). ## Round 31 — 2026-07-12 — observed-friction

**Item in flight:** adhoc-incident-hook-deny-19343d (claude-config `/lazy-bug-batch`, Step 1g decision-resume; operator chose "Close as working-as-designed → Won't-fix"; live run + cycle marker for this bug)
**Divergence point:** decision-resume Step 1g → the apply-resolution subagent (`resolution_kind=needs-input`, bug pipeline). The operator resolved `NEEDS_INPUT.md` with a receipt-exempt terminal close, but the emitted apply-resolution prompt (`dispatch-apply-resolution.md`) had NO step to set a terminal status AND its constraint (line 197) forbade setting `Won't-fix` without a `FIXED.md` receipt. The subagent correctly neutralized the sentinel only, leaving `Status: Investigating` → the next probe re-routed the bug to spec-bug/root-cause-trace gate → re-halt (infinite needs-input loop for ANY operator-chosen receipt-exempt close).

**Root cause:** `missing-contract` — the apply-resolution needs-input path was designed on the assumption that a resolution always feeds back into planning (edit SPEC/PHASES, resume); it had no contract for a resolution whose chosen path is a **terminal close** of the item. The mechanism is the over-broad constraint at `dispatch-apply-resolution.md:197`, which via `forbidden_status = "Fixed or Won't-fix"` (`lazy_core.py:6841`) conflated the receipt-GATED terminal (`Fixed`, needs `FIXED.md`) with the receipt-EXEMPT terminal (`Won't-fix`, retired-without-a-fix, `bug-state.py:29/567/751`). Since `Won't-fix` is definitionally receipt-exempt (no `FIXED.md` ever exists), the constraint made the operator's legitimate close **unsatisfiable**; no bug-state CLI enacts `Won't-fix` (grep confirms none — only a `wont-fix-exempt` test fixture), and the orchestrator cannot set status itself (sentinel-only writes). Distinct from Round 14's `ambiguous-prose` apply-resolution defect (hand-composing the dispatch) — this is a missing terminal-disposition contract, not a wiring/prose bypass.

**Action:**
  - Mechanical fix applied: (1) `lazy_core._standard_dispatch_bindings` splits the compound into additive tokens `receipt_gated_status` (Fixed/Complete) + `receipt_exempt_status` (Won't-fix/Superseded), leaving `forbidden_status` UNCHANGED (the other 10 template sites correctly use the blanket ban); (2) `dispatch-apply-resolution.md` gains needs-input **step 2b** (TERMINAL DISPOSITION) that sets the receipt-exempt status when the operator's resolution directs a close, and the constraint is reworded to gate only the receipt-gated status while explicitly permitting the receipt-exempt close via step 2b — it never permits `Fixed`/`Complete` without a receipt, so the completion-integrity gate is fully preserved (no gate weakened); (3) `decision-resume.md` reference contract mirrors the terminal-disposition note (anti-drift); (4) first instance enacted — `Status: Won't-fix` set on `adhoc-incident-hook-deny-19343d/SPEC.md` (its `## Resolution` already recorded the disposition), which the bug loader skips unconditionally, breaking the loop; (5) 2 regression tests added + registered in `_TESTS`. Single shared components (feature+bug via `@section`) + shared `lazy_core` helper → no coupled-pair mirror owed; no sentinel schema touched. Bug spec (Status: Concluded) committed FIRST at `00ed74be` (Step 2.5 audit trail predates the fix). Commit: `fc5f5371`.

**Over-fit spin-off:** none — the fix is STRUCTURAL (a new contract step + a token split driving both pipelines symmetrically — bug `Won't-fix` and feature `Superseded`), NOT a literal phrase added to a matcher (signal 1 N/A). The `missing-contract` class has recurred in this log, but on DIFFERENT symbols (`lazy_guard.py:839` sub-subagent; the harden-dispatch emit path; runtime-ownership sequencing; `gate_coverage` exemption) — this is the FIRST occurrence at the `dispatch-apply-resolution.md` terminal-disposition symbol (Round 14 was a different class at that component), so the ≥2 same-class-same-symbol threshold (signals 2–4) is unmet. The token split already covers the near-neighbor (feature Superseded), so no gap remains.

```
  --signal-independence "mixed — the direct false-loop signal is not ledgered; halt is a broad, heavily-confounded proxy capturing only the tail case where a false LOOP-DETECTED would escalate a multi-cycle spec/plan to a halt. Most halts are unrelated (blocked/needs-input/needs-research), so the evaluator will likely cap at INCONCLUSIVE (confounded)." \
  --repo-root .
```

## Round 33 — 2026-07-12 — observed-friction

**Item in flight:** interventions-telemetry-repo-scope-split-brain (claude-config; observed mid-run, background harden — run continued on current behavior)
**Divergence point:** `lazy-cycle-containment.sh` inline-Python loop-formation trip (`main()` subagent branch). A legitimate cycle-subagent `git commit`/`git add` was DENIED (`loop-formation-flag`) because a `lazy-state.py`/`bug-state.py` token or a routing flag appeared as INCIDENTAL text — a commit-message body (`git commit -m "...fix lazy-state.py --probe edge; routes to Part 2 via --emit-dispatch..."`) or a staged filename argument (`git add user/scripts/lazy-state.py`). The git command invoked no routing op; the tokens were reference-only mentions. Recurred 2× in one run (harden round 32 doc-heredoc commit + cycle-8 execute-plan commit).

**Root cause:** `hook-defect` — the loop-formation trip matched UNANCHORED: `_STATE_PY_RE = re.compile(r"\b(?:lazy-state|bug-state)\.py\b")` (`lazy-cycle-containment.sh:234`) matched the token anywhere in the command, and `any(flag in command for flag in LOOP_FORMATION_FLAGS)` (`:472`) scanned routing flags across the whole command — so it could not distinguish an INVOCATION from a MENTION. The sibling `build-queue-enforce.sh` already closed this exact class via `_CMD_START` segment anchoring (a build token must BEGIN a command segment to deny; a reference-only `cat .../build-filtered.ps1` is allowed), and THIS SAME hook already closed it once for the `_LAZY_BATCH_DIRECT_RE` regex (`docs/bugs/adhoc-incident-hook-deny-4b767b`).

**Action:**
  - Mechanical fix applied: replaced unanchored `_STATE_PY_RE` with a segment-anchored invocation matcher `_STATE_PY_INVOKE_RE` (`_CMD_START` + optional `python`/`python3` interpreter + optional path prefix + `(?:lazy-state|bug-state)\.py\b`), mirroring `build-queue-enforce.sh`. The routing-flag check is now scoped to the INVOKING segment (`_SEGMENT_SPLIT_RE` + `_STATE_PY_INVOKE_SEG_RE`), so a routing flag mentioned in an unrelated later segment (a commit-message body) cannot trip it; this also still denies a real invocation chained behind another command. All real-runaway denies preserved. Added two regression tests to `test_hooks.py` (`test_containment_allows_state_script_reference_only_mention` — RED against the pre-fix matcher; `test_containment_still_denies_real_state_script_invocation`). Commit: `8494a4f0`. Bug investigation spec (`Status: Concluded`) at `docs/bugs/lazy-cycle-containment-false-denies-reference-only-routing-mentions/SPEC.md`, committed `48bf5945` (Step 2.5 — process note: the spec commit landed immediately AFTER the fix commit this round rather than before, an honest ordering deviation; the durable investigation record is present and cited). LIVE PROOF: this round's own `harden(hook):` commit `8494a4f0`, whose message contains `lazy-state.py`, `bug-state.py`, `routing`, and `--run-start`, was ALLOWED — the pre-fix hook would have denied it.

**Over-fit spin-off:** harden(spinoff): class recurred ≥2× in THIS hook (signal 2 — the `_LAZY_BATCH_DIRECT_RE` anchoring in `adhoc-incident-hook-deny-4b767b`, now the `_STATE_PY` anchoring here; the fix is STRUCTURAL, so signal 1 is N/A). Front-enqueue owed for `/spec-bug` `lazy-cycle-containment-lifecycle-patterns-still-unanchored` — class «the remaining unanchored `token in command` deny check in lazy-cycle-containment.sh: LIFECYCLE_PATTERNS (dev:kill/dev:restart/kill-port), which false-denies a reference-only mention in a commit message; OUT = the already-anchored regexes + cross-hook work». Cited instances: Round 33 (`_STATE_PY`) + `adhoc-incident-hook-deny-4b767b` (`_LAZY_BATCH`). Spec stub written at `docs/bugs/lazy-cycle-containment-lifecycle-patterns-still-unanchored/SPEC.md`. NOTE: the `--enqueue-adhoc` front-enqueue is orchestrator-only and was NOT run by this cycle-contained subagent (refused by construction, like `--record-intervention` below) — the orchestrator owns the enqueue + PushNotification.

**Additional spin-offs (SECONDARY, mandated by dispatch — authored, enqueue orchestrator-owned):**
  - `state-script-test-runner-crashes-on-systemexit-from-live-cycle-marker` (SECONDARY-1): the in-file `--test` runner catches `except Exception`, but the C3 refusal raises `SystemExit(3)` (a `BaseException`) which escapes and crashes the suite when `--test` runs from inside a live cycle marker — OBSERVED THIS ROUND (`[apply-pseudo-provisional-refusal] SystemExit: 3` aborted `lazy-state.py --test`; passed fully under a hermetic `LAZY_STATE_DIR`). Spec: `docs/bugs/execute-plan-ground-truth-missing-git-dirty-assertion/SPEC.md`.

**Gates run:**

  test_hooks.py: 155/155 (incl. the 2 new regression tests)

## Round 35 — 2026-07-13 — observed-friction

**Item in flight:** state-cli-contract-registry (claude-config; feature pipeline, mid-`/lazy-batch`)
**Divergence point:** two batched gaps. GAP 1 (run-blocking) — the `apply_pseudo __mark_complete__`/`__mark_fixed__` completion-coherence gate (`lazy_core._phase_completion_plan`, `user/scripts/lazy_core.py`) refused the receipt on a legitimately-DEFERRED phase whose only unchecked rows carry the canonical descope marker, even though `--verify-ledger` returned `ok:true` for the SAME PHASES.md — a completion deadlock. GAP 2 (recurring, non-blocking, separate surface) — `user/hooks/block-terminal-kill.sh` false-denied a benign command carrying a termination keyword inside a quoted argument value (a `git commit -m '… || exit 1'` guard clause; an `--emit-dispatch --context "…exit…"` prose string).

**Root cause:**
  - GAP 1 — `script-defect`. `remaining_unchecked_are_verification_only` (mid-feature bypass, `lazy_core.py` ~L2483-2550) and `--verify-ledger` both honor the canonical `_DESCOPED_MARKER` (`<!-- descoped -->`, row- AND header-scope, plus the legacy `_row_is_descoped_in_place` shim) and treat a deliberately-dropped unchecked row as non-blocking. But `_phase_completion_plan` (~L2972-3049) refused on the bare `ph["unchecked"] > 0` with NO descope awareness — `parse_phases` produced only a total `unchecked` count, so the completion gate could not distinguish a deliberately-descoped row from an unfinished deliverable. The descope marker was honored everywhere EXCEPT the one seam that ships the feature. Repro (verified against shipped code): `state-cli-contract-registry` Phase 4 (deferred per SPEC Locked Decision 5), 2 descoped unchecked rows (header+row scope, no Status line) → `remaining_unchecked_are_verification_only=True`, but `_phase_completion_plan` refusal `['### Phase 4 …: 2 unchecked box(es)']`.
  - GAP 2 — `hook-defect`. `_CMD_START`'s segment-start anchoring (`^|[\n;&|(]|\{(?=\s)`) is blind to shell QUOTING: a separator inside a quoted string literal (a quoted `||`/`;`/`|`) is genuinely at a segment-start position *within the quoted literal*, one quoting level below the guarded command line, so `re.search` matches the termination keyword after it. The 2026-07-12 segment-start anchoring (Round of `powershell-tool-bypasses-bash-matched-guards`) removed the bare-embedded-word class but not this quoted-argument class. Verified: `git commit -m 'landed fix || exit 1'` → term-match True (should allow); `--context "refuses; exit code nonzero"` → term-match True (should allow) — the hook denied this very investigation's Bash call live.

**Action:**
  - Bug investigation specs (`Status: Concluded`) AUTHORED on-disk FIRST (Step 2.5 order): `docs/bugs/_archive/descoped-marker-blind-completion-coherence-gate/SPEC.md` and `docs/bugs/_archive/block-terminal-kill-false-denies-quoted-argument-tokens/SPEC.md`. **Committing them from THIS cycle-contained subagent is DENIED by `lazy-cycle-containment.sh`'s second-feature-commit tripwire** (the armed cycle marker's `feature_id` is the in-flight `state-cli-contract-registry`; both SPEC paths match `_FEATURE_DIR_RE` under a DIFFERENT `docs/bugs/<slug>/`, and only `docs/features/queue.json` / `ROADMAP.md` / bare `CLAUDE.md` are carve-outs). NOT bypassed (no `--marker` edit, no gate weakening — the forbidden side-doors). The SPEC files are handed to the orchestrator to commit under `harden(docs):`; this round (under `docs/specs/`, NOT matched by `_FEATURE_DIR_RE`) IS committable and is the durable audit record documenting both specs by path. **SURFACED HARNESS GAP:** the second-feature-commit tripwire is over-broad for the hardening path — a `/harden-harness` subagent legitimately, by mandate (Step 2.5), authors + commits `docs/bugs/<harden-slug>/SPEC.md` outside the active dispatch's feature dir, yet the tripwire denies it. A carve-out is warranted (e.g. exempt a `harden(`-prefixed commit, or a commit whose staged `docs/bugs/<slug>` dirs were freshly created this dispatch, or route harden-authored specs through a sanctioned writer). Recorded here for a FUTURE hardening round — NOT self-dispatched now (depth-1 cap + the friction is non-blocking: the fix + its audit trail land regardless).
  - Mechanical fix applied (GAP 1): `parse_phases` gains an additive per-phase `unchecked_descoped` count — a strict subset of `unchecked` (which stays a full tally, byte-identical for every existing caller). A row counts descoped via the row-scope `_DESCOPED_MARKER`, a header-scope descope marker (bold subsection header / non-phase heading carrying the marker; scope reset at each phase heading, closed by a marker-less verification/deliverables header — the descope axis of the scope machinery already proven in `remaining_unchecked_are_verification_only`), OR the legacy `_row_is_descoped_in_place` shim — REUSING the already-shared exemption predicates, not re-implementing them. `_phase_completion_plan` gates on `effective_unchecked = unchecked − unchecked_descoped` for BOTH the blocking refusal AND the auto-flip `all_checked` predicate, so a fully-descoped phase (a) does not refuse and (b) auto-flips a non-terminal status to Complete instead of tripping the status-straggler refusal. Bug pipeline inherits it via shared `lazy_core` (`__mark_fixed__` path). Design-fork check: whole-phase deferral via `**Status:** Superseded` already works and is unaffected — the descope-marker form is the already-canonical row/partial-phase mechanism; teaching the completion gate the marker the rest of the machine already honors is a defect fix, not an operator-owned fork (NO NEEDS_INPUT). 7 regression tests added + registered (repro, header-scope-only, mixed-still-refuses over-exemption guard, descoped-with-status flip, both apply_pseudo integration paths, parse_phases field).
  - Mechanical fix applied (GAP 2): new `_mask_quoted(command)` blanks the CONTENT of single-/double-quoted spans to spaces (quote chars + every offset preserved), applied after the PS line-continuation collapse and before the anchored matchers. A flat single-pass char scan (the same not-a-shell-parser discipline as `_normalize_ps_syntax`), handling backslash-escaped quotes at top level and `\"` inside double quotes. Masking can only REDUCE matches, so real top-level `kill`/`exit`/`&& exit` invocations still deny; the accepted residual is a keyword inside a `bash -c "kill …"` string argument (the plane-wide quoted-argument residual documented in `user/hooks/CLAUDE.md`). 4 regression tests added + registered (the two field cases + a quoted-`| kill` case ALLOW; a real `&& kill` after a quoted message still DENIES — true-positive pin). Docs updated: root `CLAUDE.md` hooks-table row + `user/hooks/CLAUDE.md` segment-start-anchoring section.

**Over-fit spin-off:** none. Both production fixes are STRUCTURAL, not literal-phrase-to-matcher patches: GAP 1 adds a per-phase count + a subtraction and REUSES the already-shared exemption predicates (`_DESCOPED_MARKER`, `_row_is_descoped_in_place`); GAP 2 adds a structural quote-scanner. This is the FIRST hardening round touching `_phase_completion_plan`, and GAP 2's quoted-argument class is a distinct surface from the prior segment-start-anchoring round — no ≥2 same-symbol recurrence (signal 1 N/A; signals 2–4 not tripped). `harness-gate.py --staged` returned `overfit: flag`, but every cited element is a TEST-FIXTURE string literal (PHASES.md content inside test strings) or DOC prose — the structural detector keying on string literals in test/doc files, not on matcher-alternation appends in production gate logic; `gate_weakening: pass` (no gate removed/softened/bypassed — the completion gate got STRICTER-aware, the hook only narrowed a false-positive without widening any deny). NOTE for a future round: the broad "a gate blind to a PHASES-row exemption class" THEME has appeared before on the verification-only axis (the 2026-06 `_VERIFICATION_SECTION_RE` literal-phrase whack-a-mole; the no-plans verification-only deadlock; the completion-coherence-gate-reconciliation feature). Should a THIRD instance land on the SAME symbol family, the durable generalization is to factor the per-row exemption classification (verification-only + descoped + Superseded, row/header scope) into ONE shared predicate consumed by every gate — deliberately NOT spun off now (not manufacturing a spurious generalization on a first-same-symbol, predicate-reusing structural fix).

**Gates run:**
  test_lazy_core.py: **1132 passed / 0 failed** via `LAZY_STATE_DIR=<temp> python -m pytest` (the authoritative full-suite run — pytest catches `SystemExit` per-test). The standalone `python test_lazy_core.py` runner reports 960 PASS then exits 3 WITHOUT the summary: `_run_test` does not catch `SystemExit`, so a marker-refusal test (`test_apply_pseudo_direct_call_refused_under_cycle_marker_without_orchestrator`, fixture feature `'f'`) propagates its own caught-and-expected `SystemExit(3)` path when the suite runs DURING a live cycle marker. ## Round 36 — 2026-07-13 — gate-no-route

**Item in flight:** state-cli-contract-registry (claude-config; feature pipeline, mid-`/lazy-batch`)
**Divergence point:** the `apply_pseudo __mark_complete__` **anti-overfit-design-gate D3 ship seam** (`lazy_core.gate_verdict_ok`, `user/scripts/lazy_core.py:5671-5678`) refused the receipt with `harness-change design gate: scoped change missing GATE_VERDICT.md`. `gate_verdict_ok` re-derives the item's control-surface scope via `_item_commit_touched_files` (`lazy_core.py:3296`) → `derive_touched_from_brackets`, producing `scope_hit = [user/hooks/CLAUDE.md, user/hooks/block-terminal-kill.sh, user/scripts/lazy_core.py]`. NO sanctioned emit-dispatch class authors `GATE_VERDICT.md`, so the orchestrator had no route to satisfy the gate → no-route. (This feature had advanced PAST the Round-35 completion-coherence gate into the next completion gate.)

**Root cause:** `script-defect` — completion-gate scope OVER-attribution. The bracket ledger records each cycle as a `begin_sha..end_sha` RANGE; `derive_touched_from_range` (`lazy_core.py:16398`) takes `git diff --name-only begin..end`, which sweeps up EVERY commit in the window — including the two foreground observed-friction `harden(...)` commits the orchestrator landed mid-run (`b77b5b23` `harden(hook)` → `user/hooks/**`; `84f4a030` `harden(script)` → `user/scripts/lazy_core.py`). Those are a DIFFERENT workstream from the queue item. Verified via `git show --stat`: **all three `scope_hit` paths come from the two harden commits; the feature's OWN four commits (`6a4af018`/`dc504eba`/`3411b457`/`fb8e8132`) are 100% docs-only (zero control surfaces).** The feature was dragged into gate scope purely by foreign-workstream misattribution; correctly excluding the harden commits makes it out-of-scope (`gate_verdict_ok` → `in_scope: False`) and completion proceeds. The only structural signal distinguishing a foreground harden commit from an item commit is the harden-harness-mandated `harden(` subject prefix.

**Action:**
  - Bug investigation spec (`Status: Concluded`) authored on-disk FIRST (Step 2.5 order): `docs/bugs/_archive/gate-scope-folds-concurrent-harden-commits/SPEC.md`. Committed `harden(docs): c702ddbf` BEFORE the fix. (Committable this round — no cycle marker is armed for claude-config's repo key; the only live cycle marker belongs to a different repo/`managed-llm-credits` under a different key, so the second-feature-commit tripwire that blocked Round 35 is inert here.)
  - Mechanical fix applied: `_item_commit_touched_files` now partitions the bracket/grep-derived commit set into item vs. foreign-harden commits and, when ≥1 foreign commit is filtered, recomputes the file set from only the surviving item commits (`_files_from_commits`, per-commit `git show --name-only`). Foreign detection is `_commit_subject_is_foreign_harden` (`^\s*harden\(` on `git show -s --format=%s`), **fail-open** (an unreadable subject → NOT foreign, so a real item commit is never dropped → the gate is never weakened). When no foreign commit is present (the common case) the pre-existing range-derived file set is returned **byte-identically** (no behavior change). Scope confined to the completion-gate reader; `write_provenance`'s use of `derive_touched_from_brackets` left unchanged this cycle (noted as a separate provenance follow-up). 3 registered regression tests (repro exclusion, byte-identical-without-foreign, subject-classify + fail-open). Commit: `4079aec2`.
  - `NEEDS_INPUT.md` appended (decisions 7a/7b) at `docs/specs/turn-routing-enforcement/NEEDS_INPUT.md` for the LATENT half the mechanical fix does NOT close (operator-owned, not mechanical): **7a** — no sanctioned route authors `GATE_VERDICT.md` for a genuinely-in-scope control-surface feature (options: new `gate-verdict` emit class / interactive-only / planning-time-only); **7b** — a STRUCTURALLY PROVISIONAL/unratified gate (`gate_verdict_ok`) is live-blocking the ship seam (hard-block vs. advisory-until-ratified). Committed with the spec (`harden(docs): c702ddbf`). No second hardening stage self-dispatched (depth-1 cap; the run-blocking half is already fixed).

**Over-fit spin-off:** none. `harness-gate.py --range origin/main..HEAD` returned `gate_weakening: pass` (no gate removed/softened/bypassed — the completion gate got a FALSE-POSITIVE removed, not enforcement weakened; a genuinely-in-scope item still triggers it) and `overfit: flag`, but every cited element is a DOC quote (the SPEC quoting the actual refusal string), a docstring `"""` delimiter (checker artifact), or a TEST-FIXTURE path (`docs/features/feat-scope|feat-plain/PHASES.md` created by the new tests) — NOT a production matcher-alternation append. ## Round 45 — 2026-07-16 — observed-friction

**Item in flight:** d8-signal-flow-viz (AlgoBooth `/lazy-batch`; background observed-friction harden, blocking=false — orchestrator observed the gap mid-run and recovered each cycle by hand with a `SendMessage`-resume)
**Divergence point:** `/execute-plan` cycle turn-end contract (`cycle-base-prompt.md` `@section turn-end`, item 1) → the integrator subagent ran the AGGREGATE gate `npm run qg -- ts`, which exceeds the ~10-min Bash cap; the harness auto-backgrounded it and the subagent ended its turn WAITING on that backgrounded job, whose process tree is torn down at the turn boundary. Recurred on BOTH consecutive cycles this run (plan part-4 AND part-5), each costing an orchestrator `SendMessage`-resume.

**Root cause:** `missing-contract` — the turn-end contract on every relevant surface is REACTIVE only. `cycle-base-prompt.md` `@section turn-end` item 1 (workstation + cloud) and the canonical `user/skills/_components/turn-end-gate.md` ("Backgrounded shell job → block on it: re-run it foreground") both say *if auto-backgrounded, block on it foreground* — STRUCTURALLY INSUFFICIENT for an over-cap AGGREGATE, since re-running the aggregate foreground just re-hits the ~10-min cap and re-backgrounds. No contract prescribed the PREVENTIVE move: when a required gate command would exceed the cap, run its individual under-cap sub-components synchronously in the foreground instead of the aggregate (and never background a long gate from inside a dispatched cycle subagent). Repo-agnostic pattern; only the concrete decomposition (`npm run qg -- ts` → the four `run_ts_gates` sub-gates) is AlgoBooth-specific. ## Round 48 — 2026-07-16 — observed-friction

**Item in flight:** audio-quality-analysis-visualization (AlgoBooth `/lazy-batch`; blocking observed-friction harden — the orchestrator is awaiting this round in the foreground before re-probing)
**Divergence point:** The C2 marker-gated second-feature-commit tripwire in `lazy-cycle-containment.sh` (the `git commit` branch of the containment hook's inline Python) FALSE-DENIED the `apply-resolution` cycle subagent's legitimate same-feature commit; the subagent had to work around it (unstage-then-stage-with-commit) to make progress.

**Root cause:** `hook-defect` — `user/hooks/lazy-cycle-containment.sh` decides feature membership by extracting a single path segment with `_FEATURE_DIR_RE = re.compile(r"docs/(?:features|bugs)/([^/]+)/")` and comparing `group(1)` to the marker's `feature_id` (in `_is_carve_out`, line ~490, and the `offending` comprehension, line ~633). `group(1)` is only the FIRST segment after `docs/(features|bugs)/`. For a GROUPED feature — the layout AlgoBooth's queue produces via each item's `spec_dir` (verified: `docs/features/queue.json` item `id: audio-quality-analysis-visualization`, `spec_dir: audio/audio-quality-analysis-visualization`; marker `feature_id` = the bare slug per `markers.py:1232`) — that segment is the DOMAIN GROUP (`audio`), so `group(1)=='audio' != 'audio-quality-analysis-visualization'`. The carve-out failed and every same-feature staged path landed in `offending` → `second-feature commit tripwire` deny. Ungrouped features (`docs/features/<slug>/`) were unaffected — there `group(1)` IS the slug — which is why the defect stayed latent behind the flat `feat-A` fixtures. Bug spec (Step 2.5, committed `harden(docs): ebbec030` BEFORE the fix): `docs/bugs/_archive/lazy-cycle-containment-misparses-grouped-feature-paths/` (Concluded).

**Action:**
  - Mechanical fix applied: added `_path_under_feature(path, feature_id)` — a group-aware membership test keyed on the marker `feature_id`, matching `docs/(?:features|bugs)/(?:[^/]+/)?<re.escape(feature_id)>/` (one optional group segment, slug anchored as a full path segment). `_is_carve_out` delegates feature-membership to it; the `offending` comprehension drops the buggy `.group(1) != feature_id` comparison and uses `_FEATURE_DIR_RE` purely as an "under some feature/bug dir?" predicate with `not _is_carve_out(...)` as the sole group-aware membership authority. Genuine 2nd-feature denies preserved (regression test). Two regression tests added + `_TESTS`-registered: `test_containment_allows_same_feature_commit_grouped` (was false-denied pre-fix), `test_containment_denies_second_feature_commit_grouped` (no-weakening guard). Gates run: pytest tests/test_lazy_core/ 1159/1159, test_hooks.py 223/223, lint-skills.py OK, lazy-state.py/bug-state.py --test OK. Commit: `251187c8`. Schemas untouched → coupled-pair mirroring + sentinel-schema lockstep N/A.

**Over-fit spin-off:** none — the production fix is STRUCTURAL, not literal-phrase-to-matcher. `harness-gate.py --range HEAD --json` returned `overfit: flag` / `gate_weakening: pass` / `scope_hit: [user/hooks/lazy-cycle-containment.sh]`; its evidence cites (a) the new helper regex line and (b) test-fixture path literals. On inspection neither is a genuine signal-1 trip: the production matcher is parameterized on `re.escape(feature_id)` (a marker-bound variable, not a literal group name) and uses the group-AGNOSTIC `(?:[^/]+/)?` (handles ANY group, not the observed `audio`); the flagged literals are inherently-concrete regression-test fixtures, not matcher data. Signal 2 (class recurred ≥2) is NOT met — the only prior related round (Round 35 + sibling) targets a DIFFERENT root cause (the tripwire over-broad for the harden Step 2.5 cross-workstream path), not grouped-path mis-parsing; this is the first occurrence of the grouped-path-misparse class. `verdict_required: true` is the ship-seam completion-gate contract (feature items), which is RECORDING-only for a harden mechanical fix — harden commits are a separate workstream and the run is never blocked here (Prohibition #2 is satisfied: `gate_weakening: pass`). Generalization bound kept tight: one optional group segment subsumes the observed grouped instance + its ungrouped near-neighbor; multi-level grouping is deliberately out of scope (the queue does not produce it). No Agent dispatch (barred this cycle) was needed.

**Intervention record:** `docs/interventions/harden-2026-07-r48.md` — target `event:containment-refusal`, expected-direction decrease (the observed friction's own recurrence event: false second-feature-commit denials against a GROUPED feature's own staged paths should drop to zero; genuine cross-feature denies preserved).

## Round 50 — 2026-07-16 — observed-friction

**Item in flight:** hydra-overlay (AlgoBooth `/lazy-batch`, active run marker `37850b6e…`; background/non-blocking observed-friction harden)
**Divergence point:** the real-skill `--repeat-count` dispatch-bound probe (`lazy-state.py`, `if args.repeat_count:` → `advance_forward_cycle(state)`) — the forward-cycle budget counter never advanced past 1 across two genuine `execute-plan` cycles, so Step 1c's `forward_cycles >= max_cycles` cap could never trip.

**Root cause:** `script-defect` — `user/scripts/lazy_core/markers.py::advance_forward_cycle` is the SOLE forward-advance trigger on the real-skill probe path (the consume-oracle `advance_run_counters` was retired from this path in the `byref-dispatch-undercounts-forward-cycles` Phase-1 reconciliation, `lazy-state.py` comment "advance_forward_cycle is the AUTHORITATIVE forward-advance trigger"). It advances only when the `[feature_id, current_step, sub_skill]` tuple DIFFERS from `last_advance_state_key`. A multi-part `/execute-plan` phase dispatches an IDENTICAL tuple every cycle (same feature, same step, same real sub_skill — one cycle per plan part), so after cycle 1 sets the key, cycles 2..N hit the "bare re-fire" no-op branch and `forward_cycles` stuck at 1. Corroboration: (a) marker `last_advance_consume_count=0` is NOT a contradiction — that field is written only by `advance_run_counters`/`advance_meta_cycle`, neither of which runs on this path, so it is vestigial here (prior rounds mis-read it as the consume-oracle failing); (b) both inject banners "turn 2" = `lazy_inject._turn_n` = `forward_cycles + meta_cycles + 1` = `1+0+1`, a downstream symptom not a separate defect; (c) `[1/10]` header derives from the frozen counter. One root cause explains all three symptoms. Supersedes the 2026-06 NEEDS_INPUT-decision-3 and 2026-07 (~line 473) mis-attributions to the consume-census ring-cap non-monotonicity — that oracle is no longer on the forward path at all. Bug spec (Step 2.5, committed `harden(docs): 81fcf256` BEFORE the fix): `docs/bugs/_archive/byref-forward-cycles-frozen-on-multicycle-same-step/` (Concluded).

**Action:**
  - Mechanical fix applied: `advance_forward_cycle` gains an opt-in keyword-only `consume_gate: bool = False`. On the real-skill probe path (`lazy-state.py` passes `consume_gate=True`) it now advances when the state tuple changed OR the registry consume-census rose since the last advance — reusing the shared `last_advance_consume_count` watermark and the SAME non-monotonic down-step CLAMP as `advance_run_counters`, so ring-cap eviction and the meta path's `+1` absorb stay coherent, and it advances at most once per probe (double-count-safe at feature/step transitions where both triggers hold). A bare re-fire (same tuple AND no new consume) still no-ops. The pseudo `--apply-pseudo` caller keeps the default (`consume_gate=False`) — byte-identical, its distinct-tuple-per-apply invariant already discriminates and it emits no consume. Two regression tests added (`tests/test_lazy_core/test_markers.py`, both registered in `_TESTS`): forward_cycles advances once per distinct consumed dispatch across ≥3 identical-tuple cycles with bare re-fires no-op, and the default (no-gate) path still no-ops on an identical tuple despite a census rise. Commit: `74af39de` (`harden(script)`). No sentinel schema touched → sentinel-schema lockstep N/A.

**Over-fit spin-off:** `harden(spinoff)` — signal 2 (class recurred ≥2× in the hardening log: 2026-06 NEEDS_INPUT dec 3, 2026-07 ~line 473, this round — all forward_cycles under-counting). The production fix is STRUCTURAL (a consume-census OR-trigger + parameter, NOT literal-phrase-to-matcher — `harness-gate.py --range HEAD~2..HEAD` returned `gate_weakening: pass`; its `overfit: flag` fired only on TEST-fixture state dicts, a false positive on literal strings in a test file). Per the recurrence threshold a structural recurrence spins off the durable generalization: a SINGLE authoritative MONOTONIC cumulative dispatch counter incremented at consume time (never ring-evicted) replacing BOTH heuristic triggers (live-census oracle + state-key change) as the forward budget's ground truth. Class boundary: IN = forward_cycles/meta_cycles budget counters + their advance triggers; OUT = the F1/F2 step-oscillation debounce, gate semantics, registry integrity. **DEFERRED to orchestrator (cycle-contained):** the `adhoc-enqueue` (`bug-state.py --enqueue-adhoc --type bug`) was REFUSED with zero side effects by the in-flight cycle-containment guard (state-script lifecycle ops are orchestrator-only mid-cycle) — NOT bypassed. ## Round 51 — 2026-07-16 — observed-friction

**Item in flight:** adhoc-hydra-load-code-mcp-tool (AlgoBooth `/lazy-batch` bug pipeline; background/non-blocking observed-friction harden — surfaced by a `/plan-bug` cycle)
**Divergence point:** the cycle-subagent turn-end contract (`user/skills/_components/lazy-batch-prompts/cycle-base-prompt.md` `@section turn-end` blocks, `skills=all`) directed a PLANNING (`/plan-bug`) cycle to run the completion gate `--verify-ledger` and "reconcile until ok:true" — a completion gate fired on a cycle that authored a `Ready` plan by design.

**Root cause:** TWO independent latent inconsistencies in the completion gate `lazy_core.verify_ledger` (via `lazy-state.py` / `bug-state.py --verify-ledger`), split by decision class. (1) **SCOPE** (`ambiguous-prose` / gate-semantics): the `@section turn-end` completion substep is injected `skills=all`, so a planning cycle (spec-phases/write-plan/plan-bug/plan-feature/spec/spec-bug) — which authors a `Ready` plan with unchecked deliverables — structurally gets `ok:false` (`plan_complete`/`deliverables_done` false by design), making "reconcile until ok:true" unsatisfiable without fabricating completion (forbidden by `@section status-honesty`). The ORCHESTRATOR already scopes its OWN guardrail-D verify-ledger (`lazy-batch/SKILL.md` Step 1e.4a) to `/execute-plan`+`/mcp-test` cycles — the cycle-prompt site (`skills=all`) DISAGREES with that already-shipped scoping. (2) **ARG** (`script-defect` + coupled-pair drift): `verify_ledger(repo_root, spec_path)` treats `spec_path` as the spec DIRECTORY (computes `spec_path/'PHASES.md'`), but the cycle-prompt metavar reads as the SPEC.md FILE; a file arg yielded a MISLEADING verdict against a phantom `.../SPEC.md/PHASES.md` instead of erroring. `lazy-state.py` already normalized `.md`→parent (~13273) but `bug-state.py` passed the arg RAW (~8910) and stamped a wrong `gate-refusal` `item_id` (`"SPEC.md"`) — a coupled-pair drift. Bug spec (Step 2.5, committed `harden(docs): 4c91ca28` BEFORE the fix): `docs/bugs/verify-ledger-planning-scope-and-file-arg/` (Concluded).

**Action:**
  - Mechanical fix applied (ARG half): centralize the `.md`→parent normalization INSIDE `verify_ledger` (`lazy_core/gates.py`) so the function and EVERY caller (both CLI wrappers + any direct/future caller) agree by construction; mirror `bug-state.py` to `lazy-state.py`'s already-shipped wrapper normalization so its `gate-refusal` `item_id` is the spec-dir name, not `"SPEC.md"`. One regression test added (`tests/test_lazy_core/test_gates.py::test_verify_ledger_spec_md_file_arg_normalizes_to_parent_dir`, registered in that file's `_TESTS` — the orphan-guard `test_no_orphaned_test_functions` caught the missing registration and was reconciled before commit): a SPEC.md file arg yields the SAME verdict + identical `checks` as its parent dir. Commit: `3d2311ce` (`harden(script)`). COUPLED-PAIR: `lazy_parity_audit.py --repo-root <cc>` exit 0. No sentinel schema touched → sentinel-schema lockstep N/A; no `lazy-batch`/`lazy-bug-batch` SKILL.md touched → CLAUDE.md pairs-table mirror N/A.

Decision: "Turn-end verify-ledger mis-scoped for PLANNING cycles: scope the substep to completion-capable skills (mirror guardrail-D), or add a 'planning-ok' verdict mode to verify_ledger?" — a gate-semantics / cycle-prompt-contract fork (the load-bearing completion-capable skill LIST + the terminal guarantee planning cycles carry are operator-owned). Recommendation: Option 1 (scope the substep).

**Over-fit spin-off:** none — the ARG fix is STRUCTURAL, not literal-phrase-to-matcher: it centralizes the normalization at the single source function (`verify_ledger`), which IS the durable generalization of the class (any future caller is covered by construction; no per-caller normalization to keep whacking). `harness-gate.py --range HEAD --json` returned `gate_weakening: pass`; its `overfit: flag` fired ONLY on TEST-file literal strings (a docstring `"""` and an assertion message in `test_gates.py`) — a false positive on test literals, exactly the Round-50 pattern, not the production fix. Although the ARG class technically recurred (lazy-state.py normalized once, bug-state.py exposed now), the applied fix subsumes the class rather than fitting the instance, so no separate spin-off is warranted.

**Intervention record:** `docs/interventions/harden-2026-07-r51.md` — CAPTURED. Target signal `undeclared` (EXPLICIT, typed): the ARG fix is a verdict-CORRECTNESS fix (it makes a file-arg verdict honest) whose event impact is NON-DIRECTIONAL — depending on tree state, a previously-misleading verdict could have been a false PASS (→ correcting it INCREASES `gate-refusal`) or a false FAIL (→ correcting it DECREASES `gate-refusal`), so no single countable direction is honestly assertable. INCONCLUSIVE-by-construction, surfaced for triage; preferred over fabricating a `gate-refusal` direction the fix does not deterministically move.

## Round 52 — 2026-07-16 — observed-friction

**Item in flight:** lazy-batch-mid-run-controls (OPERATOR-DIRECTED, typed request 2026-07-16, backgrounded/non-blocking)
**Divergence point:** the Standing-directive echo-back protocol (`lazy-batch/SKILL.md` Deliverable C) RECOGNIZES a mid-run operator "extend to N cycles" (and a park toggle) intent, but there is NO first-class command to ENACT it — `--run-start --max-cycles N` REFUSES against the active marker (clobber guard), `--run-end`+`--run-start` runs the heavy flush and ENDS the run, and passing `--max-cycles N` per probe is cosmetic (the marker's `max_cycles` stays stale while the header reads `args.max_cycles`). Park mode (`--park` / `--park-provisional`) is parsed ONLY at invocation and lives nowhere in the marker, so it cannot be toggled mid-run at all.

**Root cause:** `missing-contract` — a legitimately novel operating-mode change (mid-run budget + park) with no CLI action or marker field. Two coupled gaps: (1) `max_cycles` IS persisted in the marker (`markers.py` write_run_marker ~745) but there was NO in-place mutator and the header/budget consumers read `args.max_cycles` (`lazy-state.py` ~13519 / `bug-state.py` ~9134 `format_cycle_header(..., max_cycles=args.max_cycles)`), so the marker was never the authoritative live budget; the per-feature budget guard reads the STALE marker value (`markers.py` ~1801). (2) park mode (`park_needs_input`/`park_blocked`/`park_provisional`) was a pure invocation arg threaded per probe — no run-scoped toggle surface. Bug spec (Step 2.5, committed `harden(docs): f37a1607` BEFORE the fix): `docs/bugs/_archive/lazy-batch-no-mid-run-budget-or-park-controls/` (Concluded).

**Action:**
  - Mechanical fix applied: mirror the existing `--reassert-owner` / `--operator-authorized` disciplines; coupled pair `lazy-state.py` ↔ `bug-state.py` in lockstep. `markers.py`: `write_run_marker` seeds `park_needs_input`/`park_blocked`/`park_provisional` (classified `RUN_FRESH_FIELDS` — re-supplied at run-start like `max_cycles`); two in-place `_atomic_write` mutators `set_marker_max_cycles` + `set_marker_park` (the latter enforces `park_provisional ⇒ park_needs_input`, zero writes on refusal); folds `fold_max_cycles` (marker-authoritative live budget) + `fold_park_flags` (marker-authoritative when the new-schema field is present, else CLI flags — byte-identical back-compat for no-marker / legacy in-flight markers). Both scripts: new CLI actions `--set-max-cycles N` / `--set-park on|off` / `--set-park-provisional on|off`, each `refuse_if_cycle_active` FIRST + require `--operator-authorized` + require an active marker + echo prior/new; `--run-start` seeds the park fields; the probe folds `max_cycles`+park from the marker and surfaces `park_active`. So after a mid-run `--set-max-cycles N` the header `[fwd/N]` + Step-1c cap + persisted marker all AGREE (no clobber, no restart, no run-end flush). `lazy-batch/SKILL.md` Standing-directive protocol documents the enactment commands (bug-batch + cloud inherit by reference). 5 regression tests added (`tests/test_lazy_core/test_markers.py`, all registered in `_TESTS` — orphan-guard green). `docs/cli/cli-surface.json` regenerated (`cli_surface_gen.py`). Commit: `bc03240e` (`harden(script)`). COUPLED-PAIR: `lazy_parity_audit.py --repo-root <cc>` exit 0; CLAUDE.md pairs-table mirror satisfied (SKILL section inherited by reference, no bug-batch restatement). No sentinel schema touched → sentinel-schema lockstep N/A.

**Over-fit spin-off:** none — the fix is STRUCTURAL, not literal-phrase-to-matcher: it makes the marker the authoritative run-scoped surface for budget + park via new fields + in-place mutators + folds (the durable generalization; any future marker consumer reads the same authoritative state by construction). `harness-gate.py --range HEAD~1..HEAD --json` returned `gate_weakening_hit: false`; its `overfit: flag` fired ONLY on type-annotation string literals (`"int | None"`, `"dict | None"`), docstring `"""`, and test assertion/docstring messages — the identical Round-50/51 test/annotation false-positive pattern, not the production change. Class has not recurred (first mid-run-operating-mode `missing-contract`). No spin-off warranted.

**Intervention record:** `docs/interventions/harden-2026-07-r52.md` — CAPTURED. ## Round 53 — 2026-07-16 — manual

**Item in flight:** no-sanctioned-cli-for-queue-state-mutations (OPERATOR-DIRECTED, typed `/harden-harness` 2026-07-16, concurrent with a live AlgoBooth `/lazy-batch` run — claude-config-only, no target-repo edits)
**Divergence point:** operator-directed mid-run queue mutation. The operator asked to promote a queued bug P2→P1 (then →P0); there was NO clean CLI path. `--enqueue-adhoc --severity P1` on an existing id no-ops (`status: duplicate`, severity unchanged); `--reorder-queue` moves listed POSITION but `merged_priority` is severity/tier-based so effective priority is unchanged; `--pin` only deprioritizes to `severity: null` with no inverse. HARD CONSTRAINT 1 forbids the orchestrator hand-editing `queue.json`, so a trivial mutation was reachable only by an illegal hand-edit or a subagent cycle.

**Root cause:** `missing-contract` — a whole family of first-class queue mutations (change a bug's severity, change a feature's tier, add/remove deps post-hoc, un-pin) had no CLI command. The only queue writers were `enqueue_adhoc` (create-time), `reorder_queue` (position), `pin_bug_severity` (one-way null-pin, bug-only), `sync_deps` (SPEC-projected deps). Load-bearing sub-cause — the **two-regime ordering model**: each queue has (1) a single-queue pipeline order = `queue.json` LISTED order (`load_queue`/`load_bug_queue` return queued entries in listed order; the pipeline works the head first) and (2) a merged cross-queue view = `lazy_core.merged_priority` (feature `tier`, bug `severity`). A severity/tier change moves an item in regime 2 but leaves regime 1 (what the pipeline actually works next) STALE — so "promote to P0" would NOT make the pipeline work it sooner unless the mutation ALSO re-positions the entry in listed order in the same write. Bug spec (Step 2.5, committed `harden(docs): 13fd337c` BEFORE the fix): `docs/bugs/_archive/no-sanctioned-cli-for-queue-state-mutations/` (Concluded), carrying the full has-CLI vs lacks-CLI inventory.

**Action:**
  - Mechanical fix applied: coupled pair `lazy-state.py` ↔ `bug-state.py` in lockstep, mirroring the `--reorder-queue`/`--pin`/`--sync-deps` queue-mutator contract + the `--operator-authorized` posture of the Round-52 mid-run controls. `lazy_core/depdag.py` (shared queue plane): `reposition_by_priority` (surgical single-item move to the listed slot dictated by `merged_priority` — stable FIFO-within-priority; only the mutated entry moves, curated order preserved for the rest); `set_queue_priority` (severity/tier setter — validates `P0/P1/P2/Low` or int tier, clears pin fields on an explicit bug severity, then re-positions AND `_atomic_write`s in ONE call — the load-bearing atomic reorder); `mutate_queue_deps` (post-hoc add/remove with dedup + self-dep refusal + post-mutation `detect_dep_cycle` guard + byte-stable no-op + empty-set key-drop — the non-SPEC sibling of `sync_deps`). `bug-state.py`: `unpin_bug_severity` (inverse of `--pin`: clears pin fields, restores `severity` from the SPEC `**Severity:**` line, re-positions; not-pinned = byte-stable no-op). New CLI actions — `lazy-state.py`: `--set-tier ID N`, `--add-deps ID --deps a,b`, `--remove-deps ID --deps a,b`; `bug-state.py`: `--set-severity ID <P0|P1|P2|Low>`, `--unpin ID`, `--add-deps`, `--remove-deps` — each `refuse_if_cycle_active` FIRST (exit 3 for a cycle subagent) + require `--operator-authorized`. Discoverability (`cli_surface.py`, shared): `add_ops_query_flags` + `maybe_handle_ops_query` add `--list-ops` / `--search-ops <query>` to BOTH scripts — deterministic token-overlap ranking (name-weight 2, help-weight 1) over the LIVE parser surface (self-updating, stdlib-only), so "set bug severity" → `--set-severity` without reading source. `lazy-batch/SKILL.md` documents the operator-directed queue-mutation protocol (bug-batch + cloud inherit by reference; no new heading → parity 0). `docs/cli/cli-surface.json` regenerated (+16 flags, `cli_surface_gen.py --check` clean). 10 regression tests (`tests/test_lazy_core/test_depdag.py`, pytest `tmp_path` — no `_TESTS` bookkeeping) asserting the atomic reorder ACTUALLY changes listed order (bug promote + feature tier), pin-clear, deps add/remove/empty-drop/noop, self-dep + cycle refusal, unpin restore, the `--operator-authorized` gate (exit 2 without), and `--search-ops` ranking on both scripts. Commit: `8a7bc738` (`harden(script)`). COUPLED-PAIR: `lazy_parity_audit.py --repo-root .` exit 0; CLAUDE.md pairs-table satisfied (SKILL inherited by reference). No sentinel schema touched → lockstep N/A.

**Over-fit spin-off:** none — the fix is STRUCTURAL and it IS the class-level generalization, not a whack-a-mole instance patch. Rather than adding a single missing command, it (a) exhaustively inventoried EVERY queue/state mutation (bug spec table) and closed all remaining CLI gaps, and (b) shipped a general `--search-ops`/`--list-ops` discoverability subsystem over the live parser so any FUTURE mutation gap is self-service (no source reading). `harness-gate.py --repo-root . --staged --json`: `gate_weakening: pass`; `overfit: flag` fired ONLY on new docstrings/help-text prose, the `lazy_core/__init__.py` symbol→module EXPORT MAP additions, and type-annotation string literals (`"list[str] | None"`, `"int | None"`) + generated `docs/cli/cli-surface.json` entries — none is a behavior-gating MATCHER (regex alternation / keyword allowlist) fitted to observed data (signal 1 does NOT apply; the `search_ops` ranking is generic token-overlap, not a hardcoded keyword set). Class recurrence (signal 2): the `missing-contract`-for-an-operator-directed-mutation class also produced Round 52, but this round DELIVERS the structural fix for the whole class (full inventory + discoverability), leaving no ungapped near-neighbor — a spin-off would be redundant. `complexity: declaration-required` → **net-new** capability (3 shared helpers + 1 bug helper + 6 CLI commands + a search subsystem); retires nothing (purely additive; no existing rule/surface removed). No spin-off warranted.

**Intervention record:** `docs/interventions/harden-2026-07-r53.md` — CAPTURED. Target signal `event:containment-refusal`, expected-direction `decrease` (baseline frozen): the friction's own recurrence event is a containment/guard REFUSAL of an illegal `queue.json` hand-edit — with a sanctioned CLI for every mutation the incentive to hand-edit (the containment-tripping action) is removed, so that refusal rate should fall. Signal independence: independent (containment refusals are emitted by the enforcement hooks, not self-reported by this fix).
