## Round 54 — 2026-07-16 — observed-friction

**Item in flight:** hydra-overlay
**Divergence point:** the dispatch-bound routing surfaces — the enriched `lazy-state.py --repeat-count --emit-prompt --probe` probe AND the `lazy-route-inject.sh`→`lazy_inject.py` banner — route by feature-only state / the marker's STICKY `pipeline` field instead of the merged work-list head, bypassing the unified driver's `--next-merged` type-dispatch (`lazy-batch/SKILL.md` Step 1a).

**Root cause:** `hook-defect` (primary) + a paired `script-defect`. `lazy_inject.py::_run_probe` (pre-fix lines 111-119) selected the state script purely from `marker.get("pipeline", "feature")` — a per-run CONSTANT written once at `--run-start` (`markers.py` refuses a different-pipeline `--run-start` over an active marker). But a unified run's correct per-cycle type is the MERGED HEAD's type, which changes mid-run when a P0 bug jumps the bug-queue head. Because `lazy-batch/SKILL.md` line ~406 tells the orchestrator to CONSUME the injected banner directly and NOT re-probe, the stale-`feature` banner short-circuited the `--next-merged` type-dispatch and the P0 bug was never seen. Complementary script gap: `lazy-state.py --emit-prompt` runs `compute_state` over `docs/features/queue.json` only and has withholds for `pending-hardening-debt`/`audit-obligation` but none for "the merged head is a different, higher-priority item". LIVE EVIDENCE (2026-07-17): `--next-merged` correctly returned `{adhoc-hydra-sidecar-dist-esm-no-frames, bug}` while BOTH the enriched probe and the hook banner returned the `hydra-overlay` feature (execute-plan part-5); two P0 bugs silently skipped. `lazy_core.merged_priority` ordering was correct — the dispatch/hook paths just never consulted it.

**Action:**
  - Mechanical fix applied: wired the SAME `next_merged` ordering into both surfaces. (a) `lazy_core/dispatch.py` — new pure, fail-safe `merged_head_override(feature_items, bug_items, repo_root, current_item_id)` returning `{route_overridden_by: "merged-head-diverged", merged_head: {item_id, type}}` when the merged head diverges, else `None` (byte-identical common path). (b) `lazy-state.py --emit-prompt` — third `route_overridden_by` withhold (`merged-head-diverged`) after the hardening-debt/audit withholds; marker-gated + try/except fail-safe. (c) `bug-state.py --emit-prompt` — coupled-pair mirror (added `_load_feature_queue_for_merged` + the same withhold). (d) `lazy_inject.py::_run_probe` — selects the probe script by the merged head's TYPE via a `--next-merged` subprocess, fail-open to the marker pipeline. Regression fixtures: `test_dispatch.py` (4 helper unit tests + 1 end-to-end subprocess withhold test — P0 bug at head + actionable feature → `route_overridden_by=merged-head-diverged`, cycle_prompt null, no cycle registration) + `test_hooks.py` (inject banner routes bug-state.py when the merged head is a P0 bug). No gate weakened; no marker/pipeline-lifecycle change (the unified marker already drives `bug-state.py` per Step 1a). Bug spec (Step 2.5, committed `harden(docs): 1d34797d` BEFORE the fix): `docs/bugs/_archive/dispatch-probe-and-inject-bypass-merged-head/` (Concluded). Commit: `1af48e1d`.

**Over-fit spin-off:** none — the fix is STRUCTURAL (wires the merged-head consultation into the two dispatch-bound surfaces at their source), NOT a literal phrase added to a matcher (signal 1 N/A). ## Round 55 — 2026-07-17 — observed-friction

**Item in flight:** adhoc-hydra-sidecar-dist-esm-no-frames
**Divergence point:** run-marker lifecycle — (DEFECT 2) `lazy-batch/SKILL.md` Step 0.55 `--run-start` forwarded only `--max-cycles`/`--repo-root`, dropping the operator's `--park`/`--park-provisional` invocation flags, so a `--park` overnight run's marker was born park-OFF; (DEFECT 1) the inject-hook `--repeat-count` probe (`lazy-state.py:13538` → `advance_forward_cycle(consume_gate=True)`) advanced `forward_cycles` via the consume-INDEPENDENT state-change trigger on non-dispatch notification turns.

**Root cause:** DEFECT 2 = `ambiguous-prose` / missing flag forwarding. The CLI was NOT the defect — `lazy-state.py`/`bug-state.py --run-start` already thread `park_needs_input/park_blocked/park_provisional` into `write_run_marker` (park is a documented RUN_FRESH_FIELD re-supplied at run-start), but Step 0.55 never forwarded them, and the operator flag is the single `--park` umbrella while the CLI exposed only the two granular flags (a prose translation that was forgotten). DEFECT 1 = `script-defect` located but NOT mechanically fixable: `advance_forward_cycle` advances on `state_changed OR consume_rose`; a notification turn's route tuple changes (completed background dispatch flipped queue state) with no consume → false advance. Reversing them silently is Prohibition #2.

**Action:**

## Round 56 — 2026-07-17 — observed-friction

**Item in flight:** adhoc-incident-hook-deny-a51dde
**Divergence point:** the merged-head computation (`lazy_core.depdag.merged_worklist` / `next_merged`, consumed by `dispatch.merged_head_override` + the `--next-merged` CLI + both `--emit-prompt` `merged-head-diverged` withholds) ranks items by `merged_priority` ONLY and never excludes PARKED items — so in park mode, when the top-priority merged item is parked, the Round-54 withhold withholds the next-actionable item behind an undriveable parked head.

**Root cause:** `script-defect` — `merged_worklist` (`depdag.py:1222`) orders both queues by `merged_priority` with no park filter, so `next_merged`/`merged_head_override` can return a PARKED item as the merged head. The compute_state walk in each state script already SKIPS parked items (unresolved `NEEDS_INPUT.md` / `BLOCKED.md`, populating each probe's `parked[]` array) and advances to the next actionable item, but the merged-head view keeps pointing at the parked item; the Round-54 `merged-head-diverged` withhold (`lazy-state.py`/`bug-state.py --emit-prompt`) then withholds the actionable item's emission indefinitely. LIVE EVIDENCE (2026-07-17, `--park --park-provisional`): the two head-of-queue P0 bugs (`adhoc-hydra-sidecar-dist-esm-no-frames`, `adhoc-hydra-load-code-mcp-tool`) were BOTH parked on unresolved `NEEDS_INPUT.md`; `--next-merged` returned the parked `adhoc-hydra-sidecar-dist-esm-no-frames` and BOTH `--emit-prompt` probes returned `route_overridden_by=merged-head-diverged` (`cycle_model`/`cycle_prompt_ref` null) → the actionable `adhoc-incident-hook-deny-a51dde` (spec-bug) could not be dispatched → run DEADLOCK. The withhold is correct for genuine feature-vs-bug divergence; it is wrong when the head is parked (park mode cannot DRIVE it — driving just re-parks it).

**Action:**
  - Mechanical fix applied: exclude PARKED items from the merged-head computation, reusing the SAME park predicate the `parked[]` array uses. (a) `lazy_core/docmodel.py` — new pure, fail-safe `spec_dir_would_park(spec_dir, *, park_needs_input, park_blocked, park_provisional)` mirroring the compute_state park branches (canonical `BLOCKED.md` + stray `detect_noncanonical_blocker` under `--park-blocked`; unresolved `NEEDS_INPUT.md` under `--park-needs-input`, with `BLOCKED.md` precedence + provisional-eligible-ROUTES-not-parks under `--park-provisional`). (b) `lazy_core/depdag.py` — new `parked_item_ids(feature_items, bug_items, repo_root, *, park facets)` resolver (features → `docs/features/<spec_dir|id>`; bugs → loader `spec_path` else `docs/bugs/<spec_dir|id>`) + optional `exclude_ids` on `merged_worklist`/`next_merged`. (c) `dispatch.merged_head_override` — passes `exclude_ids` through. (d) callers: `lazy-state.py --next-merged` + both `--emit-prompt` probes (coupled pair) fold effective park facets (marker-authoritative `fold_park_flags`) and pass the parked exclusion set. No facet active → empty set → BYTE-IDENTICAL. Regression fixtures (`test_dispatch.py`, 4 new, registered in `_TESTS`): the predicate; the resolver over feature+bug dirs; the incident fixture (two parked P0 bugs + a lower-pri actionable bug → `--next-merged` returns the actionable bug, `merged_head_override` returns `None` WITH exclusion but the old parked head WITHOUT it); `exclude_ids` drop on `merged_worklist`/`next_merged`. No gate weakened; no marker/schema change. Bug spec (Step 2.5, committed `harden(docs): 7448eb1c` BEFORE the fix): `docs/bugs/_archive/merged-head-includes-parked-items-deadlocks-park-run/` (Concluded). Commit: `a8140ff8`.

**Over-fit spin-off:** none — the fix is STRUCTURAL (a new shared park predicate + resolver + an `exclude_ids` filter param threaded through the ordering plane), NOT a literal phrase added to a matcher (signal 1 N/A). `harness-gate.py --range 3b07fc63..HEAD --json`: `gate_weakening_hit: false`, `gate_weakening: pass`; `overfit: flag` fired ONLY on `alternation literal appended` evidence that is Python TYPE-UNION annotations (`exclude_ids: "set[str] | frozenset[str] | None"` — the `|` misread as a regex alternation) + `literal element appended to a membership construct` evidence that is test-fixture list literals and `"""` docstring delimiters — none is a behavior-gating MATCHER, so signal 1 does NOT apply (same false-positive class as Rounds 53/55). Class recurrence: this is the FIRST fix of the parked-exclusion-from-merged-head class; Round 54 introduced `merged_head_override` (a DIFFERENT class — routing bypass), so the ≥2 non-phrase threshold is unmet. Near-neighbors covered: the exclusion is applied at the single ordering source consumed by all three surfaces (`--next-merged`, feature `--emit-prompt`, bug `--emit-prompt`). No spin-off warranted.

**Intervention record:** `docs/interventions/harden-2026-07-r56.md` — CAPTURED. Target signal `event:halt`, expected-direction `decrease` (baseline frozen): the friction's own recurrence is a park-mode run reaching a no-item-dispatchable dead end (surfaced as a halt/exhaustion terminal) because every emit probe withheld behind a parked merged head — with parked items excluded from the merged head, those spurious park-mode deadlock halts should fall. Signal independence: independent (halt/exhaustion terminals are emitted by the state machine's terminal detection, not by the merged-head exclusion this fix touches).

## Round 57 — 2026-07-17 — observed-friction

**Item in flight:** adhoc-incident-hook-deny-a51dde
**Divergence point:** the merged-head exclusion set (`lazy_core.depdag.parked_item_ids` built from `docmodel.spec_dir_would_park`, threaded as `exclude_ids` through `merged_worklist`/`next_merged`/`dispatch.merged_head_override` + both `--emit-prompt` `merged-head-diverged` withholds + the `--next-merged` CLI) — landed by Round 56 — excludes only PARK-flag-gated items and NOT operator-deferred items, so an operator-deferred item remains at the merged head and the Round-54 withhold re-blocks the actionable route (same deadlock class as Round 56, different non-actionable STATE).

**Root cause:** `script-defect` — `parked_item_ids`/`spec_dir_would_park` (`depdag.py`/`docmodel.py`) model ONLY the two PARK families (`BLOCKED.md` under `--park-blocked`, unresolved `NEEDS_INPUT.md` under `--park-needs-input`), and `parked_item_ids` even fast-paths to an empty set when no park flag is set. But `compute_state` in `bug-state.py` (~L1073) skips an operator-deferred bug (`DEFERRED.md`) with a bare `continue` **UNCONDITIONALLY** — no park flag required — so such a bug is NEVER the dispatched item, yet Round 56's exclusion does not drop it. LIVE EVIDENCE (2026-07-17, immediately after Round 56's `a8140ff8` landed, `--park` active): `--next-merged` returned `non-windows-audio-output-unvalidated`; scoping it (`bug-state.py --bug-id non-windows-audio-output-unvalidated --emit-prompt`) returned `terminal_reason=operator-deferred`, `current_step "Operator-deferred (scoped)"`, `sub_skill=null` (NOT dispatchable — needs a non-Windows host); the actionable `adhoc-incident-hook-deny-a51dde` (spec-bug, Step 4) routes unscoped but its `--emit-prompt` WITHHELD (`route_overridden_by=merged-head-diverged`, `cycle_model`/`cycle_prompt_ref` null, `merged_head=non-windows-audio-output-unvalidated`) → still DEADLOCKED, now behind an operator-deferred head instead of a parked one. This is precisely the "later round may widen the boundary" case Round 56's own §Fix-scope class-boundary anticipated.

**Action:**
  - Mechanical fix applied: generalize the Round-56 mechanism from "parked" to "not dispatchable", covering the UNCONDITIONAL operator-defer. (a) `lazy_core/docmodel.py` — new pure, fail-safe `spec_dir_operator_deferred(spec_dir)` (True iff `DEFERRED.md` present; mirrors compute_state's bug-pipeline operator-defer `continue`; kept SEPARATE from `spec_dir_would_park` because it is NOT park-flag-gated). (b) `lazy_core/depdag.py` — `parked_item_ids` → `nondispatchable_item_ids`: drops the no-park-facet fast-path (operator-defer is unconditional) and excludes an item when EITHER `spec_dir_operator_deferred` OR `spec_dir_would_park` holds. (c) callers `lazy-state.py` (`--next-merged` + `--emit-prompt`) and `bug-state.py` (`--emit-prompt`, coupled pair) renamed through; `__init__` registry updated. No park facet AND no `DEFERRED.md` → empty set → BYTE-IDENTICAL. Regression fixtures (`test_dispatch.py`, +3 net, `_TESTS`-registered; the Round-56 resolver test renamed to match): the operator-defer predicate; fixture (a) top operator-deferred bug + lower actionable, NO park flag → `--next-merged` returns the actionable bug, `merged_head_override` returns `None` WITH the exclusion but the old operator-deferred head WITHOUT it (deadlock reproduced + fixed); fixture (c) mixed parked + operator-deferred + actionable → head is the actionable one. No gate weakened; no marker/schema change. Bug spec (Step 2.5, committed `harden(docs): 95f40ca0` BEFORE the fix): `docs/bugs/_archive/merged-head-excludes-parked-not-operator-deferred-deadlocks/` (Concluded). Commit: `84e656ec`.

**Over-fit spin-off:** harden(spinoff): literal-phrase-to-matcher (signal 1 — the fix appends the `DEFERRED.md` sentinel literal to a file-existence matcher) + class recurred ≥2 (signal 2 — this is the SECOND fix of the merged-head-exclusion class after Round 56's parked exclusion, same `depdag`/`docmodel` exclusion set) + agent self-flag (signal 3 — the context-conditional deferrals + non-file terminal_reasons will gap on the same file-predicate structure). Fixture (b) host-deferred from the dispatch evidence belongs to the spin-off (host-context the file predicate cannot see). NOTE: the `--enqueue-adhoc` was DENIED mid-cycle by the active-cycle guard (a subagent may not perform `lazy-state.py` routing/queue mutations in-flight — working as intended); the enqueue is therefore ORCHESTRATOR-OWNED at the cycle boundary. PushNotification sent with the item id + brief.

## Round 58 — 2026-07-17 — manual

**Item in flight:** operator-recovery-of-crashed-run-orphaned-markers (GAP 1 of a batched 2-gap manual harden)
**Divergence point:** operator teardown of a CRASHED `/lazy-batch` run's orphaned markers (`lazy-run-marker.json` + `lazy-cycle-active.json`) from a fresh, later session — the containment C3 guards + the `--run-end` gate cascade refuse it as a "single cycle subagent" with no chain-aware recovery guidance.

**Root cause:** `script-defect` + `missing-contract` — `refuse_if_cycle_active` (`user/scripts/lazy_core/markers.py:2171`) and `refuse_cycle_marker_mutation_if_subagent` (`markers.py:2233`) decide subagent-vs-orchestrator on cycle-marker PRESENCE + the `LAZY_ORCHESTRATOR`/`LAZY_CYCLE_SUBAGENT` env signals ONLY; neither reads the marker's recorded `session_id`/`started_at` (`write_cycle_marker`, `markers.py:1486-1513`) nor probes process liveness. The dead run's `session_id` was foreign to the operator and its parent PIDs were gone, but a foreign+dead owner reads identically to a live subagent. The harness's own non-destructive ownership detect (`marker_owner_status`, `markers.py:1022`) + `read_run_marker` staleness paths are not applied here (path A age>24h does not fire on a fresh crash; `read_cycle_marker` has NO staleness logic). Once containment is bypassed via `LAZY_ORCHESTRATOR=1`, the `--run-end` handler (`lazy-state.py:12613`) layers pending-hardening + efficacy-flush + terminal-reason gates, and `SANCTIONED_STOP_TERMINAL` (`markers.py:650`) has no crash/disconnect reason — forcing `--operator-authorized` + a borrowed sanctioned reason.

**Action:**
  - NEEDS_INPUT.md written: `docs/specs/turn-routing-enforcement/NEEDS_INPUT.md` decision #12. Decisions: session-liveness/ownership teardown path (changes the deny decision — authority) vs. a first-class `--recover-stale-marker`/`--force-run-end` op (new authority surface) vs. chain-aware refusal messages only (minimum) — plus whether to add a `crashed-run`/`remote-control-disconnect` sanctioned terminal reason (gate-semantics: ends a run without `--operator-authorized`). Every candidate grants authority or changes gate semantics → operator-owned; a message-only fix would enshrine whichever recovery UX is NOT chosen, so it is surfaced not baked. Bug spec (Step 2.5, committed `harden(docs):` BEFORE this round): `docs/bugs/operator-recovery-of-crashed-run-orphaned-markers-underserved/SPEC.md` (Concluded).

**Over-fit spin-off:** none — this is a NEEDS_INPUT design-fork round; nothing mechanical shipped, so no matcher/phrase fix exists to over-fit and no spin-off applies.

## Round 60 — 2026-07-17 — manual

**Item in flight:** operator-recovery-of-crashed-run-orphaned-markers (decision #12; park-provisional finish of the Round-58 park)
**Divergence point:** operator teardown of a CRASHED `/lazy-batch` run's orphaned markers from a fresh later session — the containment C3 guards (`refuse_if_cycle_active` `markers.py:2171` / `refuse_cycle_marker_mutation_if_subagent` `markers.py:2233`) + the `--run-end` gate cascade refuse it as a "single cycle subagent" with no chain-aware recovery.

Decisions: session-liveness/ownership teardown path + crashed-run terminal reason (recommended) vs. a first-class `--recover-stale-marker`/`--force-run-end` op vs. chain-aware refusal messages. Assessed under park-provisional and DELIBERATELY not implemented: the recommended option (a)+crash-terminal-reason SOFTENS the containment deny (a foreign+dead-owner teardown that is currently refused) and lets a run END WITHOUT `--operator-authorized` (both Prohibition #2 gate-weakening), and the whole decision is `divergence: structural` (authority-model fork; the cross-platform "provably dead" liveness definition is the expensive-to-redirect wrong-pick). A purely-additive `--recover-stale-marker` gated on `--operator-authorized` would be provisional-eligible in isolation but does not resolve the recommended fix and would pre-empt the operator's authority-model choice. Bug spec (Step 2.5, committed BEFORE this round): `docs/bugs/operator-recovery-of-crashed-run-orphaned-markers-underserved/SPEC.md` (Concluded).

## Round 62 — 2026-07-17 — observed-friction

**Item in flight:** adhoc-hydra-sidecar-dist-esm-no-frames
**Divergence point:** the bug-pipeline archive step (`bug-state.py --repo-root . --archive-fixed docs/bugs/<id>`, wiring `bug-state.py:8883-8889`) — the deterministic script-owned `__mark_fixed__ → --archive-fixed` mover died with an uncaught `ValueError` instead of archiving or refusing; the run fell back to a hand-passed absolute-paths workaround. Background/non-blocking observed-friction; no probe/registry state.

**Root cause:** `script-defect` in `lazy_core/gates.py::archive_fixed`. `repo_root` is resolved to absolute (`gates.py:1973`) but `spec_path` was used un-normalized (passed straight through as `Path(args.archive_fixed)`, `bug-state.py:8884-8885`). The per-file `git mv` fallback then computes `spec_path.relative_to(repo_root)` (`gates.py:2104`); a RELATIVE `spec_path` (`docs/bugs/<id>`) against an ABSOLUTE `repo_root` makes `Path.relative_to` raise `ValueError`, and the sole `try/except` catches only `(OSError, subprocess.SubprocessError)` (`gates.py:2213`) — so it is UNCAUGHT and kills `--archive-fixed` with a raw traceback rather than the structured `{"refused": …}` shape. Sibling gates (`verify_ledger` gates.py:1253 drives git via `git -C <repo_root>` and reads `spec_path` directly; `apply_pseudo`) never mix a relative `spec_path` with an absolute `repo_root` in a `relative_to()` call, so they accept a relative `spec_path` fine — hence the archive-fixed-specific surprise. Step-2.5 investigation spec: `docs/bugs/_archive/archive-fixed-relative-spec-path-valueerror/SPEC.md` (Status: Concluded), committed FIRST at `695793ff` (audit trail predates the fix).

**Action:**
  - Mechanical fix applied: anchor `spec_path` at `repo_root` immediately after `repo_root = repo_root.resolve()` (`spec_path.resolve()` if absolute, else `(repo_root / spec_path).resolve()`), so every downstream `spec_path.relative_to(repo_root)` is well-defined for both relative and absolute callers. Anchoring a relative `spec_path` at `repo_root` (not CWD) is the correct interpretation — `git ls-files` output downstream is likewise repo-relative. No gate/refusal/provenance semantics change (not gate-weakening). Regression test `test_archive_fixed_accepts_relative_spec_path` (registered in `_TESTS`) drives `archive_fixed` with a repo-relative `spec_path` and asserts a clean archive; verified RED before the fix (refused "spec_path does not exist … nothing to archive" because the un-anchored relative path resolves against CWD) / GREEN after. Gates run: test_lazy_core 1192/1192, test_hooks 238/238, lint-skills OK, lazy-state/bug-state --test OK. Commit + push: `e7d9361a`.

**Over-fit spin-off:** none — the production fix is STRUCTURAL (adds absolute-path anchoring of `spec_path`; no literal appended to any matcher/alternation/keyword-set/allow-list — signal 1 N/A) and the class has not recurred on this component (grep of both months: the path-normalization THEME appears only as `_is_noninvalidating_drift_path` separator-normalized *drift-path classification* — a different mechanism/symbol; the same-class-AND-same-component ≥2 bar for signals 2 is unmet; this is the first `archive_fixed` un-normalized-`spec_path` instance). Signals 3/4 unmet (uniform normalization, no near-neighbor gap; no repeated dance). `harness-gate.py --range origin/main..HEAD --json`: `gate_weakening: pass`, `tautology: pass`, `overfit: flag`, `scope_hit: [user/scripts/lazy_core/gates.py]`, `verdict_required: true`. The `overfit: flag` cites only TEST-FIXTURE literals (`docs/bugs/my-bug`, `2026-06-10`) — the pre-existing shared `_make_fixed_bug_repo` bug id + date reused verbatim by all six sibling `archive_fixed` tests, in the test file, NOT a production matcher append; the same checker-artifact class Rounds 35-38 documented. `retires:` = net-new (adds `spec_path` normalization + a regression test; retires no rule — the un-normalized `spec_path` was a defect, not a rule).

**Secondary observation (scoped OUT — relayed):** the reporter also noted `lazy-state.py` probe `live_settings_ok=false` for AlgoBooth ("tracked user/settings.json is missing/unreadable at <repo>/user/settings.json"). Mechanism: `lazy-state.py::live_settings_probe` (`lazy-state.py:11392`) feeds the TARGET `repo_root` into `doc-drift-lint.live_settings_status`, which reads `repo_root/user/settings.json` (`doc-drift-lint.py:560-572`) — but the tracked-settings SSOT lives in claude-config, not an arbitrary target repo, so for any non-claude-config target this resolves the wrong path and reports a non-benign `False`. A DISTINCT defect (probe semantics) carrying a small design choice (resolve against claude-config vs benign-skip when the target has no tracked `user/settings.json`); deliberately NOT bundled into this round to keep the primary fix clean, captured in the bug SPEC's "Related observation" section and relayed as a follow-up candidate.

**Gates run:**

  test_hooks.py: 238/238
  lint-skills.py --check-projected --check-capabilities: OK
  lazy-state.py --test: OK

## Round 63 — 2026-07-17 — manual

**Item in flight:** feature-tier-strings-fall-to-merged-priority-default (operator-directed harness enhancement, Jacob 2026-07-17)
**Divergence point:** the feature axis of `lazy_core.merged_priority` (`depdag.py`) — the `tier` normalizer accepted only a bare int or a numeric string, so every intent-carrying feature-tier STRING (`milestone`/`commercialization`/`major-initiative`/`follow-up`/`non-audio`/`4a`/`4b`) failed `int()` parse and fell through to `MERGED_PRIORITY_DEFAULT = 99`, sorting real features dead-last — byte-identical to a feature with no tier at all. Manual invocation; no probe/registry/deny-ledger state.

**Root cause:** `missing-contract` — the feature axis of the unified priority scale was only ever specified for integer tiers. There was no named-enum vocabulary for feature tiers parallel to the bug side's `_MERGED_SEVERITY_RANK = {P0:0,P1:1,P2:2,Low:3}` (`depdag.py:753`). A feature author who wrote an intent-carrying tier name (the natural thing) silently got the WORST priority — an invisible false-deprioritization. Step-2.5 investigation spec: `docs/bugs/_archive/feature-tier-strings-fall-to-merged-priority-default/SPEC.md` (Status: Concluded), committed FIRST at `d456f30e` (audit trail predates the fix).

**Action:**
  - Provisional design-fork resolved: implemented the recommended legacy-string→int mapping for the one product decision (the seven legacy tier values). Feature tiers become named enums (`_FEATURE_TIER_ENUM` in `depdag.py`) mapping onto the SAME integer scale as bug severity (lower = higher priority), so a feature and a bug are directly comparable. `pre-release=1` is operator-LOCKED (== P1) — load-bearing ordering `merged_priority(P0 bug)=0 < pre-release feature=1 < P2 bug=2`. A `tier` may be a single enum name, a bare int / numeric string (backward-compat, passed through), OR a LIST of those — a multi-enum feature whose effective priority is the MIN of the resolved values. Backward compat is byte-identical for bare ints, bug severity, and null/missing (only the previously-`99` legacy STRINGS change — the whole point). `--set-tier` accepts enum names (single or comma-separated), validating against the enum vocabulary; the queue-doc badge renders enum/list tiers with their effective priority (bare ints keep the historic `T<n>`). Regenerated `docs/cli/cli-surface.json` for the `--set-tier` help change (this ALSO cleared a pre-existing `--park`-flag registry staleness unrelated to this round). Regression tests (all `_TESTS`-registered / pytest-fixture): `test_merged_priority_feature_tier_enum_to_int` (enum→int + backward-compat shapes), `test_merged_priority_feature_multi_enum_takes_min` (list MIN, mixed/unresolvable elements), `test_merged_priority_prerelease_ordering_p0_before_prerelease_before_p2` (the load-bearing `0 < 1 < 2` assertion through both the scalar fn and the merged worklist), `test_set_queue_priority_feature_accepts_tier_enum` (mutator accepts enum name + comma-separated list), and the unknown-enum zero-mutation refusal. Gates run: test_lazy_core (pytest package) 1196/1196, test_hooks 248/248, lint-skills OK, lazy-state/bug-state --test OK. Commit + push: `c089142a`. Provisional sentinel: `docs/bugs/_archive/feature-tier-strings-fall-to-merged-priority-default/NEEDS_INPUT_PROVISIONAL.md` (decision_commit: `c089142ab860ed32a2938e86b3aaf24316358834`). The seven legacy-string integer VALUES are the sole provisional element (Jacob explicitly asked to own this product decision, harden req 4); `pre-release=1`, backward compat, the MIN selection, and the tests are locked, NOT provisional. Divergence graded `contained` — a wrong pick is a one-constant redirect (`_FEATURE_TIER_ENUM`) plus a deterministic `reposition_by_priority` re-sort; no persistent-data or architecture fork, so provisional-implement (not a hard-park carve-out).

**Over-fit spin-off:** none — the production change is STRUCTURAL: it ADDS the missing named-enum contract (`_FEATURE_TIER_ENUM`, parallel to `_MERGED_SEVERITY_RANK`) with a general resolver (`_resolve_feature_tier_element`) whose int / numeric-string / unknown→DEFAULT fallbacks handle ANY future value, not a literal fitted to an observed matcher. The seven legacy strings are a CLOSED enumerated vocabulary (all known legacy tier strings), and an unknown string falls to DEFAULT (explicit, tested) — no near-neighbor gap (signal 1 N/A on production). Class has not recurred (first unification of the feature tier axis; signals 2–4 unmet). `harness-gate.py --range origin/main..HEAD --json`: `gate_weakening: pass`, `tautology: pass`, `overfit: flag`, `gate_weakening_hit: false`, `scope_hit: [lazy-state.py, lazy_core/__init__.py, lazy_core/depdag.py]`. The `overfit: flag` evidence is entirely TEST-FIXTURE docstrings + the `user/scripts/CLAUDE.md` human-readable enum-list literal (`major-initiative/follow-up/non-audio/4a/4b`) + the `_resolve_feature_tier_element` def line — NONE is a production matcher/regex/allow-list append; the same checker-artifact class (doc/fixture literals, not production membership constructs) prior rounds documented. No spin-off warranted.

**Intervention record:** `docs/interventions/harden-2026-07-r63.md` (`pipeline: hardening`, `target_signal: undeclared` — a proactive operator-directed enhancement; no ledger event tracks silent feature mis-prioritization, so the recurrence signal is honestly `not-computable`, INCONCLUSIVE-by-construction).

**Gates run:**
  test_lazy_core (pytest package): 1196/1196
  test_hooks.py: 248/248
  lint-skills.py --check-projected --check-capabilities: OK
  lazy-state.py --test: OK

## Round 64 — 2026-07-17 — manual

**Item in flight:** merged-head-diverged-stalls-on-gated-head (operator-directed, Jacob 2026-07-17 — the merged-driver stall observed live during a `/lazy-batch` run on AlgoBooth)
**Divergence point:** the `--emit-prompt` merged-head divergence check in `lazy-state.py` / `bug-state.py` (`merged_head_override`). Its exclude set came ONLY from `lazy_core.nondispatchable_item_ids` (the NARROW file predicate: park families + operator-defer), while the per-pipeline skip-ahead in `compute_state` is BROADER (default-on: research-pending / BLOCKED gated heads, host/device-deferred, dep-gated). A gated head that the probe correctly SKIPPED therefore diverged from the workable item the probe dispatched, and `merged_head_override` WITHHELD the forward route (`route_overridden_by: merged-head-diverged`, null `cycle_prompt`) — stalling the driver behind an item it will never dispatch. Observed live 2026-07-17: `cross-platform-distribution`, a BLOCKED external-gate pre-release feature (`blocker_kind: external-gate`) Jacob had just pinned at tier `pre-release` (priority 1), sat at the merged head; the probe skip-advanced to `hydra-overlay` but the driver stalled on the divergence (the only mid-run escape was manually demoting the tier). Manual invocation; no probe/registry/deny-ledger state.

**Root cause:** `script-defect` — the merged-head exclude set is a NARROWER predicate than the per-pipeline skip-ahead it must agree with (`nondispatchable_item_ids`, `depdag.py`, only covers the flag-gated park families + unconditional operator-defer; it explicitly scoped OUT the context-conditional deferrals + gated heads). This is precisely the "make the merged head fully actionability-aware" generalization spun off by `merged-head-excludes-parked-not-operator-deferred-deadlocks` (over-fit signal 1 of that round: it added another sentinel-filename literal to the file matcher; the near-neighbor gated heads gap on the same structure). Step-2.5 investigation spec: `docs/bugs/_archive/merged-head-diverged-stalls-on-gated-head/SPEC.md` (Status: Concluded), committed FIRST at `b6b16642` (audit trail predates the fix).

**Action:**
  - Mechanical fix applied: new pure helper `lazy_core.dispatch.probe_skipped_ids(state, items)` folds the per-pipeline probe's OWN same-cycle skip lists — `gated_heads` / `host_deferred_features` (id-keyed) / `dep_gated` (id-keyed) / `device_deferred_features` (name→id resolved via the loaded items); bug side: `device_deferred_features` + `operator_deferred` — into one id set, unioned into the exclude set feeding `merged_head_override` in both `lazy-state.py --emit-prompt` and `bug-state.py --emit-prompt` (coupled-pair mirrored; the current `feature_id` is defensively discarded). Reusing the probe's OWN realized skips (not a second scoped re-probe) keeps the merged head in EXACT parity with skip-ahead: it honors `--strict-research-halt` (under it `gated_heads` is empty → the gated head is NOT excluded → the run halts on it, opt-in preserved), the two-key skip-ahead predicate, and the fully-gated terminal (no skip-ahead-ready alternative → the probe clears `gated_heads` and dispatches the gated head as its blocked/needs-research terminal → the set is empty → the merged head equals that terminal head — the existing terminal, NOT an infinite skip). A skipped item is by definition never the dispatched item, so the current dispatch target is never excluded (loop-free). The `merged-head-diverged` withhold now fires ONLY for a genuine dispatchable-item divergence (a P0 bug jumping the queue). `--next-merged` stays PURE (its documented pure-ordering / no-per-item-state-inference contract is intact); the `--emit-prompt` override is the authoritative skip gate, and a gated head returned by `--next-merged` is harmless (correct-type dispatch → the override emits the workable item / redirects across type). Non-withholding observability diagnostic added; the skip also stays visible in the existing `gated_heads` / `*_deferred_features` / `dep_gated` probe keys. Regression tests (all `_TESTS`-registered): `test_probe_skipped_ids_collects_all_skip_lists_and_resolves_names` (id + name-keyed lists, empty common path), `test_merged_head_override_gated_head_excluded_no_false_withhold` (no false withhold with a gated head excluded, yet still withholds for a dispatchable P0 bug), and three end-to-end subprocess `--emit-prompt` tests — `test_subprocess_emit_prompt_skips_blocked_gated_head_no_withhold` (BLOCKED gated head skipped → workable feature dispatched, no withhold, gated head still observable), `test_subprocess_emit_prompt_fully_gated_surfaces_blocked_terminal` (fully-gated → blocked terminal, no infinite skip), `test_subprocess_emit_prompt_single_type_workable_head_unchanged` (byte-identical common path). Gates run: test_lazy_core (pytest package) 1201/1201, test_hooks.py 248/248, lint-skills.py OK, lazy-state.py/bug-state.py --test OK, lazy_parity_audit.py --report + --merged-view exit 0. Commit + push: `3add529d`.

**Over-fit spin-off:** none — the fix is STRUCTURAL: it reuses the per-pipeline probe's OWN surfaced skip decisions (`gated_heads` / `*_deferred_features` / `dep_gated`) rather than adding a literal (e.g. "blocked") to a matcher, and it IS the durable "fully actionability-aware merged head" generalization the merged-head-exclusion class was ALREADY spun off toward by `merged-head-excludes-parked-not-operator-deferred-deadlocks` — this round CLOSES that class for the task's scope (the file-predicate narrowness is now subsumed by the probe's own skip signal), it does not add another whack-a-mole instance. `harness-gate.py --range origin/main..HEAD --json`: `gate_weakening: pass`, `gate_weakening_hit: false`, `tautology: pass`, `overfit: flag`, `scope_hit: [bug-state.py, lazy-state.py, lazy_core/dispatch.py]`. The `overfit: flag` evidence is entirely the observability-diagnostic string literals (`.append(_diag_line)` content), the new `probe_skipped_ids` `def`/docstring line, and test-fixture literals — NONE is a production matcher/regex/allow-list phrase append; the same checker-artifact class (diagnostic/docstring/fixture literals, not production membership constructs) that Rounds 62–63 documented. Class boundary drawn tightly: budget-guard eviction (marker-plumbed `budget_evicted`, NOT surfaced in the state dict, and outside the task's named scope of research/blocked/host/device) is a deliberately OUT-of-class further neighbor — no evidence it has stalled the driver; a later round widens if it ever does. No spin-off warranted.

**Intervention record:** `docs/interventions/harden-2026-07-r64.md` (`pipeline: hardening`, `target_signal: event:halt` — the merged-driver stall manifests as a driver halt/no-forward-progress; the intervention's expected effect is a decrease in such halts).

**Gates run:**
  test_lazy_core (pytest package): 1201/1201
  test_hooks.py: 248/248
  lint-skills.py --check-projected --check-capabilities: OK
  lazy-state.py --test: OK

## Round 65 — 2026-07-17 — manual

**Item in flight:** research-gated-head-buried-by-skip-ahead-and-merged-fallthrough (operator-observed live during a `/lazy-batch` run on AlgoBooth, 2026-07-17)
**Divergence point:** the `--emit-prompt` merged-head exclude computation (`lazy-state.py` merged-override block + `lazy_core.dispatch.probe_skipped_ids`). Round 64's `probe_skipped_ids` folds ALL `gated_heads` — research-pending AND BLOCKED — into the merged-head exclude set. So when a skip past a research-pending head is REALIZED (an independent lower-priority alternative / a cross-type bug exists), the research head is excluded from the merged view and the driver falls through to the lower-priority item, surfacing NO needs-research halt. Two pre-release (P1) research-gated features (`inspector-sample-clip-view`, `inspector-track-dashboard`) were buried behind a lower-priority bug; the operator never saw the research prompt.

**Root cause:** `script-defect` — research-gating is treated identically to BLOCKED-gating in the DEFAULT skip-ahead / merged-fallthrough path. They are not equivalent: a BLOCKED head (external gate / host) is not operator-resolvable in-session, so skip-ahead to independent ready work is reasonable; a research gap is operator-resolvable in seconds (Gemini upload), so burying it defeats the needs-research halt's purpose. The single-gated-head / no-alternative case already worked (`gated_head_fallback` dispatches the head to its Step-5 terminal); the defect is the realized-skip case. Step-2.5 investigation spec: `docs/bugs/_archive/research-gated-head-buried-by-skip-ahead-and-merged-fallthrough/SPEC.md` (Status: Concluded), committed FIRST in the specs commit (audit trail predates the fix).

**Action:**
  - Provisional design-fork resolved: implemented the recommended precedence rule for the two routing-precedence decisions. `compute_state` classifies gated heads by kind (`_gated_head_kind` -> research | blocked | None; research-first when both present, per the Step-1h research-blocked carve-out) and surfaces the research subset as a new `research_gated_heads` probe key (mirrors `gated_heads`; absent when empty; cleared in the `gated_head_fallback` path). New pure helper `lazy_core.dispatch.research_halt_head` re-includes ONLY the research skips into the merged head; when a research head is the research-inclusive merged head (strictly ahead in the FULL merged ordering incl. the type tie-break) it outranks the fallthrough -> the `--emit-prompt` path re-emits as that head's SCOPED needs-research terminal (a `compute_state(scope_feature_id=<head>, strict_research_halt=True)` re-run, adopted only if it yields `terminal_reason=needs-research`; `route_overridden_by: research-gated-head`), which the driver's existing Step-4 halt surfaces — loop-free. A lower-priority research head is NOT surfaced (no over-halt). Feature-pipeline only (bug pipeline has no research gate — documented parity in `bug-state.py`, mirroring the `strict_research_halt` asymmetry). Coupled trio prose + parity audit reconciled. Regression tests (all `_TESTS`-registered): `test_research_halt_head_surfaces_when_research_head_outranks_bug`, `test_research_halt_head_none_when_ready_work_outranks_research_head` (no over-halt + BLOCKED-not-surfaced + no-research common path), and end-to-end `test_subprocess_emit_prompt_surfaces_needs_research_over_lower_bug`. Gates run: pytest package 1205/1205, test_hooks 238/238, lint-skills OK, lazy-state/bug-state --test OK, parity --report + --merged-view exit 0. Commit + push: `adb80ec7` (code) + `b8387cbe` (tie-break gate-test name retention). ## Round 66 — 2026-07-17 — manual (operator-directed)

**Item in flight:** non-p0-bug-outranks-p1-feature-on-aged-tie (operator directive, Jacob 2026-07-17: "I only want P0 bugs to sort ahead of P1 features")
**Divergence point:** the equal-rank tie-break in `lazy_core.merged_worklist` / `next_merged` (`depdag.py`). `_MERGED_TYPE_ORDER = {"bug": 0, "feature": 1}` made a bug win an equal effective rank. A P2 bug (`protocol-generic-claims-drift`, `**Discovered:** 2026-07-09`) age-escalated to rank 1 (`age_escalated_rank(2, ...)`, floor `_AGE_ESCALATION_FLOOR_RANK = 1`), tying the P1 (pre-release) feature `hydra-overlay` — and the bug-before-feature tie-break made `--next-merged` return the P2 bug over the P1 feature.

**Root cause:** `missing-contract` — the tie-break policy (bug-before-feature) predates both the aging feature and the operator's "only P0 ahead of P1" rule. Because the age floor is rank 1 (no aged bug reaches rank 0), the ONLY way a non-P0 bug precedes a P1 feature is the equal-rank tie-break resolving for the bug. Step-2.5 investigation spec: `docs/bugs/_archive/non-p0-bug-outranks-p1-feature-on-aged-tie/SPEC.md` (Status: Concluded), committed FIRST in the specs commit.

**Action:**
  - Mechanical fix applied (operator-directed — the design fork is resolved by the verbatim directive, so no provisional sentinel): flipped `_MERGED_TYPE_ORDER` to `{"feature": 0, "bug": 1}` (feature wins ties). With the rank-1 age floor this yields EXACTLY the directive: P0 bug (rank 0) < P1 feature (rank 1) -> bug wins (P0 ahead of P1); any equal-rank bug/feature -> feature wins (only P0 ahead of P1). Scalar `merged_priority` values unchanged (the Round-63 load-bearing statement holds for the scalar); only the equal-rank tie-break flips. Reconciled the load-bearing comment block, the `merged_worklist` docstring + seed-order comment, `lazy_parity_audit.py`'s "bugs break ties" comment, both scripts' `--next-merged` prose, and the SKILL trio's four "breaks ties bug-before-feature" statements. Regression tests: `test_merged_worklist_bug_breaks_tie_at_equal_priority` (gate-test NAME retained across the flip — assertion corrected to feature-before-bug + P0-still-ahead leg; docstring documents the inversion so no gate-test def is removed) and new `test_merged_worklist_aged_p2_bug_sorts_behind_p1_feature` (the exact live scenario: aged-P2->rank-1 bug sorts behind the P1 feature; a genuine P0 still precedes it). Updated `test_merged_worklist_stable_within_queue_for_equal_keys` + the test_misc "bug-breaks-tie" fixture wording to the new invariant. Gates run: pytest package 1205/1205, test_hooks 238/238, lint-skills OK, lazy-state/bug-state --test OK, parity --report + --merged-view exit 0. Commit + push: `adb80ec7` (shared with Round 65's code commit) + `b8387cbe` (gate-test name retention).

**Over-fit spin-off:** none — a single-constant tie-break flip is the least-collateral faithful implementation of the directive (a narrower P1-only guard would be an over-fit literal; lowering the age floor alone would NOT fix a genuine P1 bug tying a P1 feature). Class has not recurred. `harness-gate` on my isolated range (`115a991a..b8387cbe`): `gate_weakening_hit: false`. No spin-off warranted.

**Intervention record:** `docs/interventions/harden-2026-07-r66.md` (`pipeline: hardening`, `target_signal: undeclared` — an operator-directed ordering enhancement; no closed ledger-event tracks the merged-ordering invariant, so the recurrence signal is honestly `not-computable` / INCONCLUSIVE-by-construction, exactly as Round 63's tier unification. The precise countable — a non-P0 bug never precedes a P1 feature — is MECHANICALLY enforced by the regression test, the durable guarantee).

## Round 67 — 2026-07-17 — manual (operator-directed)

**Item in flight:** cycle-budget-counters-double-count-on-probes-and-inject-hook (operator directive, Jacob 2026-07-17: offload cycle-counting to the SCRIPT; a cycle counts only on a real dispatch, decoupled from probes)
**Divergence point:** `lazy_core.advance_forward_cycle(state, consume_gate=True)` on the `--repeat-count` probe path (`lazy-state.py` ~13685, `bug-state.py` ~9336). It advances on a `(feature_id, current_step, sub_skill)` state-change OR a consume rise, so ANY probe caller — an inspection probe, the dispatch-bound probe, AND the per-turn inject-hook probe — inflates `forward_cycles` with no dispatch (live: three discovery probes drove forward 0->3; a per-turn inject-hook probe bumped forward 1->2 on a non-dispatch turn). `meta_cycles` was advanced separately at `--emit-dispatch`.

**Root cause:** `script-defect` — budget counting is a side effect of the PROBE / `update_repeat_counts` path instead of a real dispatch event the script observes. The `--cycle-begin`/`--cycle-end` bracket already wraps exactly one Agent dispatch and carries `--kind real|meta` — the correct increment anchor. Step-2.5 investigation spec: `docs/bugs/_archive/cycle-budget-counters-double-count-on-probes-and-inject-hook/SPEC.md` (Status: Concluded), committed FIRST at `0584c07f`. Implemented by a dispatched general-purpose subagent under the design in that spec; verified independently by this stage (harness-gate + targeted regression run).

**Action:**
  - Mechanical fix applied: new marker helper `lazy_core.markers.advance_cycle_bracket_counter(cycle_marker)` (marker-gated; `kind == real` -> `forward_cycles` + the sibling `_bump_per_feature_forward`; `kind == meta` -> `meta_cycles`; atomic-writes the run marker), registered in `lazy_core/__init__.py` and called from BOTH `--cycle-end` handlers after reading + before clearing the cycle marker (idempotent per bracket). REMOVED the probe-path `advance_forward_cycle(state, consume_gate=True)` (lazy-state ~13685, bug-state ~9336) and the `--emit-dispatch` `advance_meta_cycle()` (lazy-state ~13038; bug-state had none) — meta dispatches are bracketed `--kind meta`, so `--cycle-end` now counts them (counting at emit would double-count). `--apply-pseudo`'s forward/cleanup increment is UNCHANGED (pseudos dispatch no Agent, are not bracketed). `update_repeat_counts` (streaks) untouched. Net: inspection + inject-hook probes are budget-neutral; a real bracket counts exactly once; forward stays capped at `max_cycles`, meta uncapped. Coupled trio prose reconciled (~10 spots). Regression tests (5 new in `test_markers.py`, `_TESTS`-registered): inspection-probe budget-neutral (a), inject-hook non-dispatch-turn budget-neutral (b), real bracket -> forward+1 + per-feature (c), meta bracket -> meta+1 & cleanup pseudo -> meta (d), forward pseudo -> forward+1 (e); plus 2 repurposed `test_statedir.py` tests (def names + gate identity retained; bodies assert the new bracket-coupled contract — no coverage dropped). Gates run: pytest package 1210/1210, test_hooks 238/238, lint-skills OK, lazy-state/bug-state --test OK, parity --report + --merged-view exit 0. Commit + push: `e91bd305` (script) + `9819702f` (test) + `306a6714` (prose).
  - Honest design note (documented in all three SKILLs, no scope change): `__flip_plan_complete_stale__` is applied INLINE (not a `--apply-pseudo` name, not bracketed), so with the probe-path advance removed the script no longer counts its meta cycle. Budget-neutral by the SPEC's own Safety argument (`meta_cycles` is uncapped, display-only) — a meta under-count never affects the `forward_cycles >= max_cycles` halt. Not a NEEDS_INPUT (within the SPEC's stated safety envelope).

**Over-fit spin-off:** none — the fix RELOCATES counting to a structural dispatch event (the cycle bracket), it does not add a literal to a matcher. `harness-gate.py --range e91bd305^..306a6714 --json`: `gate_weakening_hit: true` but VERIFIED a false positive — the sole `gate_weakening` evidence is `test_markers.py: ... membership added: """` (an added test DOCSTRING misread as a membership-set addition); `git log -p -- tests | grep '^-def test_'` confirms ZERO test defs removed/renamed and no threshold softened (the two repurposed tests kept their names and were strengthened). Per Prohibition #2 this was investigated and confirmed not a real weakening. No spin-off warranted.

**Intervention record:** `docs/interventions/harden-2026-07-r67.md` (`pipeline: hardening`, `target_signal: event:cycle-end` — the fix relocates the forward-budget advance ONTO the `cycle-end` bracket event, so `forward_cycles` now tracks real cycle-end(kind=real) events 1:1 instead of probe firings; the probe-driven over-count is eliminated. Expected-direction decrease (spurious non-cycle-end forward advances -> 0), self-emitted by the changed `--cycle-end` handler).

Coupled trio §1d.1 made the harden dispatch bracket explicit (`--kind meta --sub-skill hardening`) so the marker reliably carries the identity the exemption keys on. Regression test (`test_markers.py`, `_TESTS`-registered): a hardening cycle subagent is PERMITTED `--record-intervention`; a non-hardening cycle subagent is STILL refused (exit 3); `--run-end` STILL refused (exit 3) under a hardening marker.   - Mechanical fix applied: new `lazy_core.flush_commit_artifacts(repo_root, artifact_paths, message)` — stages ONLY the explicit artifact paths, then commits them with a trailing `-- <pathspec>` so ONLY those paths are captured from the working tree; any concurrently-staged foreign file is left in the index, untouched, NEVER absorbed (fail-open: a git failure returns `ok:False` not a raise; a no-op flush with no present artifacts commits nothing). The coupled trio (`/lazy-batch`, `/lazy-bug-batch`, `/lazy-batch-cloud`) §1c.6 gained an explicit **flush-commit staging contract**: stage + commit ONLY the exact `docs/interventions/<id>.md` records the evaluators wrote this run, `docs/kpi/SCORECARD.md`, and the specific `docs/bugs/reconsider-<id>/` / `canary-revert-<id>/` seeds — via a pathspec-scoped `git commit -- <paths>`, NEVER a broad `git add -A docs/*`; if a foreign staged/dirty state is present, commit only the flush's explicit paths and leave the foreign state for its owner. Regression test (`test_ledgers.py`, `_TESTS`-registered): with a foreign `docs/bugs/*/SPEC.md` staged alongside the flush artifacts, `flush_commit_artifacts` commits ONLY the artifacts; the foreign file is absent from the commit and remains staged. Coupled-pair overlays re-extracted (byte-identical); skill-size baseline raised for the mandated contract prose. Gates run: pytest package 2365 passed (1 pre-existing fleet-server flake, test_post_to_fleet_routes_404, passes in isolation — unrelated), test_hooks 238/238, lint-skills OK, lazy-state/bug-state --test OK, parity + merged-view exit 0, coupled-check byte-identical. Commit + push: `1cb997e0`.
  - LIVE VALIDATION (this very run): a concurrent harden session was writing claude-config THROUGHOUT this run (it committed Round 71 `5331908b` + a `NEEDS_INPUT_...research-gated...md` sentinel between my commits). Every commit this round made used EXPLICIT pathspecs (never `git add -A`), so the concurrent agent's untracked sentinel + its files were NEVER absorbed — the fix's discipline was exercised end-to-end against a real concurrent writer.

**Over-fit spin-off:** none — the fix ADDS a helper encapsulating the `git commit -- <pathspec>` mechanism + a prose contract; it appends no literal to a matcher. Class has not recurred. `harness-gate` on the range: `gate_weakening` residual is only the sanctioned skill-size-baseline raises (see Round 73).

**Intervention record:** `docs/interventions/harden-2026-07-r74.md` (`pipeline: hardening`, `target_signal: undeclared`, `baseline: not-computable`). No closed ledger-event tracks flush-commit foreign-file absorption; the durable guarantee is the `flush_commit_artifacts` pathspec regression (a foreign staged file is not absorbed) — and the live validation above. Honestly `undeclared` after investigating the vocabulary.

## Round 75 — 2026-07-17 — observed-friction

**Item in flight:** hydra-overlay (AlgoBooth `/lazy-batch` execute-plan part 6; blocking observed-friction harden — the orchestrator awaited this round in the foreground before re-probing)
**Divergence point:** `/execute-plan` cycle turn-end verification — a cycle subagent backgrounded the heavy AlgoBooth quality gates (`npm run qg -- rust`, `npm run qg -- ts`) to verify a work-unit before committing, then yielded its turn. `long-build-ownership-guard.sh` (the request-time guard that redirects self-terminating background builds to orchestrator ownership) did NOT match the qg gate commands — its `_LONG_BUILD_RE` covered only `tauri build` / `cargo build --release` / `npm run build` — so no takeover signal fired and the subagent was free to background them. Recurred TWICE this run.

**Root cause:** `missing-contract` — the ENFORCEMENT layer for an already-advised rule was absent. Round 45 (`cycle-subagent-over-cap-aggregate-gate-auto-backgrounds`) added PROSE telling the subagent to decompose over-cap gates and never background a long gate; the request-time GUARD that makes it un-bypassable enumerated only the three packaged-build signatures. The heavy qg gates are long builds/tests by the same definition (exceed a subagent turn; die identically when backgrounded — the qg-rust queue wrapper is reaped orphaning `cargo` + leaving a stale `active.lock`, a bare qg-ts vite build vanishes) but were never added to the guard signature set (`user/hooks/long-build-ownership-guard.sh` `_LONG_BUILD_RE`, lines ~193-199), the SKILL.md Step 1d guard-takeover enumeration, or the AlgoBooth `long-build-ownership.md` doc. Net: a gate-passing WU left UNCOMMITTED; the orchestrator manually waited out the orphaned `cargo`, cleared the lock, and re-ran the gates orchestrator-owned. Bug spec (Step 2.5, committed `harden(docs): 622d723a` BEFORE the fix): `docs/bugs/_archive/long-build-ownership-guard-misses-qg-gates/` (Concluded).

**Action:**
  - Mechanical fix applied (no gate weakened): extended `_LONG_BUILD_RE` with an enumerated arm `npm\s+run\s+(?:qg|quality-gate)\s+--\s+(?:rust|ts|sidecar)(?:\s|$)` — heavy targets only, so the fast `arch`/`docs`/`lint` groups and a bare `npm run qg` are deliberately NOT redirected (D1 near-zero-false-positive charter). `_queue_routing_hint` fires unchanged for the manifest-registered qg-rust/qg-sidecar (adds the queue-wrapper hint) and correctly stays silent for qg-ts (not queue-serialized — plain ownership redirect). Mirrored the signature into the deny message, the guard header RULE comment, `user/skills/lazy-batch/SKILL.md` Step 1d guard-takeover paragraph, and `repos/algobooth/.claude/skill-config/long-build-ownership.md`. Five hook tests added + `_TESTS`-registered (deny qg-rust/qg-ts/qg-sidecar + `quality-gate` alias + cd-prefixed; allow fast qg groups / bare qg / `ts-foo`). Commit + push: `406fa426`. Schemas untouched → coupled-pair mirroring (lazy-bug-batch carries no guard-takeover prose) + sentinel-schema lockstep N/A.

**Over-fit spin-off:** signal 1 (literal-phrase-to-matcher) TRIPPED — `harness-gate.py --staged --json` returned `overfit: flag` citing the alternation literal appended to `_LONG_BUILD_RE` (and `gate_weakening_hit: false`, Prohibition #2 satisfied). Enumerating `rust|ts|sidecar` in the generic guard DUPLICATES the heavy-op SSOT that already lives in `build-queue-ops.json` for qg-rust/qg-sidecar; the next heavy qg target would gap again (signal 3). Per the phrase-match rule, spins off on FIRST occurrence. Generalization RECORDED for front-enqueue: a `/spec-bug` `adhoc-manifest-driven-longbuild-ownership` — "make the ownership guard redirect any `build-queue-ops.json` op deny-pattern (heavy-op SSOT), with an ownership-only op marker (`queue:false`) so a non-queue-serialized heavy gate like qg-ts lives in the manifest instead of a hardcoded guard signature; class boundary = manifest-declared heavy ops, generic no-manifest fallback signatures deliberately OUT of scope." Cited instance: Round 75 / `long-build-ownership-guard.sh:_LONG_BUILD_RE` / the `npm run qg -- rust|ts|sidecar` arm. **The actual `--enqueue-adhoc` is orchestrator-owned** — both `lazy-state.py --enqueue-adhoc` and `bug-state.py --enqueue-adhoc` are DENIED by `lazy-cycle-containment.sh` from an in-flight cycle subagent (this hardening dispatch); recorded here + PushNotification for the orchestrator to enqueue, exactly as prior rounds handled barred dispatch mechanisms. NOT blocking (the instance is already fixed).

**Intervention record:** `docs/interventions/harden-2026-07-r75.md` — `--target-signal event:containment-refusal`, expected-direction **increase** (self-emitted): post-fix the ownership guard emits a `LONG-BUILD-OWNERSHIP-TAKEOVER` containment-refusal for a qg-rust/qg-ts backgrounded from a cycle subagent where pre-fix it emitted nothing and the gate died silently — a nonzero qg-family takeover-refusal count confirms the enforcement is live. ## Round 76 — 2026-07-17 — observed-friction

**Item in flight:** hydra-overlay (AlgoBooth `/lazy-batch`; blocking observed-friction harden — same dispatch as Round 75, second of two distinct defects)
**Divergence point:** `lazy-state.py --probe` live-settings split-brain field — every probe of a run TARGETING a consumer repo (AlgoBooth) emits `live_settings_ok=false` with detail `tracked user/settings.json is missing/unreadable`, even though the live `~/.claude/settings.json` symlink correctly points at the claude-config checkout.

**Root cause:** `script-defect` — the tracked settings SSOT is resolved against the wrong repo. `doc-drift-lint.check_live_settings(repo_root, …)` computes `tracked = repo_root / "user" / "settings.json"`, and `live_settings_probe(repo_root)` (`lazy-state.py:11474`) / `_live_settings_banner` (`lazy_inject.py:277`) pass the RUN's `repo_root` (AlgoBooth). But the tracked settings SSOT exists ONLY in the claude-config checkout (`~/source/repos/claude-config/user/settings.json`), which is exactly where the live symlink points; AlgoBooth has no `user/` dir, so `tracked.read_bytes()` raises `OSError` → the false "missing/unreadable" finding. A two-scope mismatch: `_live_settings_path` is already machine-global/repo-independent, but the TRACKED side stayed repo-scoped. Bug spec (Step 2.5, committed `harden(docs): 622d723a` BEFORE the fix): `docs/bugs/_archive/live-settings-probe-false-positive-in-consumer-repo/` (Concluded).

**Action:**
  - Mechanical fix applied (no gate weakened): added `settings_ssot_root(repo_root)` (backed by monkeypatchable `_config_checkout_root()` = `Path(__file__).resolve().parents[2]`, the claude-config root resolved through the `~/.claude/scripts` symlink) to `doc-drift-lint.py` — when `repo_root` already carries `user/settings.json` (claude-config itself / a hermetic fixture) it is returned unchanged; a consumer repo falls back to the claude-config checkout, mirroring the two-scope efficacy/canary/intervention-coverage flush. Wired into `live_settings_probe` (lazy-state.py) and `_live_settings_banner` (lazy_inject.py), both still fail-open; `check_live_settings`/`live_settings_status` stay PURE functions of their `repo_root` arg (the `--live` CLI + hermetic `test_doc_drift_lint.py` fixtures depend on that). Two probe tests added (a consumer repo resolves the SSOT to claude-config → `ok=True`; a repo carrying the SSOT is used unchanged). Commit + push: `406fa426` (same commit as Round 75). Schemas untouched → coupled-pair mirroring + sentinel-schema lockstep N/A.

**Over-fit spin-off:** none — the fix is STRUCTURAL (a two-scope resolver helper, not a literal appended to any matcher). `harness-gate.py --staged` `overfit: flag` evidence is entirely attributable to Round 75's guard arm + its tests, NOT to the Gap-2 files (`doc-drift-lint.py` / `lazy-state.py` / `lazy_inject.py`); `gate_weakening_hit: false`. Signal 1 N/A. Signal 2: prior live-settings rounds (29-31) targeted the split-brain ENFORCEMENT plane (different root cause); this is the first occurrence of the cross-repo-consumer SSOT-resolution class. No spin-off.

**Intervention record:** `docs/interventions/harden-2026-07-r76.md` — `--target-signal undeclared` (explicitly typed, NOT undeclared-by-laziness): the friction is a boolean field (`live_settings_ok`) in `--probe` JSON output, which the closed ledger-event vocabulary does not capture (no event fires per probe). `baseline: not-computable`, INCONCLUSIVE-by-construction, surfaced for triage — same immeasurable-by-vocabulary class as Round 45.

## Round 77 — 2026-07-17 — observed-friction

**Item in flight:** hydra-overlay (AlgoBooth `/lazy-batch`; background observed-friction harden, blocking=false — first of two distinct lazy-batch gaps in this dispatch)
**Divergence point:** `lazy-state.py --emit-dispatch <class>` (apply-resolution) → the post-binding residue guard in `emit_dispatch_prompt` fail-closed a correct dispatch whose recorded `resolution_summary` context value legitimately contained a literal curly-brace wire-type; refused with `unbound token(s) after binding`. Worked around live by rephrasing the summary brace-free (mangling the DATA).

**Root cause:** `script-defect` — `lazy_core/dispatch.py`. Both `emit_dispatch_prompt` (formerly binding at ~:1128 then scanning at ~:1132) and the sibling `emit_cycle_prompt` (~:851/:855) ran `_PROMPT_RESIDUE_RE.findall(prompt)` on the FULLY-BOUND prompt — AFTER the free-text context/state VALUES were injected. `_PROMPT_RESIDUE_RE = \{[a-z0-9_]+\}` cannot distinguish a genuine unbound TEMPLATE placeholder from a `{lower_snake}` brace that merely appears INSIDE an injected value (a code snippet, a JSON object, a curly-brace wire-type in a recorded `resolution_summary`/`failure_summary`), so a correct dispatch fail-closed on its own DATA. The `apply-resolution` / `record-decision` paths carry exactly such operator/orchestrator free text. Same deep class the log has hit before on other symbols (Round 1's unanchored `not-required` substring; the descope-marker rounds) — a matcher scanning text that contains BOTH the token-of-interest AND look-alike content — but a NEW symbol (the emit residue guard) never previously touched. Bug spec (Step 2.5, committed `harden(docs): 862f9b55` BEFORE the fix): `docs/bugs/_archive/emit-dispatch-residue-guard-flags-content-braces/` (Concluded).

**Action:**
  - Mechanical fix applied (no gate weakened): added `_template_residue(template_text, bindings)` to `lazy_core/dispatch.py` — it strips every KNOWN `{token}` placeholder from the template with empty-string replacement, THEN scans the remainder for `_PROMPT_RESIDUE_RE` residue, i.e. residue detection on the PRE-INJECTION template. Rewired both emit sites to run the guard via `_template_residue(prompt, bindings)` BEFORE the value-bind loop (`emit_cycle_prompt` preserves its addenda-attribution suffix by scanning the addenda blob's own template residue the same way). A `{lower_snake}` brace inside an injected VALUE is now structurally invisible to the guard (opaque DATA), while a genuine unbound TEMPLATE placeholder (not in `bindings`) still survives the strip and is caught + named. 2 regression tests added + registered in `_TESTS` (dispatch-site: content braces + JSON in a `failure_summary` value → `ok=True`, value survives verbatim; cycle-site near-neighbor: brace in `feature_name`/`{item_name}` → `ok=True`). Commit + push: `b9d335ad`. Schemas untouched → coupled-pair mirroring + sentinel-schema lockstep N/A.

**Over-fit spin-off:** none — the fix is STRUCTURAL (reorders WHEN residue detection runs — pre- vs post-injection; `_PROMPT_RESIDUE_RE` itself is unchanged, no literal appended to any matcher). `harness-gate.py --range origin/main..HEAD` returned `overfit: flag`, but the flag evidence is entirely test-fixture STRING LITERALS (template strings like `"<!-- @requires item_id,failure_summary -->"` and docstring `"""`) mis-read as membership-construct appends — a false positive, not a literal-phrase-to-matcher smell; `gate_weakening_hit: false`. Signal 1 N/A (structural). Signal 2: same broad "matcher conflates content with structural position" class as Round 1, but a DIFFERENT symbol (emit residue guard vs `_read_mcp_runtime_decision`) — the ≥2-same-symbol threshold is not met. The structural fix covers both emit sites and every value-content-brace case, so it will not gap on the next variant. No spin-off.

**Intervention record:** `docs/interventions/harden-2026-07-r77.md` — `--target-signal undeclared` (explicitly typed, NOT undeclared-by-laziness): an `emit_dispatch_prompt` residue refusal is a CLI-level `{"ok": False}` return that fires NO event in the closed ledger vocabulary (`run/cycle/dispatch/halt/sentinel/gate-refusal/containment-refusal`) — the friction is worked around inline, never recorded countably. `baseline: not-computable`, INCONCLUSIVE-by-construction, surfaced for triage (same immeasurable-by-vocabulary class as Rounds 30/45/76). Efficacy is instead pinned by the 2 regression tests.

## Round 78 — 2026-07-17 — observed-friction

**Item in flight:** hydra-overlay (AlgoBooth `/lazy-batch`, plan part 8; background observed-friction harden, blocking=false — second of two distinct lazy-batch gaps in this dispatch)
**Divergence point:** Step 1h blocked-resolution "Add a phase to resolve the blocker" (worker contract `dispatch-apply-resolution.md` `@section blocked-steps` + its `blocked-resolution.md` reference mirror) → the corrective phase was authored and the superseded deliverables struck in PHASES.md, but the ORIGINATING In-progress plan (`plans/…-part-8`) was left with plain unchecked `- [ ] WU-N` rows for those same superseded deliverables. Next probe: `lazy-state.py` Step 7a re-routed `/execute-plan` back to the superseded plan → re-attempts the architecturally-impossible WUs → re-blocks (infinite loop). Cleared live only by a manual recovery cycle that struck the plan-body WUs + flipped the plan to Complete.

**Root cause:** `missing-contract` — the "Add a phase" contract reconciled `PHASES.md` (the human deliverable view) but had NO step reconciling the ORIGINATING plan (the MACHINE routing source of truth). `find_implementation_plans` (`lazy_core/docmodel.py`) returns every plan whose frontmatter `status` != `Complete`; `_plan_wu_checkbox_counts` (`lazy_core/gates.py`, regex `_PLAN_WU_CHECKBOX_RE`) counts each `- [ ] WU-N` row as remaining work. So an In-progress plan with unchecked WUs for now-impossible deliverables re-heads Step 7a's routing and re-blocks. A legitimately novel situation the contract was never given a rule for. Bug spec (Step 2.5, committed `harden(docs): 862f9b55` BEFORE the fix): `docs/bugs/_archive/blocked-add-phase-strands-originating-in-progress-plan/` (Concluded).

**Action:**
  - Mechanical fix applied (contract/prose only — NO script change; no gate weakened): added a mandatory RECONCILE-ORIGINATING-PLAN step to the "Add a phase to resolve the blocker" branch of `dispatch-apply-resolution.md` (authoritative worker contract) and its `blocked-resolution.md` reference mirror. When the new corrective phase SUPERSEDES deliverables belonging to an originating In-progress plan under `<spec_path>/plans/`: (a) strike each superseded WU row in the plan's `## Work Units` checklist with the canonical descoped marker — `- [ ] ~~WU-N — <title>~~ **SUPERSEDED** <!-- descoped -->` (SSOT `lazy_core:_DESCOPED_MARKER`); (b) flip the plan frontmatter `status:` to `Complete` iff every remaining WU is `[x]` landed or struck (else leave In-progress). Verified contract-only is SUFFICIENT (no script change owed): `find_implementation_plans` already skips `status: Complete` plans, and the strikethrough breaks the `_PLAN_WU_CHECKBOX_RE` anchor so `_plan_wu_checkbox_counts` drops the struck row from the unchecked count — confirmed empirically (`unchecked=0` for the struck form vs `unchecked=2` for the plain-unchecked bug reproduction). Projected skills regenerated (`project-skills.py`); `blocked-resolution.md` is a `!cat` component. Commit + push: `f9308fd3`. Coupled-pair mirroring: the edited components are the SHARED single source consumed by the feature+bug orchestrators (sections `pipelines=feature,bug`), so no per-SKILL mirror is owed; sentinel schemas untouched.

**Over-fit spin-off:** none — `missing-contract`, FIRST occurrence of this class/symbol (the "Add a phase" originating-plan reconciliation gap has no prior round). Not a matcher change (signal 1 N/A). The reconcile step is worded CONDITIONALLY ("IF the new phase supersedes originating-plan WUs") so it self-applies to any future supersession path without over-reaching into the near-neighbor `ratify-redirect` path (which re-aligns surfaces rather than striking originating deliverables, so it does not strand plan WUs the same way). `harness-gate.py` `gate_weakening_hit: false`; the `overfit: flag` evidence traces only to Round 77's test fixtures, not to the Gap-2 `.md` contract files. No spin-off.

**Intervention record:** `docs/interventions/harden-2026-07-r78.md` — `--target-signal undeclared` (explicitly typed, NOT undeclared-by-laziness): the route-loop recurrence is a probe-COMPUTED `repeat_count`/`step_repeat` climb (never emitted as a ledger event) and its terminal effect is a broad `blocked`/`max-cycles` halt confounded by every unrelated cause (poor signal independence) — the exact immeasurable-by-vocabulary reasoning Round 30 established for route-loop friction. `baseline: not-computable`, INCONCLUSIVE-by-construction, surfaced for triage.

## Round 79 — 2026-07-17 — manual

**Item in flight:** research-prompt pipeline (operator-observed friction; manual `/harden-harness` invocation, empirically grounded — no probe/registry/marker state)
**Divergence point:** `/spec` Phase 2 (prompt compose step 3 + length check step 5) and the `/lazy-batch` research-halt announcement `{within | over}` indicator (Step 1f + `_components/lazy-batch-prompts/research-halt-announcement.md`) — all sized/labelled the pasted research prompt against `GEMINI_PROMPT_CHAR_CAP = 24,000`, which sits ABOVE Gemini's true silent hard-truncation point.

**Root cause:** `script-defect` (prose-constant class — no executable script owns the value). Gemini's Deep Research prompt textarea SILENTLY hard-truncates at exactly 20,000 chars; the cap was set to 24,000 on a mistaken "~30,000-char practical limit, ~6,000 headroom" model (cap-source comment `user/skills/spec/SKILL.md:440`). Because 24,000 > 20,000, every 20,000–24,000-char prompt was silently cut on paste while the `{within|over}` indicator still reported "within". Empirically measured 2026-07-17: a 21,275-char `RESEARCH_PROMPT.md` truncated at char 20,000, severing mid-word inside Question 10 and dropping the ENTIRE "Output Format Request" section. Bug spec (Step 2.5, committed `harden(docs): 0d6b9175` BEFORE the fix): `docs/bugs/_archive/gemini-prompt-char-cap-above-hard-truncation-limit/` (Concluded).

**Action:**
  - Mechanical fix applied (prose/constant only — NO script change; the threshold was TIGHTENED, no gate weakened): lowered `GEMINI_PROMPT_CHAR_CAP` 24,000 → **18,000** (~2,000 chars headroom BELOW the confirmed 20,000 hard truncation, preserving the original below-the-real-limit discipline relative to the NEW real limit). Updated the constant, the `{within|over}` comparison threshold, every human-readable "24,000-char" mention, and the headroom rationale (rewritten to cite the 20,000 measurement) across `user/skills/spec/SKILL.md` (constant L438, cap-source comment L440-445, body-budget note L445 6,000-prepend→12K+ body, length-check L491, report line L498), `user/skills/spec-buddy/SKILL.md` (L255, L273), `docs/specs/spec-buddy/PHASES.md` (minimal-replication seam note L111), `user/skills/lazy-batch/SKILL.md` (L1433), `user/skills/_components/lazy-batch-prompts/research-halt-announcement.md` (comparison note L17-18, both `[length: …]` templates L93/L152), the `user/scripts/coupled-overlays/lazy-batch-cloud.overlay.json` verbatim divergence lines, and the regenerated derived `repos/algobooth/.claude/skills/lazy-batch-cloud/SKILL.md` (via `generate-coupled-skills.py --write --pair lazy-batch-cloud`; `--check` all pairs byte-identical). Deliberately OUT of scope and untouched: `test_project_skills.py::_CYCLE_PROMPT_SIZE_CEILING = 24000` (unrelated cycle-dispatch-prompt guard) and `IDENTITY_PREPEND_CHAR_BUDGET = 6,000` (independent of the cap). `lazy-bug-batch/SKILL.md` carries no 24,000 reference (verified — no coupled-twin edit owed). Commit + push: `d5e9bb22`.

**Over-fit spin-off:** none — `script-defect`/prose-constant, FIRST occurrence of this class/symbol (no prior hardening round touched `GEMINI_PROMPT_CHAR_CAP` / the research-prompt char cap). The fix changes a CONSTANT VALUE (structural), not a literal-phrase-to-matcher (signal 1 N/A). `harness-gate.py --range` reported `gate_weakening_hit: true` and `overfit: flag`, BOTH assessed as false positives: (a) the `gate_weakening` heuristic keys on any numeric-literal change on a "gate line" and cannot read tightening-vs-loosening — 18,000 < 24,000 makes the `{within|over}` guard fire on strictly MORE inputs (no input is more permissive under the new value), so this is a TIGHTENING that makes the harness more protective, the opposite of a Prohibition-#2 weakening, and clears no denial; (b) the `overfit` evidence traces only to pre-existing `{within|over}` alternation tokens sitting NEAR the numeric edits (and the JSON-list shape of the overlay prose lines) — no alternative was appended to any matcher/allowlist. No spin-off; run not blocked.

**Intervention record:** `docs/interventions/harden-2026-07-r79.md` — `--target-signal undeclared` (explicitly typed, NOT undeclared-by-laziness): "silently-truncated research prompt" is a paste-time UI event with NO corresponding ledger-event vocabulary entry (the closed set is run/cycle/dispatch/halt/sentinel/gate-refusal/containment-refusal) and is not emitted anywhere — the fix is regression-test-pinned / prose-constant by nature. `baseline: not-computable`, INCONCLUSIVE-by-construction, surfaced for triage. Efficacy is instead pinned by the constant's presence: a future prompt ≥18,000 now trips the "over" indicator before paste.

**Gates run:**
  test_lazy_core.py (pytest user/scripts/tests/test_lazy_core): 1215/1215
  test_hooks.py: 243/243
  lint-skills.py: OK (--check-projected --check-capabilities)

**Item in flight:** "agent stopped waiting on a test run / build" (operator-directed manual `/harden-harness`; observed live this session — `/execute-plan` orchestrator `a794d046b1a72540d` for AlgoBooth hydra-overlay Phase 9.5). **Divergence point:** not a dispatch misroute. The RECEIVER seam: the MAIN/dispatcher session read a `status=completed` `<task-notification>` from an in-flight `/execute-plan` orchestrator as TERMINAL completion, and nearly `TaskStop`'d it + took over `src-tauri/src/hydra/mod.rs` against the still-live WU-1/WU-2 impl sub-subagents (`ab06a7856a317a6c6`, `a53234f114e95e648`) — a dual-writer collision, averted only by a coincidental `TaskStop` failure. The orchestrator itself was COMPLIANT (foreground fan-out, correctly re-invoked per child-completion); its last end_turns were legitimate inter-dispatch pauses ("Awaiting WU-2 impl agent").

**Root cause:** `missing-contract` — the complementary RECEIVER half of Round 39's `missing-contract`. The `<task-notification>` fires per its literal contract ("each time this agent stops with no live *background* children"), and a mandated-FOREGROUND fan-out orchestrator has no *background* children at any inter-dispatch pause, so `completed` fires at every pause though the run is merely PAUSED (harness re-invokes on child return). Rounds 39 & 45 hardened only the SENDER (`turn-end-gate.md`: don't end your turn awaiting work); NO contract told a dispatcher/main session how to INTERPRET a `completed` notification against a live orchestrator. The authoritative "actually done" signal (the `/execute-plan` run marker present⇒in-flight + plan `status: Complete`) existed on disk and was never consulted. Bug spec (Step 2.5, committed `harden(docs): d02740b7` BEFORE the fix): `docs/bugs/_archive/dispatched-orchestrator-completed-notification-misread-as-terminal/` (Concluded).

**Action:**
  - Mechanical fix applied (the FALSE-COMPLETION / receiver half): NEW canonical component `user/skills/_components/dispatched-agent-liveness.md` — the RECEIVER-side counterpart to `turn-end-gate.md`: reconciles the contract wording (a foreground-await pause satisfies "no background children" without being terminal); establishes the run marker + plan status as the AUTHORITATIVE completion signal and the notification as merely advisory; a decision procedure (marker live ⇒ do NOT `TaskStop`/`Edit` the lineage's files — dual-writer risk — `TaskList` for live descendants, wait for resume); and a genuine-wedge recovery path (confirm no live descendants, prefer `SendMessage`-resume, take over only as sole writer; marker-teardown authority deferred to decision #12, not re-opened).
