## Round 92 — 2026-07-18 — no-route

**Item in flight:** external-owner-contracts-locked-without-consultation
**Divergence point:** `/lazy-batch-parallel` Step-1a merged-head divergence check — cross-script split-brain. `lazy-state.py --emit-prompt --skip-needs-research` (skip-aware) excluded the research-pending feature heads and computed merged head = the `Concluded` bug `external-owner-contracts-locked-without-consultation`, WITHHOLDING the feature-side emit (`route_overridden_by: merged-head-diverged`); but `bug-state.py --emit-prompt` (scoped to that exact bug, NO `--skip-needs-research` flag — it doesn't accept one) computed its merged head WITHOUT the exclusion = the research-pending feature `merged-head-actionability-oracle` and ALSO withheld (`merged-head-diverged`). Neither script emitted any route — the two coupled scripts computed DIFFERENT merged heads for the same on-disk state.

**Root cause:** script-defect — the research-pending exclusion in `nondispatchable_item_ids` (`lazy_core/depdag.py`) was gated on `skip_needs_research`, a flag only `lazy-state.py` threads and `bug-state.py` cannot accept (`bug-state.py --skip-needs-research` = argparse usage error). This is the follow-up incompleteness of Round 91 (`baf07a6d`), whose log explicitly left `bug-state.py`'s coupled merged-head caller "byte-identical" on the reasoning that "research gating is a feature/bug divergence." That reasoning is wrong for the MERGED-head computation: `bug-state.py`'s merged-head-override reads the FEATURE queue too (`_load_feature_queue_for_merged`) to detect a higher-priority cross-pipeline item, so it MUST exclude a research-pending FEATURE head — but it has no flag and its `probe_skipped_ids(state, _mo_bugs)` is bug-scoped (can never fold in a feature head), so the file predicate in `nondispatchable_item_ids` is its ONLY reachable exclusion, and the flag-gate made that inert on the bug side. 6th facet of the merged-head exclude-set recurring class.

**Action:**
  - Mechanical fix applied: dropped the `skip_needs_research and` gate in `lazy_core/depdag.py::nondispatchable_item_ids` so `docmodel.spec_dir_research_pending` is an UNCONDITIONAL member — the on-disk `NEEDS_RESEARCH.md` / `RESEARCH_PROMPT.md`-without-`RESEARCH*.md` sentinel IS the deliberate research-defer decision, so no flag context is needed. A research-pending head is non-dispatchable on EVERY run (halts at the Step-5 walk gate, or is skipped under `--skip-needs-research`), and the merged-head-override never CREATES a dispatch (it only withholds an already-chosen forward route on a higher-priority DISPATCHABLE divergence), so excluding it unconditionally can never suppress a legitimate withhold and on a halt the override is not reached. Byte-identical for `lazy-state.py` forward routing (the head was already excluded via the file predicate under the flag, or via `probe_skipped_ids`/`gated_heads` under default skip-ahead) and CORRECT for `bug-state.py`. The `skip_needs_research` kwarg is retained accepted-but-INERT for call-site signature compatibility. Updated `depdag.py` + `docmodel.py` docstrings. Regression: updated the existing fixture to assert unconditional exclusion (excluded WITH and WITHOUT the flag) + NEW `test_research_pending_exclusion_consistent_across_state_scripts` (research-skipped feature head + `Concluded` on-disk bug -> both callers' exclude sets EQUAL -> SAME merged head = the bug -> bug side emits, feature side withholds pointing at the DISPATCHABLE bug; no deadlock). `retires:` the flag-gating of the research-pending merged-head exclusion (a redundant second gate only one coupled script could read); the `--skip-needs-research` CLI flag + its `compute_state` WALK behavior are UNTOUCHED. harness-gate (`--staged`): `gate_weakening: pass` / `tautology: pass` / `complexity: declaration-required -> retires: flag-gating` / `overfit: flag` = **FALSE POSITIVE** (all four evidence lines are test-fixture queue-id string literals in assertion `set`s — `external-owner-contracts-locked-without-consultation`, `merged-head-actionability-oracle`, `subagent-wedge-backstop-hook` — NOT a production matcher/allow-list append; the production change REMOVED a gate condition — structural, the opposite of a phrase append; same false-positive class Round 91 documented). Commit + push: `981191ae` (bug spec `7d8160f8`).

**Over-fit spin-off:** none NEW — signal 1 (literal-phrase-to-matcher) does NOT apply (the production change removed a conditional gate; the overfit flag is a test-fixture false positive). Signal 2 (class recurred >=2 — this is the 6th facet) DOES apply, but the structural generalization was ALREADY spun off by Round 91 as the `/spec` handback «replace the category-enumerated merged-head exclude set with a single per-item actionability oracle asking "would `compute_state` dispatch this item this run?"». That item now EXISTS in-queue as the research-pending feature `merged-head-actionability-oracle` (commits `a9aefec0`/`a4a9c1ad` — it is literally one of THIS deadlock's two wedge heads). No duplicate enqueue; this round reinforces the existing handback — a 6th facet the same day is strong evidence the operator should prioritize the oracle. Cross-ref: this round's spec names `merged-head-actionability-oracle` as the durable generalization.

**Reconciliation:** done (inline, partial handback) — this round FULLY fixed `docs/bugs/merged-head-research-exclusion-flag-gated-splits-cross-script`. Wrote the hand `FIXED.md` receipt (`provenance: backfilled-unverified`, citing fix `981191ae` + green gates), flipped `**Status:** Concluded -> Fixed`, and ran `bug-state.py --archive-fixed docs/bugs/merged-head-research-exclusion-flag-gated-splits-cross-script` (RC=0, committed `2b97f912`, archived to `docs/bugs/_archive/`). `--record-intervention` also ran directly (RC=0). ## Round 93 — 2026-07-18 — no-route

**Item in flight:** dispatched-harden-record-intervention-refused-by-containment
**Divergence point:** `bug-state.py::compute_state` Step-7 plan-needed predicate — routed `sub_skill=write-plan` for a PHASES whose all impl deliverables are `[x]` and whose sole unchecked row is `<!-- verification-only -->` with NO `plans/` dir; the dispatched `/write-plan` (cycle 26) correctly authored zero WUs (Step 1c.5 excludes verification-only rows; Step 4.5 needs ≥1 WU), so the probe re-returned write-plan → a guaranteed `probe→write-plan→no-op` step-repeat loop.

**Root cause:** script-defect (coupled-pair parity gap) — `bug-state.py`'s Step-7 verification-only bypass required `not plans and _has_any_complete_plan(spec_dir) and remaining_unchecked_are_verification_only(phases_text)`. When the fix lands OUT-OF-PIPELINE there is no plan file, so `_has_any_complete_plan` is False → the bypass is skipped → control falls to `elif not plans:` → write-plan → loop. The **feature-side** `lazy-state.py` fixed this exact class on 2026-06-15 (mcp-testing deadlock, `lazy-state.py:3391-3428`) by splitting the bypass into `cloud_bypass = cloud and not plans and _has_any_complete_plan` and `workstation_bypass = not cloud and not plans and verification_only`, DROPPING `_has_any_complete_plan` from the workstation path — a verification-only remainder is itself proof no impl work remains (write-plan is banned by its Step 1c.5 from emitting such a WU). That fix was never mirrored to `bug-state.py`, whose comment even CLAIMED to "mirror the identical bypass in lazy-state.py" but carried the pre-fix combined form. Routing predicate ≠ the completion-gate's `remaining_unchecked_are_verification_only()` semantics (which already exempts a verification-only remainder). Live evidence: `docs/bugs/_archive/dispatched-harden-record-intervention-refused-by-containment/PHASES.md` line 33 (6 impl `[x]` + 1 verification-only `[ ]`, no `plans/`).

## Round 94 — 2026-07-18 — discovered-defect-batch

**Item in flight:** parallel-run-harness-gaps-round-2
**Divergence point:** `lazy-state.py::main` `--emit-prompt` merged-head divergence guard — the `/lazy-batch-parallel` coordinator's SERIAL-TAIL probe (`--emit-prompt --feature-id polyphonic-parameter-modulation`, run at the MAIN root against the PARENT marker, `parent_run: null`) returned `route_overridden_by: merged-head-diverged` and WITHHELD the tail's mcp-test dispatch, because the merged head had become the freshly-research-ingested `inspector-track-dashboard`. Round-85's gap-1 lane exemption keys on `parent_run` (set only for lane markers), so the parent-marker tail was not exempted.

**Root cause:** batch — **script-defect** (gap 8, RUN-BLOCKING) + **missing-contract** (gap 9).
- Gap 8: `merged_head_override`'s serial priority-inversion premise is void for a coordinator-authorized emission that is legitimately not the global head. Round-85 handled the LANE form (`parent_run`); the post-merge validation TAIL runs at the main root against the PARENT marker (`parent_run: null` → `_emit_is_lane` False → guard runs). The tail item holds a LIVE `lazy_coord` lease (`leases.json` in the main-root state dir) and its lane is already merged — a live lease on the PROBED item is actively-owned in-flight work, never the stale route the guard exists to catch. Lease-EXCLUSION (round-85's rejected alt) still would not clear it — the divergent head here is a fresh NON-leased item, so it stays the head; only exempting the probe for its OWN live lease removes the withhold. Evidence: probe JSON `{"route_overridden_by": "merged-head-diverged", "probed": "polyphonic-parameter-modulation", "context": "main-root serial-tail emission; item lease-held and lane-merged"}`; guard at `lazy-state.py:14021` (mirror `bug-state.py:9667`).
- Gap 9: `--ensure-runtime` killed under `run_in_background` (two instant zero-byte kills under an active marker; identical foreground → READY/health 200). It owns its own background `dev:restart` + a synchronous multi-minute health poll (`runtimeplane.restart()`), so it is foreground-only; backgrounding it lets the recovery `dev:restart` → `kill-dev.js` process sweep reach the background launcher's own process tree. Root cause hinges on target-repo `kill-dev.js` (Prohibition #1, out of scope) + Claude Code `run_in_background` lifecycle (undocumented; `claude-code-guide` not dispatchable — subagent Agent policy) → the evidence-sanctioned resolution is a documented foreground-only contract, not load-bearing logic on an undocumented mechanism.

**Action:**
  - Mechanical fix applied. Gap 8: added pure read-only `lazy_coord.has_live_lease(leases_path, wi_id)` (factors out `claim_shardable`'s exact liveness predicate — missing file/key → False; present-but-unreadable entry → True, conservative) and exempted the `--emit-prompt` merged-head guard when the probed `feature_id` holds a live lease — the exact analog of the round-85 lane exemption (`_emit_is_lease_held` alongside `_emit_is_lane`, with an observability diagnostic). Mirrored identically into `bug-state.py` (coupled pair). Fail-safe: any read error / no `leases.json` / no live lease → False → guard runs unchanged (byte-identical for every serial run — none has a `leases.json`). Gap 9: documented the FOREGROUND-ONLY CONTRACT in `user/scripts/CLAUDE.md` (`--ensure-runtime` reference) + the `lazy-batch-parallel/SKILL.md` serial-tail step. Regression: `lazy_coord` Fixture 22 `has-live-lease-predicate` (live/expired/missing-key/missing-file/unreadable → correct); `test_dispatch.py` subprocess `test_..._serial_tail_lease_held_skips_merged_head_withhold` (lease-held → NOT withheld) + negative control `test_..._serial_tail_no_lease_still_withholds` (no lease → still withholds, lease-gating proof), both registered in `_TESTS`. harness-gate (`origin/main..HEAD`): `gate_weakening: pass`; `overfit: flag` = **FALSE POSITIVE** (all 14 evidence lines are appended diagnostic-message strings, test-fixture dicts/argv, and the appended doc sentence — NOT matcher/alternation/keyword-set fitting; the production change ADDED a structural boolean predicate + an exemption CONDITION keyed on lease STATE, the opposite of a phrase-to-matcher append — the Round 92/93-documented false-positive class); `complexity: declaration-required` → **retires: net-new** (adds `has_live_lease` + an exemption branch mirroring the existing lane exemption; retires no rule/surface — the exemption keeps the guard's blast radius the same, only adding a second coordinator-authorized carve-out). ## Round 95 — 2026-07-18 — observed-friction

**Item in flight:** managed-llm-credits
**Divergence point:** `/lazy-batch` unified driver Step-1a — the merged-head computation shared by `lazy-state.py --next-merged` (`lazy-state.py:12652`), the feature/bug `--emit-prompt` merged-head divergence guards (`lazy-state.py:14222`, `bug-state.py:9785`), and `research_halt` (`lazy-state.py:14034`), all via `dispatch.merged_head_nondispatchable_ids` + `is_dispatchable` (`lazy_core/dispatch.py:639`/`:601`). Three inconsistent merged heads in one cycle → mutual `route_overridden_by: merged-head-diverged` WITHHOLD (feature names `{worktree…, bug}`; bug names `{hydra-overlay, feature}`; `--next-merged` names the BLOCKED `{hydra-overlay, feature}`) → total no-route deadlock.

**Root cause:** `script-defect` (structural remedy) — a defect in the COMPLETED `merged-head-actionability-oracle` feature's Locked Decision **L3**. The oracle classifies **cross-pipeline** and **stateless `--next-merged`** candidates via a **per-item scoped `compute_state` probe** (`is_dispatchable`), while the **same-pipeline** side (L2) reuses the full probe's own `probe_skipped_ids`. A single-item scoped probe **cannot reproduce a context-dependent skip** the cross-pipeline FULL probe makes, so context-skipped heads misclassify as dispatchable. Two facets reproduced deterministically in-process against the live AlgoBooth queue: (1) BLOCKED-spike head `hydra-overlay` scoped→`sub_skill=spike` dispatchable but full-probe SKIPS it (`_gated_head_kind` "blocked", `lazy-state.py:1936`) — the `spike-pipeline-role` Step-3 route (`lazy-state.py:3094`) flipped a `runtime-spike-verdict-pending` `BLOCKED.md` from `terminal_reason="blocked"` (non-dispatchable) to a dispatchable `spike`, the specific regression that widened the hole; (2) not-independent head `inspector-track-dashboard` scoped→`realign-spec` dispatchable but full-probe SKIPS it (`skip_ahead_ready` fails, `independent` unset after a gated head was skipped). Fixing facet 1 alone moves the deadlock to facet 2 → one structural root, not two patches. **7th facet of the merged-head-exclude-set recurring class** (Rounds 91/92 + `merged-head-diverged-stalls-on-gated-head` + `…-not-skip-ahead-ready-milestone` + parked/operator-defer facets) — this facet is a defect in the very oracle those rounds spun off to end the class. Verified correct model: merged head = higher-merged-priority of each pipeline's ACTUAL full-probe head = `managed-llm-credits` (the checkpoint's intended `next_route`).

**Action:**
  - NEEDS_INPUT.md written (hard-park carve-out — structural, nothing implemented): `docs/specs/turn-routing-enforcement/NEEDS_INPUT_2026-07-18-merged-head-oracle-cross-pipeline-context.md`. Decisions: (1) cross-pipeline/stateless merged-head classification mechanism — recommend "higher-priority-of-two-full-probe-heads" replacing L3's scoped-probe walk; (2) spike-pipeline-role interaction (spike-BLOCKED merged-dispatchable iff it is the pipeline's actual full-probe head). Grade `structural`: the fix revises a LOCKED decision (L3) of a COMPLETED feature, changes core cross-pipeline dispatch routing, and is coupled-pair mirrored across three sites — a wrong provisional pick silently mis-prioritizes work and overrides an operator-ratified baseline. The narrow facet-1-only patch was VERIFIED insufficient (deadlock moves to facet 2), so no partial mechanical fix was landed. Operator interim workaround documented + verified: `--park-blocked` breaks the deadlock (dispatches `inspector-track-dashboard`).

**Over-fit spin-off:** none NEW — the durable generalization is the `merged-head-actionability-oracle` feature itself (already COMPLETE); this round is a structural defect IN that oracle, hard-parked for operator ratification (a NEEDS_INPUT, not an over-fit patch). No literal-phrase-to-matcher append (nothing shipped). The recurring-class handback from Rounds 91/92 already named this oracle as the durable home; this round reports its remaining cross-pipeline-context hole.

**Reconciliation:** none — this round shipped no `docs/bugs/` FIX (pure structural hard-park). The round's own investigation spec `docs/bugs/merged-head-oracle-scoped-probe-blind-to-cross-pipeline-skip-context` is `**Status:** Concluded` with a `BLOCKED.md` (`blocker_kind: needs-operator-decision`) gating the bug pipeline until the NEEDS_INPUT is ratified — no fix committed, so nothing to archive/link.

**Intervention record:** none — pure hard-park round ships no change; per the SKILL an intervention record is captured only for a `Mechanical fix applied` / `Provisional design-fork resolved` action.

**Gates run:** none required — no production script/skill/hook/template was modified (docs-only: bug investigation spec + BLOCKED + NEEDS_INPUT sentinel + this log round). No coupled-pair or sentinel-schema code touched. Reproduction was via read-only in-process probes against the live AlgoBooth queue.

## Round 96 — 2026-07-18 — observed-friction

**Item in flight:** merged-head-actionability-oracle
**Divergence point:** the invariant gate battery itself — a cycle subagent running `pytest user/scripts/tests/test_lazy_core/` DURING a live `/lazy-batch` run (which cycle subagents do by design) got ~80 spurious `SystemExit(3)` failures in the `test_pseudo`/`test_misc` `apply_pseudo`/`mark_complete` family. Not a routing deny/no-route — an observed harness gap where the gate battery is not cleanly runnable mid-run.

**Root cause:** `script-defect` (test-harness isolation gap). `lazy_core.apply_pseudo` guards its entry with `refuse_if_cycle_active("apply_pseudo")` (`user/scripts/lazy_core/pseudo.py:482`) — its inline comment asserts *"In-process test callers run with no marker … → the guard is a silent no-op."* That assumption holds only under state-dir isolation. The ~80 failing tests call `apply_pseudo(Path(td), …)` with a `tempfile` REPO ROOT but do NOT isolate `LAZY_STATE_DIR`, so `claude_state_dir()` resolves to the REAL per-repo keyed dir `~/.claude/state/<repo_key>/`, which during a live run carries the cycle marker → `refuse_if_cycle_active` fires → `SystemExit(3)`. Reproduced live this round: `80 failed, 194 passed` for the two suites under the live marker; `1254 passed` for the full package once isolated. Violates the `user/scripts/CLAUDE.md` contributor convention ("isolate `LAZY_STATE_DIR`"). The existing ad-hoc queue stub `adhoc-lazy-core-tests-not-isolated-from-live-cycle-marker` (enqueued earlier this run) is the same defect; concluded its SPEC and fixed OUT-OF-PIPELINE.

**Action:**
  - Mechanical fix applied. `tests/test_lazy_core/_util.py` now seeds an isolated per-process temp `LAZY_STATE_DIR` via `os.environ.setdefault(...)` at the shared import chokepoint (imported by every shard in BOTH pytest and the standalone per-shard `__main__` runners), placed BEFORE `_ORIGINAL_LAZY_STATE_DIR` is captured so the `_clear_state_dir` restore path stays isolated too; an `atexit` rmtree cleans the temp dir. `setdefault` (never overwrite) preserves the documented operator `LAZY_STATE_DIR=<temp> python3 …` override. Structural single-chokepoint fix — not 80 per-test edits — covering the whole class (any in-process `refuse_if_cycle_active`-guarded call) and both invocation modes. Verified under the LIVE cycle marker: the two red suites → `274 passed` (was `80 failed`); full lazy_core package → `1254 passed`. `test_clear_state_dir_restores_process_launch_override` is unaffected (it monkeypatches `_util._ORIGINAL_LAZY_STATE_DIR` directly). harness-gate (`origin/main..HEAD`): `in_scope: false` (test/docs diff touches no control-surface glob) → no gate/matcher/threshold change, nothing to flag. Commit + push: `1684f20b` (bug spec `046c81af`).

**Over-fit spin-off:** none — structural chokepoint fix (isolation seam), not a literal-phrase-to-matcher append; `harness-gate` reports the diff out-of-scope (no matcher/keyword-set touched). No over-fit smell tripped.

  - SEPARATE DISCOVERED DEFECT (surfaced, NOT fixed — depth-1 cap + subagent Agent policy forbid a second harden dispatch): running the `test_hooks.py` gate this round exposed 22 pre-existing `test_containment_*` failures. Root cause: `lazy-cycle-containment.sh`'s inline python body `$_LCC_PY` is **33,575 bytes**, exceeding the Windows `CreateProcess` command-line limit of 32,767, so line 809's `"$PYTHON" -c "$_LCC_PY"` fails with E2BIG and the hook fail-opens (exit 0, no deny) — **silently disarming the containment guard on this Windows workstation**, with NO breadcrumb (E2BIG slips between the "no-python" bash fallback and the python-side `except`). NOT caused by this round (touches zero hooks; independent of the live marker and of env size ~3.7KB); a prior harden round (`cb666120`) grew the body past the limit. Captured as a drivable, auto-discovered bug: `docs/bugs/_archive/containment-hook-inline-python-exceeds-windows-cmdline-limit/SPEC.md` (`**Status:** Concluded`; proposed fix = feed the body via stdin/temp-file instead of `-c`, + a Windows deny regression, + a plane-wide sibling-hook body-size audit). Surfaced via the captured auto-discovered bug + the harden Return to the orchestrator (the dispatched subagent has no `PushNotification` tool — the orchestrator fires it at the harden-return seam).

## Round 97 — 2026-07-18 — observed-friction

**Item in flight:** containment-hook-inline-python-exceeds-windows-cmdline-limit
**Divergence point:** the `/lazy-batch` unified driver's `--emit-prompt` merged-head override — every bug probe (scoped `--bug-id` AND unscoped) returned `route_overridden_by: merged-head-diverged` with `merged_head: {block-terminal-kill-matches-separators-inside-quoted-args, bug}` and withheld `cycle_prompt`/`cycle_prompt_ref`/`cycle_model` (all null), so NO item could emit a dispatchable prompt → the run wedged.

**Root cause:** `script-defect` — `bug-state.py::_find_open_bug_dirs` omits the `Superseded` done-status filter that its feature-pipeline mirror `lazy-state.py::_find_open_feature_dirs` already has (`if status == "Superseded": continue`, receipt-exempt, `_find_open_feature_dirs:564`). Its done-status filter skipped only `Won't-fix` (bug-state.py:728) and receipted `Fixed`; a `**Status:** Superseded` dir fell straight through to `candidates.append(...)`. So the resolved-but-unarchived `docs/bugs/block-terminal-kill-matches-separators-inside-quoted-args` (Status: Superseded, carries `DEFERRED.md`, not archived) was auto-discovered as open work, entered `lazy_core.depdag.merged_worklist`, ranked as the highest-priority merged head, and — since no scoped/computed head ever equals it — fired the Round-54 `merged-head-diverged` withhold universally. The downstream actionability oracle (`dispatch.merged_head_nondispatchable_ids`, Round-57 generalization) does not catch it because for a SAME-pipeline bug probe it folds `probe_skipped_ids`+`parked` and breaks on the first same-pipeline id (`iid in same_ids`) WITHOUT scoped-probing — a Superseded dir is in neither list. The correct stop point is the LOADER, before the dir ever enters the work list, exactly as the feature side does.

**Action:**
  - Mechanical fix applied: brought `_find_open_bug_dirs` into parity with `_find_open_feature_dirs`. Added `BUG_STATUS_SUPERSEDED = "Superseded"` and an unconditional skip branch beside the existing `Won't-fix` branch (receipt-exempt, BEFORE the receipt-aware `Fixed` branch), so a `Superseded` bug dir never enters `bug_items`/`merged_worklist`/the merged head. Regression fixture `superseded-dir-excluded-from-pickup` added to the `bug-state.py --test` smoke harness (Superseded dir excluded; open control dir still returned — proves the filter is not over-broad); bug-state smoke baseline regenerated via the sanctioned `_normalize_smoke_output` helper (single-line diff — the new fixture line only). No gate weakened; no coupled-pair mirror owed (`load_queue`/`load_bug_queue` symmetry is explicitly NOT parity-audited — the fix CLOSES a pre-existing asymmetry); no sentinel schema touched. Verified the run is unblocked: `bug-state.py --bug-id containment-hook-inline-python-exceeds-windows-cmdline-limit --emit-prompt --probe` → `route_overridden_by: null`, `merged_head: null`, `sub_skill: plan-bug` (real cycle_prompt, model opus); `--next-merged` returns the actionable in-flight bug. Bug spec (Step 2.5) committed FIRST at `harden(docs): fb87bff1` (audit trail predates the fix). Commit + push: `04ecf963`.

**Over-fit spin-off:** none. The fix is STRUCTURAL — a new status-equality branch (`if status == BUG_STATUS_SUPERSEDED: continue`) mirroring the existing `Won't-fix` branch and the feature-side loader, NOT a literal appended to a matcher alternation/list/set (signal 1 N/A for the production change). `harness-gate.py --range origin/main..HEAD --json`: `gate_weakening: pass` (evidence empty — no gate removed/softened/bypassed), `overfit: flag` but every cited element is a TEST-FIXTURE string literal in the new smoke fixture (the `SPEC.md`/`DEFERRED.md` `.write_text(...)` content strings — `"**Status:** Superseded\n\n"` etc.), the documented false-positive class the detector keys on for string literals in test code (identical to Rounds 53/55/56); `complexity: net-new` (restores loader parity, retires no rule/surface); `scope_hit: [user/scripts/bug-state.py]`. The broader class (merged head pointing at a non-actionable item) ALREADY has its shipped generalization — `merged_head_nondispatchable_ids` (the Round-57 actionability oracle) + the `merged-head-actionability-oracle` feature — and THIS exact loader-parity gap was ALREADY the queued bug `adhoc-bug-pickup-routes-superseded-specs` (now fixed this round); manufacturing a new spin-off would duplicate the existing generalization. No new spin-off.

  - SEPARATE OBSERVATION (not a new defect — already captured): running the `test_hooks.py` gate this round reproduced the 22 pre-existing `test_containment_*` failures. These are the ALREADY-CAPTURED `containment-hook-inline-python-exceeds-windows-cmdline-limit` defect (Round 96 root-caused it: `lazy-cycle-containment.sh`'s inline python body exceeds the Windows CreateProcess 32,767-byte limit → E2BIG → hook fail-opens). ## Round 98 — 2026-07-18 — manual (operator-directed, inline)

**Item in flight:** concurrent-worktree-agent-coordination (live `/lazy-batch` run, paused via operator-authorized checkpoint to run this inline harden)
**Divergence point:** §1d dispatch/await — the orchestrator acted on GRANDCHILD (sub-sub-agent) `<task-notification>` events as if they were its OWN cycle's return, and `TaskStop`-killed two productive cycle subagents mid-work.

**Root cause:** `ambiguous-prose` / `missing-contract` — the `/lazy-batch` (and coupled `/lazy-bug-batch`, `/lazy-batch-cloud`) §1d prose implied a SYNCHRONOUS `Agent` return ("IMMEDIATELY after the Agent returns") and never told the orchestrator that (a) the cycle dispatch is ASYNC, delivering its result via a `<task-notification>` the orchestrator is re-invoked on, and (b) a cycle subagent's OWN sub-subagents' notifications BUBBLE UP to the top orchestrator session, not only to the cycle subagent that dispatched them. With no direct-child-vs-grandchild contract, the orchestrator applied its only heuristic — "a BLOCKED notification means my work failed" — to two grandchild Explore notifications and killed the direct spec cycle. Evidence: this session's kill notification for the direct child (`a67b27d4…`) revealed *"Both agents returned precise anchors … I have full grounding … draft the baseline SPEC.md"* — the killed cycle was productive; the two BLOCKED notifications (`af1772d5…`, `a9c766b9…`) were read-only Explore fan-outs the cycle subagent had dispatched (grandchildren), carrying task-ids the orchestrator never dispatched. Platform mechanics (grandchild-notification bubbling, task-id↔agentId correlation, and the `No tools needed for summary` wedge string) confirmed UNDOCUMENTED via `claude-code-guide`; the fix uses the task-id match as a POSITIVE signal with a WAIT default, never DEPENDING on the undocumented behavior. Bug spec (Step 2.5): `docs/bugs/_archive/orchestrator-misroutes-on-grandchild-subagent-notifications/` (committed FIRST at `harden(docs): c3be4165`, audit trail predates the fix).

**Action:**
  - Mechanical fix applied: (1) BUG 1 — new `§1d-await` subsection in `lazy-batch` / `lazy-bug-batch` / `lazy-batch-cloud` SKILL.md (coupled trio, mirrored): the `Agent` cycle dispatch is async; act ONLY on the DIRECT child's notification (task-id == the dispatched `agentId`, positive signal; WAIT default on any non-match/ambiguity). Grandchild (sub-sub-agent) notifications bubble up and are the CYCLE subagent's to handle — NEVER `--cycle-end`/probe/route/`TaskStop` on them; NEVER kill a cycle on a grandchild BLOCKED/failure (the only sanctioned `TaskStop` is an operator-directed pause). (2) BUG 2 — sub-sub-agent tool-wedge standing rule added to §1d.1 Trigger 5 (×3) + a `user/CLAUDE.md` auto-invoke pointer: a TOTAL tool-execution wedge is POST-HOC observed friction with a TRANSIENT carve-out (single wedge whose siblings/re-dispatch succeed, or a platform/API blip like the undocumented `No tools needed for summary` → do NOT harden; reproducible / ≥2×-recurring / non-platform → harden). The `No tools needed for summary` wedge ITSELF is PINNED as a platform-runtime transient — `grep` finds it nowhere in claude-config and it fires uniformly before every tool type (no per-tool `PreToolUse` hook could produce it), so it is not a claude-config surface and not fixable here. Gates run below. Commit + push: `ca7f2c8b`.

**Over-fit spin-off:** none — the fix adds STRUCTURAL prose contracts (direct-child-only await; a transient-carve-out wedge rule), NOT a literal-phrase-to-matcher (signal 1 N/A), and the class (`grandchild-notification-misroute`) is NEW (first occurrence — the ≥2 threshold for signals 2–4 is not met). `harness-gate.py --staged --json`: `gate_weakening: pass` (evidence empty — no gate removed/softened/bypassed), `overfit: pass` (evidence empty), `tautology: pass`, `complexity: declaration-required → net-new` (adds a missing await/notification contract, retires no rule/surface), `scope_hit: [lazy-batch/SKILL.md, lazy-bug-batch/SKILL.md]`. No mechanical enforcement is possible: task-notifications are delivered by the harness directly into the orchestrator's LLM context — no state script, hook, or registry ever observes them, so prose + judgment (biased to the safe non-intervention default) is the only available lever (recorded in the bug spec so a future round does not re-investigate looking for a script fix that cannot exist).

**Reconciliation:** done — inline manual `/harden-harness` (no cycle marker; the live run was checkpoint-paused before invoking the skill the operator typed). The round's own bug spec is FULLY resolved by this round (BUG 1 fixed; BUG 2 pinned + standing rule shipped). Wrote the hand `FIXED.md` receipt (`kind: fixed`, `provenance: backfilled-unverified`, cites `ca7f2c8b` + green gates), flipped `**Status:** Concluded → Fixed`, then `--archive-fixed` + `--link-provenance --commits ca7f2c8b`.

**Intervention record:** `docs/interventions/harden-2026-07-r98.md` — CAPTURED. Target signal `undeclared` (`baseline: not-computable`, INCONCLUSIVE-by-construction), expected-direction `decrease`, signal-independence `self-emitted / immeasurable`: this friction class (a spurious orchestrator `TaskStop` of a productive cycle over a grandchild notification) has NO countable ledger event — task-notifications never reach a state script — so an honest `undeclared` is declared rather than a fabricated measurable proxy.

## Round 99 — 2026-07-18 — observed-friction

**Item in flight:** concurrent-worktree-agent-coordination (feature `/lazy-batch` run; background harden, non-blocking)
**Divergence point:** TWO harness gaps observed mid-run (not a routing deny): (GAP 1) `lazy-state.py --emit-dispatch apply-resolution`'s decision-record lookup missing a decision the orchestrator DID record via `--record-decision`; (GAP 2) the `subagent-wedge-backstop.sh` SubagentStop hook BLOCKING a `/spec` cycle subagent's stop over a stray plan.

**Root cause:** `script-defect` (GAP 1) + `hook-defect` (GAP 2).
- GAP 1 — `lazy_core/ledgers.py::_normalize_sentinel_key` derived its dict key with `os.path.normpath(...).replace("\\","/")`. Both writer (`record_decision`) and reader (`read_decision_record` via `bind_decision_record_context`) call this SAME helper, but `normpath` collapses separators/`.`/`..` WITHOUT absolutizing — so a decision recorded with a repo-relative `docs/features/<f>/NEEDS_INPUT.md` (key `docs/features/<f>/NEEDS_INPUT.md`) silently missed an emit passing the absolute Windows path (key `C:/.../docs/features/<f>/NEEDS_INPUT.md`), yielding `no recorded decision for sentinel` and forcing the orchestrator to guess the path form. The helper's own docstring FALSELY promised "relative vs absolute ... still round-trips." (The dispatch's framing "record keys raw, emit normalizes" is imprecise — both normalize identically; the shared normalizer is simply too weak.)
- GAP 2 — `subagent-wedge-backstop.sh`'s `_active_plan_unchecked` resolved "the active plan" by globbing EVERY `docs/{features,bugs}/*/plans/*.md` and counting unchecked WU checkboxes in any non-terminal plan (`glob.glob` + `_plan_wu_checkbox_counts`). A `/spec`/research/realign cycle owns no `/execute-plan` plan, but a stray non-terminal `plans/*.md` (a `plans/realign-2026-07-18.md`, a prior part's plan) made `active` non-empty, and the git-dirty half of the predicate (a `/spec` cycle writes SPEC.md) then tripped the block. The just-stopped cycle's real plan identity WAS available on disk: the cycle marker (`lazy-cycle-active.json`, present at SubagentStop — cleared only later by `--cycle-end`) carries `sub_skill` + `sub_skill_args`.

**Action:**
  - Mechanical fix applied: (GAP 1) `_normalize_sentinel_key` now absolutizes via `os.path.abspath` (both callers run from the run's repo-root cwd) before the forward-slash normalization, so a relative record and an absolute lookup map to ONE key; same-spelling round-trip preserved (abspath idempotent on absolute, deterministic on relative from a fixed cwd); `abspath` not `realpath` (a sentinel lives in the repo working tree, never behind a `~/.claude/*` skill symlink). (GAP 2) `_active_plan_unchecked` now reads the cycle marker (`lazy_core.read_cycle_marker`) and counts unchecked WUs in ONLY the plan the active cycle is executing — `sub_skill == "execute-plan"` + the `sub_skill_args` plan path (resolved against `repo_root`); a non-execute-plan cycle (or absent/unreadable marker) resolves NO active plan (empty) → the caller's `if not active: _allow()` biases to false-negative, so a stray `plans/*.md` never false-fires. A genuine execute-plan wedge (dirty tree OR its own plan's unchecked WUs) still BLOCKS once. Removed the now-unused `import glob`. Regression tests: `test_record_decision_key_reconciles_relative_and_absolute` (test_ledgers.py); `test_wedge_non_execute_cycle_ignores_stray_plan_allows` + `test_wedge_execute_plan_scoped_plan_wu_blocks_on_clean_tree` (test_hooks.py); six existing wedge block-path tests updated to name the plan via a cycle marker (they implicitly relied on glob-all — NOT a weakening: setup added, no test deleted, no threshold softened). Root `CLAUDE.md` wedge-backstop row predicate description updated to the scoped form. Bug specs committed FIRST (`harden(docs): b066f1bf`, audit trail predates the fix). Commit + push: `bd0948bc`.

**Over-fit spin-off:** none — both fixes are STRUCTURAL, not literal-phrase-to-matcher (GAP 1 swaps `normpath`→`abspath`, a function change; GAP 2 replaces a repo-wide glob with a cycle-marker-scoped read — proven by the `ledgers.py` diff), so signal 1 is N/A; neither root-cause class has recurred in the log (`_normalize_sentinel_key` first occurrence; this is the first hardening round fixing a DEFECT in the shipped wedge hook — prior wedge mentions are the feature that SHIPPED it), so the ≥2 threshold for signals 2–4 is not met; signal 3 N/A (the fixes handle the whole class — any relative/absolute spelling; any non-execute-plan cycle + any stray plan — not just the observed instance). `harness-gate.py --range origin/main..HEAD --json`: `gate_weakening_hit: false` (no gate removed/softened/bypassed), `overfit: flag` = **FALSE POSITIVE** (same documented class as Rounds 91 and the 981191ae round: all evidence lines are a Python docstring `"""` delimiter in the hook, the CLAUDE.md `|`-delimited doc-TABLE row, an incident-shaped TEST-fixture path `docs/features/wedge-feat/plans/plan.md`, and test assertion/tuple string literals — NONE a production matcher/allow-list append), `tautology: pass`, `scope_hit: [subagent-wedge-backstop.sh, lazy_core/ledgers.py]`, `verdict_required: true` (advisory recording, not a block — mechanical fix landed first, run never blocked; judgment recorded here). PushNotification: not applicable (no queued spin-off item).

**Reconciliation:** WHOLE handback → orchestrator, `**Status:** Concluded` LEFT UNTOUCHED (the sanctioned `docs/bugs/CLAUDE.md` fallback, stated explicitly). Both bug slugs are FULLY resolved by the fix (`bd0948bc`), but this dispatched harden meta-cycle CANNOT commit their `docs/bugs/<slug>/` reconciliation artifacts: the marker-armed `lazy-cycle-containment.sh` **second-feature commit tripwire** denies any staged `docs/(features|bugs)/<slug>/` path that is not a carve-out for the ACTIVE dispatch's `feature_id` (`concurrent-worktree-agent-coordination`), and a harden bug slug is never that feature (`_is_carve_out` exempts only the marker's own feature dir + `ingest-research` batch-docs writers — not a `sub_skill: hardening` cycle). Committing a `FIXED.md` receipt or a `Concluded → Fixed` flip there would require defeating that guard, which is prohibited (never fight a gate). So I reverted my inline receipt/flip (bug specs restored to `Concluded`, uncommitted `FIXED.md` removed — no stranded `unarchived-fixed` debt) and hand the WHOLE reconciliation back. Orchestrator (marker cleared after `--cycle-end` → no containment) or the bug pipeline runs, for EACH of `adhoc-decision-key-relative-absolute-mismatch` and `adhoc-subagent-wedge-hook-overfires-globs-all-plans`: write `FIXED.md` (`kind: fixed`, `provenance: backfilled-unverified`, cite `bd0948bc` + green gates) + flip `**Status:** Concluded → Fixed`, then `python3 user/scripts/bug-state.py --repo-root . --archive-fixed docs/bugs/<slug>` and `python3 user/scripts/lazy-state.py --link-provenance --id <slug> --commits bd0948bc`. **Harness-gap note (NOT re-dispatched — depth-1 cap; surfaced for the operator):** a `sub_skill: hardening` cycle legitimately authors its OWN `docs/bugs/<harden-slug>/` SPEC + FIXED receipt, but the second-feature tripwire has no `hardening` carve-out — so a harden round's bug-spec/receipt commits are guard-denied whenever the marker is armed to a DIFFERENT host feature. (This round's earlier bug-spec commit `b066f1bf` landed only because the async orchestrator had the marker in a different state at that instant — a race, not a stable allowance.) A future harden round should evaluate adding `hardening` to the `_batch_docs_writer` / carve-out set (scoped to `docs/bugs/**` only), OR routing harden bug-doc commits through a sanctioned path.

**Intervention record:** `docs/interventions/harden-2026-07-r99.md` — target signal `undeclared` (`baseline: not-computable`, INCONCLUSIVE-by-construction), expected-direction `decrease`, signal-independence `self-emitted / immeasurable`: neither friction's recurrence maps to the closed `_INTERVENTION_EVENT_VOCABULARY` — GAP 2's wedge false-fire surfaces as a `hook-events.jsonl` `kind:block` (subagent-wedge-backstop) and GAP 1's decision miss as an emit `dispatch_prompt_refused`, both OUTSIDE the intervention-event vocabulary the efficacy evaluator reads — so a typed `undeclared` is the honest classification rather than a mismatched `event:` proxy. (Capture deferred to the harden-return seam if `--record-intervention` is cycle-refused for this dispatched meta-cycle — see Return `reconcile`/notes.)

**Gates run:**

## Round 100 — 2026-07-18 — observed-friction

**Item in flight:** concurrent-worktree-agent-coordination (feature `/lazy-batch` run; blocking observed-friction — orchestrator awaited this harden in the foreground before re-probing)
**Divergence point:** cycle-dispatch contract, `@section workstation-dispatch` of `user/skills/_components/lazy-batch-prompts/cycle-base-prompt.md` (the sub-sub-agent dispatch policy auto-refreshed into every emitted workstation cycle prompt). A plan-feature cycle subagent (`a911…`) dispatched three spec-phases capability/reuse audit sub-sub-agents; all three grandchildren wedged on the depth-2 `No tools needed for summary` platform limitation; the cycle subagent announced *"I'll wait for the two remaining audit agents"* and TERMINATED without drafting PHASES.md, stranding the feature at Step 6 with `step_repeat_count` climbing toward the oscillation tripwire. Sibling `/spec`, `/realign-spec`, Phase-2 cycles the SAME run had their grandchildren wedge identically but fell back to inline reads and completed.

**Root cause:** `missing-contract` — the `workstation-dispatch` section authorizes `Agent` fan-out and carries a `SYNCHRONOUS AWAIT` guardrail, but that guardrail only covers the child→parent SendMessage deadlock ("never wait on a message FROM a child"). It had NO contract for the case where an AWAITED dispatch RETURNS a total tool-execution wedge (every tool call erroring before executing). With no explicit directive, the cycle subagent mapped "grandchildren produced no usable output" to "keep waiting" rather than "the fan-out failed — do this work INLINE myself (depth-1 tools work)." Round 98 (`ca7f2c8b`, `grandchild-notification-misroute`) fixed the ORCHESTRATOR side (don't misroute/`TaskStop` over a bubbled grandchild notification) + the harden-auto-invoke wedge-classification rule, but never touched the cycle subagent's OWN dispatch contract — this is the distinct, uncovered parent-of-the-wedged-grandchildren seam. Platform behavior (depth-2 wedge, grandchild bubbling, the `No tools needed for summary` string) is UNDOCUMENTED (confirmed via `claude-code-guide` in Round 98 and pinned there as a platform-runtime transient); this fix is RESILIENCE to it (fall back to inline) and does NOT depend on the undocumented behavior — the recommended posture. Bug spec (Step 2.5): `docs/bugs/_archive/cycle-subagent-stalls-on-wedged-sub-subagent/SPEC.md` (`**Status:** Concluded`), committed FIRST at `harden(docs): 56c37dd0` (audit trail predates the fix).

**Action:**
  - Mechanical fix applied: added a `WEDGE RESILIENCE` guardrail to `@section workstation-dispatch` (`modes=workstation`, `pipelines=feature,bug`, `skills=all` — one shared-component edit covers both pipelines; cloud is resilient by construction via `@section cloud-override`'s inline mandate). Directive: a dispatched sub-sub-agent that returns a total tool-execution wedge is NOT waited on and NOT re-dispatched (it wedges identically) — the cycle subagent performs that work INLINE with its own depth-1 Read/Grep/Glob/Bash and still produces the skill's deliverable (PHASES.md / plan / tested code). Names the fan-out skills that would otherwise strand (spec-phases audits, plan-feature / spec-phases(-batch) / write-plan Sonnet fan-out, /execute-plan test/impl split) and equates "waiting for the remaining wedged agents" to the forbidden child-message-wait state above. No `{token}` residue introduced (prose is brace-free). No coupled-pair SKILL mirror owed (the emitter reads this one template for both pipelines; not a `/lazy-batch` ↔ `/lazy-bug-batch` SKILL.md change). No sentinel schema touched. `harness-gate.py --staged --json`: `in_scope: false` (skill-component prose edit touches no control-surface glob — no matcher/gate/threshold change to flag). Commit + push: `e7c2b89e`.

**Over-fit spin-off:** none — the fix adds a STRUCTURAL prose contract (an inline-fallback directive covering the whole depth-2-wedge class), NOT a literal-phrase-to-matcher (signal 1 N/A — nothing appended to any regex/list/set), and the class is distinct from Round 98's: different component/symbol (`cycle-base-prompt.md workstation-dispatch` vs the `/lazy-batch` §1d SKILL prose) and different actor (the cycle SUBAGENT's resilience vs the ORCHESTRATOR's routing), so the ≥2-same-class threshold for signals 2–4 is not met. `harness-gate` reports the diff out-of-scope. No spin-off manufactured.

## Round 101 — 2026-07-19 — no-route

**Item in flight:** byref-updatedinput-unapplied-on-background-agent-dispatch
**Divergence point:** bug-pipeline `--emit-prompt` `merged-head-diverged` withhold — the exclude set built by `lazy_core.dispatch.merged_head_nondispatchable_ids` OMITTED the parked merged head (byref, highest severity), so `next_merged` kept byref the head and every probe (merged AND scoped-to-adhoc-harness-gate) withheld `cycle_prompt_ref` behind an undriveable head → park-mode deadlock; the run could not reach `queue-exhausted-all-parked` and the next-priority dispatchable bug (adhoc-harness-gate, `/spec-bug`) was never routed.

**Root cause:** script-defect — `merged_head_nondispatchable_ids`'s same-pipeline fast-path `if iid in same_ids: break` (`dispatch.py`) assumed ANY same-pipeline item ranked above the emitted item was dispatchable "by the probe's own choice". That holds only when the emit probe's queue-order `compute_state` walk reached and classified every higher-priority same-pipeline item. byref wrote a **structural-divergence `NEEDS_INPUT.md` mid-`/execute-plan`** (Phase 1 landed, Phase 2 halted); its SCOPED probe classifies `needs-input-scoped`/parked correctly, but the emit walk returned adhoc-harness-gate as current BEFORE reaching byref, so byref was absent from `state["parked"]` (`parked: []`) and from `probe_skipped_ids` → not folded into `exclude` → hit the `same_ids` fast-path as a "dispatchable head". Discovering byref's parked state requires per-item scoped re-inference the fast-path skipped. The already-correct stateless `--next-merged` path (`same_pipeline_state=None` + a TYPE-AWARE probe) scope-probes every candidate and excludes byref — the two divergent oracle-walk implementations were the defect. Recurrence of `merged-head-includes-parked-items-deadlocks-park-run` on the bug pipeline / mid-execute-plan root-NEEDS_INPUT case.

**Action:**
  - Mechanical fix applied: removed the `same_ids` fast-path in `merged_head_nondispatchable_ids` so the walk classifies EVERY unreached candidate (cross- and same-pipeline) via scoped `is_dispatchable` re-inference — making the emit-path walk IDENTICAL to the stateless `--next-merged` walk (probe-decided parked/skipped items stay folded into `exclude` and dropped from the worklist, so L2's ordering-context invariant is preserved for reached items). Made all three emit-path `scoped_probe` callables TYPE-AWARE via an id→type map (bug-state merged-override; lazy-state research-halt + merged-override), mirroring the stateless `_nm_scoped_probe`. New regression `test_merged_head_nondispatchable_ids_excludes_parked_UNREACHED_same_pipeline_head` (parked unreached head excluded → no withhold; dispatchable head NOT excluded → withhold still fires). Gates: full `lazy_core` pytest 1278/1278, `test_hooks.py` 268/268, `lazy-state.py --test` + `bug-state.py --test` OK, `lint-skills.py --check-projected --check-capabilities` OK, `lazy_parity_audit.py` exit 0, `bug-state.py --fsck` ok. `harness-gate.py` verdict (recorded here — the per-item `GATE_VERDICT.md` could not be committed, see Reconciliation; `harness-gate.py --range origin/main..HEAD --json`): `gate_weakening: pass` (no gate removed/softened/bypassed), `complexity: declared` (retires the `same_ids` fast-path — the divergent membership short-circuit is DELETED, not appended to; two oracle-walk implementations collapse to one), `tautology: pass`, `overfit: flag-justified` (FALSE POSITIVE — the checker matched a quoted JSON string `"route_overridden_by":"merged-head-diverged"` inside the SPEC's probe-example, NOT a literal appended to a code matcher; the CODE change REMOVES a membership construct). `scope_hit`: dispatch.py + both state scripts. **Item in flight:** adhoc-harness-gate-gate-weakening-blind-to-cross-file-construct-move (the dispatchable bug the withhold suppressed; the operator-deferred head was `native-android-pipeline-steering`)

Round 57 (`merged-head-excludes-parked-not-operator-deferred-deadlocks`, `c5a3b385`) had fixed exactly this with a pure file-predicate (`docmodel.spec_dir_operator_deferred`, True iff `DEFERRED.md`) inside an UNCONDITIONAL merged-head exclusion (`nondispatchable_item_ids`) that ran over every candidate regardless of owning pipeline. The `merged-head-actionability-oracle` refactor RETIRED that file-predicate, replacing it with per-candidate scoped `is_dispatchable` re-inference under the premise "any truthy `terminal_reason` ⇒ non-dispatchable, so the oracle covers every category" — TRUE for a BUG candidate (`bug-state.py` surfaces `terminal_reason: operator-deferred`), FALSE for a cross-pipeline FEATURE (the signal is invisible to the probe the oracle trusts). Type-agnostic (feature AND bug candidates), applied at the single oracle both pipelines' merged-head paths + the stateless `--next-merged` path share, so the bug-side and feature-side merged heads exclude operator-deferred features identically. ## Round 104 — 2026-07-19 — observed-friction (batched gap 2 of 2)

**Item in flight:** canary-band-only-trip-auto-enqueues-without-attribution
**Divergence point:** `efficacy-eval.py --canary` trip consequence — `run_canary` fired the revert-triage enqueue on ANY `ev["trip"]`, where `trip = band.trip OR incident_trip`. A band-only aggregate swing of a high-volume SELF-EMITTED signal (e.g. `event:containment-refusal`) with ZERO surface attribution auto-enqueued a `canary-revert-<id>` bug stub (observed: 20 open canaries, 728 unattributed / 0 attributed, ~11 noise stubs in one cycle).

**Root cause:** `script-defect` — the band trip (`_canary_band_trip`) is a pure aggregate-rate comparison vs the frozen baseline with no confound guard; the attribution signal (`_canary_attribute`) is computed but consumed ONLY by the separate `incident_trip` (≥2 attributed). So a band-only trip auto-enqueued with no attribution/independence corroboration. For a self-emitted signal the shipped change can only REDUCE the signal on its OWN path, so an unattributed aggregate swing is confounded (not caused by the change).

**Action:**
  - Mechanical fix applied: split trip DETECTION (always surfaced — D4 preserved) from auto-ENQUEUE via a new `_canary_should_enqueue(band, incident_trip, attributed, meta)` guard. Enqueue iff: an incident trip (≥2 attributed) OR — for a band-only trip — the signal's `signal_independence` starts with "independent" OR ≥1 fresh incident attributes to the change's own surface. A band-only trip on a non-independent (self-emitted/mixed/undeclared) signal with zero attribution is SUPPRESSED: surfaced in `run_canary`'s new `payload.suppressed[]` + `suppressed_notify`, the record left OPEN (never closed, never consequence-fired — re-surfaces until attribution appears or the operator acts). NOTHING reverted (D4). Keys on structural signals, never a signal id. 3 new tests in `test_efficacy_eval.py`: self-emitted-zero-attribution suppressed / independent-signal still enqueues / self-emitted-with-1-attribution enqueues. Commit + push: `9aa8f8a5`. Bug spec (Step 2.5, committed FIRST): `docs/bugs/_archive/canary-band-only-trip-auto-enqueues-without-attribution/`.
  - Design choice surfaced (not provisionalized — operator directed the fix and offered "guard OR tune the band"): chose the structural attribution/independence guard over a magic-number band widening (a wider band still fires on a large enough unattributed swing). Recorded in the bug SPEC's Locked Decisions; band-tuning remains an orthogonal future option. `efficacy-eval.py` is NOT on `docs/gate/control-surfaces.json`, so this change is `in_scope: false` for `harness-gate.py` (no GATE_VERDICT required); the guard is structural by construction.

**Over-fit spin-off:** none — the fix is structural (a confound predicate over the already-computed attribution + declared independence), not a literal-phrase patch, and this class (canary trip sensitivity) has not recurred in the hardening log.

**Reconciliation:** done — inline manual (no run marker active): `FIXED.md` receipt written, `**Status:** Concluded → Fixed`, `--archive-fixed` + `--link-provenance --commits 9aa8f8a5` run.

**Intervention record:** `docs/interventions/harden-2026-07-r104.md` (`target_signal: undeclared` — the efficacy is reduced canary noise-stub auto-enqueue volume, a bug-queue metric with no ledger-event proxy in the closed intervention vocabulary; recorded typed + retro-visible, INCONCLUSIVE-by-construction).

**Gates run:**
  test_lazy_core.py: 1300/1300
  test_hooks.py: pass
  test_efficacy_eval.py: 53/53
  lint-skills.py: OK
  lazy-state.py --test: OK
  bug-state.py --test: OK
  lazy_parity_audit.py: exit 0
  bug-state.py --fsck: ok

## Round 105 — 2026-07-19 — observed-friction

**Item in flight:** adhoc-orchestrator-redundant-recovery-on-background-suite-reinvoke (run context; this round's subject is the operator's global-attribution directive)
**Divergence point:** Not a routing deny/no-route — an operator-directed config gap surfaced mid-run: Claude's commit/PR attribution trailers (Co-Authored-By / Generated-with / Claude-Session) were still emitted universally because the user-scope `settings.json` never carried the platform toggle that suppresses them.

## Round 107 — 2026-07-19 — observed-friction

**Item in flight:** adhoc-orchestrator-redundant-recovery-on-background-suite-reinvoke
**Divergence point:** SubagentStop wedge-backstop (`subagent-wedge-backstop.sh`) — a dispatched grandchild's stop was BLOCKED even though its own 3 changed files were already committed+landed; the block fired on the DIRTY-TREE half of the wedge predicate, which read the WHOLE repo tree via `git status --porcelain`, NOT scoped to the stopping agent's own changed paths.

**Root cause:** hook-defect — `subagent-wedge-backstop.sh::_git_dirty(repo_root)` (embedded python) returned `bool(git status --porcelain)` over the entire tree, so under the sanctioned concurrent-writer regime (user/CLAUDE.md `<orchestration>`) a FOREIGN lane's uncommitted residue — a `docs/features/<other>/IMPLEMENTED.md` / the shared `docs/provenance-index.json` left by a concurrent mark-complete/mark-fixed cycle — made the tree dirty and false-fired the block on an agent that had genuinely finished its own work. Distinct facet from `adhoc-subagent-wedge-hook-overfires-globs-all-plans` (Round 99, which scoped the plan-WU half): this is the git-dirty half, the last repo-wide input in the same predicate. Blocks at most once (loop-guard intact), so latent/non-blocking, but reproducible on every concurrent run.

**Action:**
  - Mechanical fix applied: replaced `_git_dirty(repo_root)` with `_own_work_dirty(repo_root, own_item_dir)` (+ helpers `_own_item_dir` deriving the cycle's own `docs/{features,bugs}/<slug>` from the cycle-marker execute-plan plan path, and `_porcelain_path`). STRUCTURAL rule (no incident-literal filename denylist): a dirty path under `docs/` that is NOT under the active cycle's own item dir is concurrent-lane residue (ignored); every non-`docs/` (source) path and the cycle's own item dir counts as OWN pending work — genuine own-source wedge detection preserved. `_active_plan_unchecked` now returns `(list, plan_path)` so `main()` can derive the own item dir. Fail-OPEN posture + block-at-most-once loop-guard unchanged. Root `CLAUDE.md` hooks-table predicate prose updated in lockstep. Gates run: test_hooks.py 280/280 (3 new `test_wedge_*`), test_lazy_core 1300 passed, lazy-state.py/bug-state.py --test OK, bug-state --fsck ok, lint-skills.py OK. Commit + push: `4a12e218`. Bug spec: `docs/bugs/_archive/subagent-wedge-backstop-dirty-tree-predicate-repo-wide/` (commit `43d4ac93`).
  - harness-gate.py (`bda4441b..HEAD`, over-fit checker): `overfit: pass`, `gate_weakening: pass` (structural rule, no matcher-literal append, no gate weakened), `tautology: pass`; `complexity: declaration-required` (verdict_required, exit 1) — expected for an in-scope control-surface diff; `/harden-harness` is never blocked by this gate (blocking authority lives only at the completion-gate ship seam). `retires:` rationale: retires the whole-tree `_git_dirty` predicate, replaced by the own-item-dir-scoped `_own_work_dirty` (net structure-preserving, one predicate input rescoped, no new gate/surface).

**Over-fit spin-off:** none — the fix changes STRUCTURE, not a phrase (harness-gate `overfit: pass`). The predicate-scoping class HAS now recurred twice (Round 99 plan-WU half + this git-dirty half, same component, same "repo-wide predicate not scoped to the cycle's own work" family), but the wedge predicate has exactly TWO inputs and BOTH are now cycle-scoped, so the class is closed by construction — there is no remaining un-scoped input / near-neighbor to generalize. Spinning off a `/spec-bug` for a non-existent third input would be the speculative rewrite the generalization bound forbids ("draw the boundary tighter; do not manufacture a spurious spin-off"). Recurrence recorded here so a future third un-scoped input added to this predicate is an unambiguous trigger.

**Reconciliation:** handback → orchestrator: `subagent-wedge-backstop-dirty-tree-predicate-repo-wide` — hand `FIXED.md` receipt written (`kind: fixed`, `provenance: backfilled-unverified`, citing fix commit `4a12e218` + green regression evidence) + `**Status:** Concluded → Fixed` flipped; the two orchestrator-only ops are handed back for the harden-return seam (`/lazy-batch(-bug-batch)` §1d.1): `python3 user/scripts/bug-state.py --repo-root . --archive-fixed docs/bugs/subagent-wedge-backstop-dirty-tree-predicate-repo-wide` and `python3 user/scripts/lazy-state.py --link-provenance --id subagent-wedge-backstop-dirty-tree-predicate-repo-wide --commits 4a12e218`.

**Intervention record:** none — the wedge-backstop `block`/false-fire is emitted ONLY to `hook-events.jsonl` (kind `block`), which is NOT a member of the closed `_INTERVENTION_EVENT_VOCABULARY`; no measurable `event:<type>` target fits (the friction is not a deny-ledger `gate-refusal`/`containment-refusal`). Additionally, `--record-intervention` is orchestrator-only (`refuse_if_cycle_active`) and this is a DISPATCHED harden (a cycle marker is active), so the CLI would be refused (exit 3) — recording is deliberately skipped, per the dispatch steer.

## Round 108 — 2026-07-19 — observed-friction

**Item in flight:** hydra-overlay
**Divergence point:** SubagentStop wedge-backstop (`subagent-wedge-backstop.sh`) — during the `hydra-overlay` phase-8.5 `execute-plan` cycle it BLOCKED (exit 2) 3 correctly-scoped, non-committing WU sub-subagents (great-grandchildren the integrator dispatched via the workstation sub-subagent split). The now-cycle-scoped predicate cannot tell WHICH agent under the shared cycle marker is stopping (integrator vs nested worker).

**Root cause:** hook-defect + missing-contract — Rounds 99 (`adhoc-subagent-wedge-hook-overfires-globs-all-plans`, plan-WU half) and 107 (`subagent-wedge-backstop-dirty-tree-predicate-repo-wide`, git-dirty half) scoped BOTH predicate inputs to the active cycle via the cycle marker, closing the PATH/plan axis. This is a DISTINCT axis — AGENT IDENTITY. The cycle marker is a cycle-level object: the integrator AND every nested WU worker stop under the same marker, naming the same non-terminal plan with the same unchecked WUs, so `plan_pending` (`subagent-wedge-backstop.sh::_active_plan_unchecked`) is UNAVOIDABLY true for any worker stopping mid-cycle (the integrator ticks only after workers return), and the two states are byte-identical on disk. Discrimination needs agent lineage, which the harness lacks at SubagentStop: only `agent_id` is documented+stable and it carries NO parent/depth (`subagent-wedge-backstop-hook/RESEARCH_SUMMARY.md`; hook header); `agent_id` is hook-input-only (`markers.py` ~L2388–2394); `worker_subdispatch` events key the worker's dispatch `tool_use_id`, uncorrelated to the stopping `agent_id`. Whether SubagentStop exposes any lineage field is undocumented in-repo and confirming it needs a `claude-code-guide` dispatch — prohibited to the marked-run harden agent. Root 107 explicitly predicted "a future third un-scoped input… is an unambiguous trigger." Non-blocking (loop-guard bounds the block to once per `agent_id`; each worker proceeds on its second stop).

**Action:**
  - NEEDS_INPUT.md written (hard-park carve-out — structural + unconfirmed-platform dependency; nothing implemented): `docs/specs/turn-routing-enforcement/NEEDS_INPUT_2026-07-19-wedge-backstop-integrator-vs-worker-identity.md`. Decision: `wedge-backstop-integrator-vs-worker-identity` (`divergence: structural`). Three recommendation-first options — A (RECOMMENDED): self-managed integrator-`agent_id` breadcrumb (a PreToolUse seam records the FIRST `agent_id` under each cycle-marker generation as the integrator; wedge blocks only when stopping `agent_id` == recorded integrator; non-platform-dependent, uses the serial-tool-call ordering the consumed-fence already relies on; structural). B: platform lineage field (blocked on `claude-code-guide` confirmation; Round-81 rule forbids shipping on assumption). C: broad `subagent_model` exemption (one line, non-dependent, but never blocks an execute-plan integrator wedge — the hook's PRIMARY target — so coverage-reducing). Why hard-park not park-provisional: every viable option is structural, coverage-reducing, or platform-unconfirmed; the friction is non-blocking so no interim degradation is warranted. Bug spec: `docs/bugs/_archive/subagent-wedge-backstop-blocks-nested-wu-workers/SPEC.md` (Status: Concluded — root cause proven, fix operator-parked). Committed under `harden(docs):`.

**Over-fit spin-off:** none — no landed fix to generalize (hard-park). This is the 3rd false-fire of the wedge-backstop predicate class, but on a NEW axis (agent identity) orthogonal to the two path/plan-scoping facets Rounds 99+107 closed; the NEEDS_INPUT deliberately frames the GENERAL problem (integrator-vs-worker identity), i.e. the park IS the structural generalization the over-fit reflex would demand — not a third narrow patch. A separate `/spec-bug` spin-off for the same class the park already owns would be redundant.

**Reconciliation:** none — this round shipped no `docs/bugs/` FIX (pure hard-park). The round's own bug spec (`subagent-wedge-backstop-blocks-nested-wu-workers`) stays `Status: Concluded` with its fix explicitly operator-parked (the Concluded-with-fix-SHIPPED limbo the reconcile step guards does NOT apply — nothing shipped); the bug pipeline / operator resolves it via the NEEDS_INPUT.

**Intervention record:** none — pure hard-park NEEDS_INPUT round; nothing shipped, so no intervention is recorded (Step 4: intervention records are for `Mechanical fix applied` / `Provisional design-fork resolved` rounds only). The measurable target signal for the eventual fix (the wedge `block` false-fire count on execute-plan cycles) will be declared when the operator-blessed follow-on fix ships.

## Round 110 — 2026-07-19 — observed-friction

**Item in flight:** hydra-overlay
**Divergence point:** /execute-plan Step 1a.6a (dispatch class: `skill-execute-plan`, a strict-order `Plan series` prerequisite audit). Cycle-3's dispatch of hydra-overlay `part-12` ran the prose-driven strict-order prerequisite audit, ordered the sibling parts by RAW part-number, and treated `part-10` as an unmet prerequisite (`10 < 12`) — writing `docs/features/visuals/hydra-overlay/BLOCKED.md` (`blocker_kind: prerequisite-part-incomplete`) — even though the operator had rescheduled `part-10` to run LAST via `series_index: 15` and part-12's real entry criterion (Phase 11 preset schema/manager) was satisfied.

**Root cause:** ambiguous-prose. The strict-order prerequisite audit has NO script that computes the prerequisite SET — it is a prose instruction executed by the /execute-plan subagent (`execute-plan/SKILL.md` rule 1a.6a #1, line 73) and mirrored in the orchestrator's cycle prompt (`_components/lazy-batch-prompts/cycle-base-prompt.md`, workstation §skill-execute-plan lines 317-322 + cloud §skill-execute-plan-cloud lines 344-349). Neither prose site DEFINED which order determines "earlier"/"prerequisite" for a strict-order series, so the subagent defaulted to raw part-number / filename order and never consulted the frontmatter `series_index:` reschedule. The ROUTING primitive is NOT at fault: `_plan_series_index` (`lazy_core/docmodel.py:620`) reads frontmatter `series_index` first — `yaml.safe_load` strips the inline `# RESCHEDULED …` comment — so `_plan_sort_key` already orders part-12 (series 12) before part-10 (series 15). Verified empirically this round: `series_index(part-10)=15`, `series_index(part-12)=12`, `sort_key(part-12) < sort_key(part-10)`. Only the audit prose lagged the ordering primitive.

**Action:**
  - Mechanical fix applied: defined prerequisite-ness for a strict-order series by `series_index` execution order (frontmatter-honored, the same order `find_implementation_plans`/`_plan_sort_key` route by) — a sibling P is a prerequisite of the dispatched part D iff `series_index(P) < series_index(D)`; a part rescheduled to a HIGHER `series_index` is NOT a prerequisite of a lower-`series_index` part even when its filename `-part-K` number is lower; raw-part-number fallback when no `series_index` (no regression for un-rescheduled series). Rewrote `execute-plan/SKILL.md` rule 1a.6a #1; mirrored (coupled-prose lockstep) in `cycle-base-prompt.md` workstation + cloud `skill-execute-plan[-cloud]` sections; added a producer note to the `write-plan/SKILL.md` `Plan series` preamble ("in order" = `series_index` order). Regression test `test_rescheduled_high_series_index_part_not_prerequisite_of_lower` (`tests/test_lazy_core/test_docmodel.py`, registered in `_TESTS`) encodes the exact hydra-overlay scenario incl. the inline `# RESCHEDULED` YAML comment, asserting the rescheduled high-`series_index` part sorts AFTER (is not a prerequisite of) the lower-`series_index` later-part-numbered part. Bug spec (Step 2.5): `docs/bugs/_archive/execute-plan-strict-order-prereq-ignores-series-index-reschedule/SPEC.md` (committed under `harden(docs):` first, `57b07fe5`). Gates: pytest `tests/test_lazy_core/` 1312/1312, test_hooks.py 284/284, lint-skills.py --check-projected --check-capabilities OK, lazy-state.py/bug-state.py --test OK, bug-state --fsck clean. Commit + push: `9ce3b8f1`.

**Over-fit spin-off:** none. `harness-gate.py --range origin/main..HEAD`: `in_scope: false`, `scope_hit: []`, no `overfit`/`gate_weakening` findings — the diff is prose + a test addition, touching no matcher/gate surface. Manual check confirms: signal 1 (literal-phrase-to-matcher) NO — the fix defines prerequisite-ness by the existing ordering primitive, not a phrase appended to a matcher; signal 2 (class recurred ≥2) NO — first occurrence of the prose-audit-ignores-series_index class in the hardening log (the related `_plan_sort_key` ISSUE-1 fix was a routing-order code fix, a different symptom); signals 3/4 NO. The fix is the structural closure (prerequisite order ≡ routing order), not a narrow phrase patch.

**Reconciliation:** handback → orchestrator: `execute-plan-strict-order-prereq-ignores-series-index-reschedule` — the Step-2.5 bug spec's scope is FULLY resolved by the shipped fix (`9ce3b8f1`), but this is an observed-friction dispatch with NO cycle marker present and a CONCURRENT non-harden lane holding a dirty `docs/provenance-index.json` (mid-cycle on `decision-2-6-uncovered-row-reroute-to-mcp-test`). Running `--archive-fixed`/`--link-provenance` inline would commit + collide on that dirty file, so per `docs/bugs/CLAUDE.md` OUT-OF-PIPELINE ("cannot rely on the orchestrator honoring the handback") the WHOLE reconciliation is handed back and `**Status:** Concluded` is left UNTOUCHED (no `unarchived-fixed` debt stranded, no receipt written). The orchestrator, at a between-cycle clean-tree moment, should: write the `FIXED.md` receipt (`kind: fixed`, `provenance: backfilled-unverified`, citing `9ce3b8f1`), flip SPEC `**Status:** Concluded → Fixed`, then `python3 user/scripts/bug-state.py --repo-root . --archive-fixed docs/bugs/execute-plan-strict-order-prereq-ignores-series-index-reschedule` and `python3 user/scripts/lazy-state.py --link-provenance --id execute-plan-strict-order-prereq-ignores-series-index-reschedule --commits 9ce3b8f1`. See the Return `reconcile:` field.

**Intervention record:** `docs/interventions/harden-2026-07-r110.md` — target signal `event:halt` (expected decrease): the false-block manifests as a spurious `BLOCKED.md`/blocked-halt cycle, so the fix should drive down prerequisite-false-block halts on rescheduled strict-order series. Signal independence: independent (halt events are emitted by the pipeline's normal cycle bracketing, not by this fix) though `halt` is a broad bucket — the rescheduled-series false-block subset is the true target, so a total-halt decrease is only weakly attributable (noted `mixed` in the record).

## Round 111 — 2026-07-19 — process-friction

**Item in flight:** decision-2-6-uncovered-row-reroute-to-mcp-test
**Divergence point:** the `--cycle-end` process-friction detector (`cycle_end_friction_check → detect_cycle_bracket_friction` signal (b) `unexpected-commits`) for the `decision-2-6` `execute-plan` cycle (dispatch class `skill-execute-plan`). The detector charged the cycle's per-`sub_skill` budget (7, phase-scaled) with 11 window commits and tripped `unexpected-commits` — but 8 of the 11 were SANCTIONED CONCURRENT same-run writers, not the cycle's own runaway.

**Root cause:** `missing-contract` — the concurrent-writer attribution (`_count_concurrent_writer_commits`, `user/scripts/lazy_core/markers.py:2148`) unions only (1) a DIFFERENT committer-email and (2) a concurrent-activity-ledger sha under a DIFFERENT run identity. The 8 concurrent commits were a background `/harden-harness` lane (Rounds 109/110), a wedge-backstop `--archive-fixed`, and reconcile/provenance ops — all DISPATCHED WITHIN THE SAME RUN, so they share this box's single git identity (`66210812+jacobrocks1212@...`, no work `includeIf`) AND the live run marker's `started_at`. Signal 1 misses them (same identity); signal 2 misses them (`rsa != current_run_started_at` is False for a same-run dispatch, and the Agent-driven `harden(...)` commits are not in the script-owned ledger at all). Both arms attribute 0 → `chargeable_commits == commits_since == 11 > 7`. **Dispositive runtime proof:** the friction detail carried NO `concurrent_writer_commits=..., chargeable=...` suffix, which `markers.py:2016` emits iff `chargeable != commits_since` — its absence proves the attribution returned 0/None. Serving-path trace (each hop `file:line`) in the Step-2.5 spec. Also dogfooded live: repo HEAD advanced `4f6b280f → 4f92bd47` from a concurrent same-run writer DURING this investigation. This is the THIRD recurrence of the concurrent-writer / `unexpected-commits` class (after `gate-scope-folds-concurrent-harden-commits` + `adhoc-process-friction-detector-counts-concurrent-session-commits`), on a NEW axis (same-run + same-identity) orthogonal to the two the predecessors closed (distinct-identity; distinct-run-identity-ledger).

**Action:**
  - NEEDS_INPUT.md written (hard-park carve-out — structural + gate-integrity; nothing implemented): `docs/specs/turn-routing-enforcement/NEEDS_INPUT_2026-07-19-process-friction-same-run-concurrent-dispatch-attribution.md`. Decision: `same-run concurrent-dispatch commit attribution` (`divergence: structural`). Four recommendation-first options — **A (RECOMMENDED): per-commit cycle-nonce attribution → a PURELY-ADDITIVE third arm** (tag each cycle's own commits by the cycle marker `nonce` via the C2 hook's existing `commit_tally` increment site or a `Cycle-Nonce:` trailer; attribute-concurrent any window sha whose nonce differs/absent — never reduces the cycle's OWN count, so NO false negative, non-gate-weakening; measures the cycle's own commits instead of the pollutable window proxy). B: cap `chargeable` by `commit_tally` — PARTIAL (polluted during the live window) AND removes the window count's unique hook-bypassed-runaway catch → coverage-reducing, rejected. C: message-slug attribution — heuristic/fragile, rejected. D: broaden the ledger to script-owned between-cycle sites only — partial (misses Agent-driven `harden(...)` commits), fold into A. Why HARD-PARK not park-provisional: every option either forks the detector's core INTEGRITY measurement with false-negative stakes (B), is a broad multi-site change (A/D), or is a fragile heuristic (C); the friction is NON-BLOCKING (observed-friction background harden — the run continues), so no interim degradation warrants a risky/partial provisional (mirrors Round 108). Widening the budget is explicitly rejected as gate-weakening (Prohibition #2). Bug spec (Step 2.5, committed FIRST under `harden(docs):`): `docs/bugs/process-friction-counts-same-run-concurrent-dispatch-commits/SPEC.md` (Status: Concluded — root cause proven, fix operator-parked).

**Over-fit spin-off:** none — no landed fix to generalize (hard-park). This IS the 3rd recurrence of the concurrent-writer/`unexpected-commits` class, but the NEEDS_INPUT deliberately frames the GENERAL problem (the whole same-run concurrent-writer ATTRIBUTION axis + the recommended structural measurement redesign), i.e. the park IS the structural generalization the over-fit reflex would demand — NOT a fourth narrow attribution arm (which is precisely the whack-a-mole the reflex warns against; prior rounds added arm-1 email and arm-2 ledger). A separate `/spec-bug` spin-off for the same class the park already owns would be redundant (same reasoning as Round 108).

**Reconciliation:** none — this round shipped no `docs/bugs/` FIX (pure hard-park). The round's own bug spec (`process-friction-counts-same-run-concurrent-dispatch-commits`) stays `Status: Concluded` with its fix explicitly operator-parked (the `Concluded`-with-fix-SHIPPED limbo the reconcile step guards does NOT apply — nothing shipped); the operator resolves it via the NEEDS_INPUT.

**Intervention record:** none — pure hard-park NEEDS_INPUT round; nothing shipped, so no intervention is recorded (Step 4: intervention records are for `Mechanical fix applied` / `Provisional design-fork resolved` rounds only). The measurable target signal for the eventual fix (`event:containment-refusal`-adjacent — the `unexpected-commits` process-friction `kind: process-friction` ledger-event false-fire count on execute-plan cycles running under concurrent same-run dispatch) will be declared when the operator-blessed Option-A fix ships.

**Gates run:**
  (docs-only hard-park — no script/skill/hook change; no mechanical-commit gate battery required, per the Round-108 precedent)

## Round 112 — 2026-07-19 — validate-deny

**Item in flight:** hydra-overlay
**Divergence point:** Step 7a (execute-plan cycle). At a fresh execute-plan cycle-begin (`nonce 29ef8b47cfaa…`, `cycle-begin` telemetry `1784488944.3`, `kind: real`, `sub_skill: execute-plan`) the orchestrator held a valid, freshly-registered cycle emission (`emitted_at 1784488920.2`, **`consumed: false`**) but instead of dispatching that SINGLE emitted `cycle_prompt` verbatim to ONE subagent, it hand-composed execute-plan's INTERNAL test-agent worker prompts at the orchestrator level (`prompt_head: "You are a TEST-WRITING agent for AlgoBooth … Write FAILING tests only …"`, `denied_sha12: bc608cd07fb0` + `cd064b69ad2b`). The dispatch guard (`lazy_guard.py` branch 2b, consumed-fence FALSE) correctly DENIED both, withheld the forward route (`route_overridden_by: pending-hardening-debt`, `pending_hardening=2`) and dispatched this hardening stage.

**Root cause:** `missing-contract` — the 2b workstation sub-subagent exemption (`dispatch-guard-denies-workstation-subsubagent-split`, Rounds 9/10) requires the active `subagent_model` cycle's OWN emission to be consumed (the consumed fence, `lazy_core.dispatch.emission_consumed_by_nonce`) before admitting a worker-composed sub-subagent prompt — precisely to close "the window where the orchestrator itself could improvise an unregistered dispatch under its freshly-armed cycle marker" (that function's own docstring). Here the fence held correctly (execute-plan's emission `29ef8b47…` was NEVER consumed — no worker was ever in flight; session tool calls are serial), so the two improvised prompts fell through to the GENERIC `_deny_default(marker, _default_deny_reason(), …)`. That generic corrective recipe does not NAME the specific, mechanically-detectable mistake (armed `subagent_model` cycle + own emission NOT consumed + unregistered `Agent` prompt ⇒ orchestrator composing the skill's internal split itself). This is the `missing-contract` SUCCESSOR to Rounds 9/10 (same guard region — they classified the ABSENCE of the exemption; this is its DENY fall-through). Prose contributor (secondary, NOT the fix site): `lazy-batch/SKILL.md` line 42 states "it still dispatches exactly one Agent per cycle" but buries it beside the enticing `e.g. /execute-plan → Sonnet test-agent + impl-agent split` example — the durable backstop is the mechanical self-announcing deny, so the fix lands in the guard, not the prose. Reconstruction cited from the live AlgoBooth state dir (`~/.claude/state/37850b6e…`: `lazy-deny-ledger.jsonl`, `lazy-prompt-registry.json` entry `29ef8b47…` `consumed:false`, `lazy-telemetry.jsonl` cycle-begin/cycle-end brackets).

**Action:**
  - Mechanical fix applied: added `_subagent_model_improvisation_deny_reason(cycle)` (`lazy_guard.py`) and a new 2b branch — when the active `subagent_model: true` cycle's own emission is NOT consumed, the deny self-announces the improvisation + the corrective ("the orchestrator dispatches EXACTLY ONE Agent per cycle: dispatch the SINGLE emitted cycle_prompt VERBATIM to ONE subagent — the `<sub_skill>` SUBAGENT performs its own test-agent/impl-agent (or Explore) split INTERNALLY"), prepended to the standard `_CORRECTIVE_RECIPE`. Deny VERDICT + hardening-debt semantics UNCHANGED (routed via the same `_deny_default`; a bound marker still accrues debt + routes hardening) — a message upgrade, NOT a gate change. New regression `test_guard_subagent_model_improvisation_deny_self_announces` (`test_hooks.py`, registered in `_TESTS`): asserts deny + self-announcing reason (`orchestrator-improvised` / `EXACTLY ONE Agent per cycle` / `cycle_prompt` / `execute-plan`) + diagnosis-prepends-recipe + `pending_hardening() == 1` (debt preserved); the sibling consumed-fence-true ALLOW path is untouched. Bug spec (Step 2.5, committed FIRST under `harden(docs):` `7eb5cbb7`): `docs/bugs/_archive/dispatch-guard-improvisation-deny-not-self-announcing/SPEC.md`.
